
-----title
眉山 (出生地)

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　九月壬辰（十七日），以镇江节度推官阮逸为镇安节度掌书记、知城父县。苏洵尝与阮逸有交往。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　苏洵回乡过鹿头坡，抵家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　苏洵长子景先卒。<br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　董储以都官员外郎知眉州。苏洵与游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　苏洵与史经臣（彦辅）游。<br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　在眉山。任伋（师中）官清江，苏洵作诗送行。作品：《送任师中任清江》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134154' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134154' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134154?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送任师中任清江</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134154")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134154_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134154'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134154'>吾喜送任师<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作尚喜事）</span>，羡君方少年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134154'>有如伏枥马，看彼始及鞍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134154'>奔腾过吾目，萧条正思边。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134154'>谁知脱吾羁，傲睨登太山。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134154'>君今始得县，翱翔大江干。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134154'>大江多风波，渺然势<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作天）</span>欲翻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134154'>浩荡吞九野，开阖壮士肝。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134154'>人生患不出，局束守一廛。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134154'>未常见大物，不识天地宽。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134154'>今君吾乡秀，固已见西川。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134154'>去年作边吏，出入烽火閒。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134154'>儒冠杂武弁，屈<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作屡）</span>与毡裘言。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134154'>又当适南土<span /></div><div class='label1' id='98dfabd4841d4111af23329803be165a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("98dfabd4841d4111af23329803be165a");'><span id='98dfabd4841d4111af23329803be165a_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年2月</a>　二月，苏涣、苏洵兄弟葬父序于眉山县修文乡安道里先茔之侧。后来，苏轼作行状，曾巩作墓志铭。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='3f1dc3e16f2c4c3ba290c38398d199e8_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　苏洵居丧及居丧后近十年，不出蜀，教二子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　苏洵尝命轼、辙兄弟学于刘巨（微之）；从巨学者，尚有家定国（退翁）、家安国（复礼）、家勤国（汉公）兄弟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　苏洵尝与二子轼、辙同读富弼（郑公）《使北语录》，因论之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　苏轼、苏辙读书南轩。洵名南轩为“来风”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　在眉山。苏洵题张仙画像，并书之。作品：《题张仙画像》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165006' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165006' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165006?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题张仙画像</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165006")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165006_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165006'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165006'>洵尝于天圣庚午重九日玉局观无碍子肆中见一画像，笔法清奇，云乃张仙也，有祷必应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165006_comment'></div>因解玉环易之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165006_comment'></div>洵尝无嗣，每旦露香以告，逮数年乃得轼，又得辙，性皆嗜书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165006_comment'></div>乃知真人急于接物，而无碍子之言不吾妄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165006_comment'></div>故识其本末，使异时欲祈嗣者，于此加敬云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1165006_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年8月</a>　秋八月，苏洵与兄涣免丧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《名二子说》，名轼及辙。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165075' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165075' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165075?labeling=true' target='_blank'>名二子说</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165075")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165075_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165075'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165075'>轮辐盖轸，皆有职乎车，而轼独若无所为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165075_comment'></div>虽然，去轼，则吾未见其为完车也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165075_comment'></div>轼乎，吾惧汝之不外饰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165075_comment'></div>天下之车莫不由辙，而言车之功者，辙不与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165075_comment'></div>虽然，车仆马毙，而患亦不及辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165075_comment'></div>是辙者，善处乎祸福之间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165075_comment'></div>辙乎，吾知免矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1165075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1165075'><span class='label'>按：</span>《苏老泉先生全集》卷一五。又见《崇古文诀》卷二二，《国朝二百家名贤文粹》卷一七三，《古今事文类聚》后集卷二，《古今合璧事类备要》续集卷二，《文章类选》卷九，《文章辨体汇选》卷四三○，《古文真宝》后集卷二，《名世文宗》卷二五，《戒子通录》卷五，《古今图书集成》家范典卷一六，人事典卷四一。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1165075_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《仲兄字文甫说》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165076' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165076' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165076?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仲兄字文甫说</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165076")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165076_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165076'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165076'>洵读《易》至《涣》之六四，曰：「涣其群，元吉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165076_comment'></div>曰：嗟夫，群者，圣人所欲涣以混一天下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165076_comment'></div>盖余仲兄名涣，而字公群，则是以圣人之所欲解散涤荡者以自命也，而可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165076_comment'></div>他日以告，兄曰：「子可无为我易之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165076_comment'></div>洵曰：「唯」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165076_comment'></div>既而曰：请以文甫易之，如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165076_comment'></div>且兄尝见夫水之与风乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165076_comment'></div>油然而行，渊然而留，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1165076", 1165076, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>渟洄</span>汪洋，满而上浮者，是水也，而风实起之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165076_comment'></div>蓬蓬然而发乎大空，不终日而行乎四方，荡乎其无形，飘乎其远来，既往而不知其迹之所存者，是风也，而水实形之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165076_comment'></div>今夫风水之相遭乎大泽之陂也，纡馀委蛇，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1165076", 1165076, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>蜿蜒</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1165076", 1165076, "Clauses/36/Comments/1")'>沦涟</span>，安而相推，怒而相凌，舒而如云，蹙而如鳞，疾而如驰，徐而如徊，揖让旋辟，相顾而不前，其繁如縠，其乱如雾，纷纭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1165076", 1165076, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>郁扰</span>，百里若一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165076_comment'></div>汩乎顺流，至乎沧海之滨，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1165076", 1165076, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>滂薄</span>汹涌，号怒相轧，交横绸缪，放乎空虚，掉乎无垠，横流逆折，濆旋倾侧，宛转胶戾，回者如轮，萦者如带，直者如燧，奔者如燄，跳者如鹭，跃者如鲤，殊状异态，而风水之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1165076", 1165076, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>极观</span>备矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165076_comment'></div>故曰：「风行水上涣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165076_comment'></div>此亦天下之至文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165076_comment'></div>然而此二物者，岂有求乎文哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165076_comment'></div>无意乎相求，不期而相遭，而文生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165076_comment'></div>是其为文也，非水之文也，非风之文也，二物者非能为文，而不能不为文也，物之相使而文出于其间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165076_comment'></div>故曰，此天下之至文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165076_comment'></div>今夫玉非不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1165076", 1165076, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>温然</span>美矣，而不得以为文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165076_comment'></div>刻镂组绣，非不文矣，而不可与论乎自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165076_comment'></div>故夫天下之无营而文生之者，惟水与风而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165076_comment'></div>昔者君子之处于世，不求有功，不得已而功成，则天下以为贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165076_comment'></div>不求有言，不得已而言出，则天下以为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1165076", 1165076, "Clauses/96/Comments/0")'>口实</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165076_comment'></div>呜呼，此不可与他人道之，惟吾兄可也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1165076_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　苏洵在乡与史经臣（彦辅）、任伋（师中）游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　苏洵自丁家艰，闭户益读书；焚旧文稿。文章于是精进。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　苏轼约于本岁前后作《却鼠刀铭》，父洵称之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　苏洵幼女适程之才。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　不详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年5月</a>　五月，苏洵幼女遭夫家（舅程濬、姑宋氏、夫之才）之虐死去。于是苏、程结怨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　十二月庚申（二十五日），太常博士吴中复（仲庶）为监察御史里行。赴阙。苏洵与中复有交往。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　胡允文（执中）从苏洵游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《权书》作品：《权书·权书叙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷二。）</span>《权书·心术》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷二。）</span>《权书·法制》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷二。）</span>《权书·强弱》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷二。）</span>《权书·攻守》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷二。）</span>《权书·用间》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷二。）</span>《权书·孙武》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷三。）</span>《权书·子贡》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷三。）</span>《权书·六国》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷三。）</span>《权书·项籍》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷三。）</span>《权书·高祖》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1165009' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165009' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165009?labeling=true' target='_blank'>权书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>权书叙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165009")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165009_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165009'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165009'>人有言曰：儒者不言兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165009_comment'></div>仁义之兵，无术而自胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165009_comment'></div>使仁义之兵无术而自胜也，则武王何用乎太公？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165009_comment'></div>而牧野之战，「四伐、五伐、六伐、七伐乃止齐焉」，又何用也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165009_comment'></div>《权书》，兵书也，而所以用仁济义之术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165009_comment'></div>吾疾夫世之人不究本末，而妄以我为孙武之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165009_comment'></div>夫孙氏之言兵为常言也，而我以此书为不得已而言之之书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165009_comment'></div>故仁义不得已，而后吾《权书》用焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165009_comment'></div>然则权者，为仁义之穷而作也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1165009_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165010' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165010' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165010?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>心术</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165010_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165010'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165010'>为将之道，当先治心，泰山崩于前而色不变，麋鹿兴于左而目不瞬，然后可以制利害，可以待敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165010_comment'></div>凡兵上义，不义，虽利勿动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165010_comment'></div>非一动之为害，而他日将有所不可措手足也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165010_comment'></div>夫惟义可以怒士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165010_comment'></div>士以义怒，可与百战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165010_comment'></div>凡战之道，未战养其财，将战养其力，既战养其气，既胜养其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165010_comment'></div>谨烽燧，严斥堠，使耕者无所顾忌，所以养其财；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165010_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1165010", 1165010, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>丰犒</span>而优游之，所以养其力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165010_comment'></div>小胜益急，小挫益厉，所以养其气；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165010_comment'></div>用人不尽其所欲为，所以养其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165010_comment'></div>故士常蓄其怒、怀其欲而不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165010_comment'></div>怒不尽则有馀勇，欲不尽则有馀贪，故虽并天下而士不厌兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165010_comment'></div>此黄帝之所以七十战而兵不殆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165010_comment'></div>不养其心，一战而胜，不可用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165010_comment'></div>凡将欲智而严，凡士欲愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165010_comment'></div>智则不可测，严则不可犯，故士皆委己而听命，夫安得不愚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165010_comment'></div>夫惟士愚，而后可与之皆死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165010_comment'></div>凡兵之动，知敌之主，知敌之将，而后可以动于险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165010_comment'></div>邓艾缒兵于穴中，非刘禅之庸，则百万之师可以坐缚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165010_comment'></div>彼固有所侮而动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165010_comment'></div>故古之贤将，能以兵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1165010", 1165010, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>尝敌</span>，而又以敌自尝，故去就可以决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165010_comment'></div>凡主将之道，知理而后可以举兵，知势而后可以加兵，知节而后可以用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165010_comment'></div>知理则不屈，知势则不沮，知节则不穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165010_comment'></div>见小利不动，见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1165010", 1165010, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>小患</span>不避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165010_comment'></div>小利<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1165010", 1165010, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>小患</span>不足以辱吾技也，夫然后可以支大利大患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165010_comment'></div>夫惟养技而自爱者，无敌于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165010_comment'></div>故一忍可以支百勇，一静可以制百动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165010_comment'></div>兵有长短，敌我一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165010_comment'></div>敢问吾之所长，吾出而用之，彼将不与吾校；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165010_comment'></div>吾之所短，吾蔽而置之，彼将强与吾角，奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165010_comment'></div>曰：吾之所短，吾抗而暴之，使之疑而却；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165010_comment'></div>吾之所长，吾阴而养之，使之狎而堕其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165010_comment'></div>此用长短之术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165010_comment'></div>善用兵者，使之无所顾，有所恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165010_comment'></div>无所顾，则知死之不足惜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165010_comment'></div>有所恃，则知不至于必败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165010_comment'></div>尺箠当猛虎，奋呼而操击；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165010_comment'></div>徒手遇蜥蜴，变色而却步，人之情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165010_comment'></div>知此者，可以将矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165010_comment'></div>袒裼而按剑，则乌获不敢逼，冠胄衣甲，据兵而寝，则童子弯弓杀之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165010_comment'></div>故善用兵者以形固，夫能以形固，则力有馀矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1165010_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1165010'><span class='label'>按：</span>《苏老泉先生全集》卷二。又见《皇朝文鉴》卷九七，《宋史》卷四四三《苏洵传》，《名世文宗》卷二四，《经济类编》卷五五，《古今图书集成》官常典卷五四三、戎政典卷九○。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1165010_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1165011' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165011' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165011?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>法制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165011_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165011'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165011'>将战必审知其将之贤愚：与贤将战，则持之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165011_comment'></div>与愚将战，则乘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165011_comment'></div>持之则容有所伺而为之谋，乘之则一举而夺其气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165011_comment'></div>虽然，非愚将勿乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165011_comment'></div>乘之不动，其祸在我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165011_comment'></div>分兵而迭进，所以持之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165011_comment'></div>并力而一战，所以乘之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165011_comment'></div>古之善军者，以刑使人，以赏使人，以怒使人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165011_comment'></div>而其中必有以义附者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165011_comment'></div>不以战，不以掠，而以备急难，故越有君子六千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165011_comment'></div>韩之战，秦之斗士倍于晋，而出穆公于淖者，赦食马者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165011_comment'></div>兵或寡而易危，或众而易叛，莫难于用众，莫危于用寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165011_comment'></div>治众者法欲繁，繁则士难以动；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165011_comment'></div>治寡者法欲简，简则士易以察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165011_comment'></div>不然，则士不任战矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165011_comment'></div>惟众而繁，虽劳不害为强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165011_comment'></div>以众入险阻，必分军而疏行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165011_comment'></div>夫险阻必有伏，伏必有约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165011_comment'></div>军分则伏不知所击，而其约携矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165011_comment'></div>险阻惧蹙，疏行以纾士气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165011_comment'></div>兵莫危于攻，莫难于守，客主之势然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165011_comment'></div>故城有二不可守：兵少不足以实城，城小不足以容兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165011_comment'></div>夫惟贤将能以寡为众，以小为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165011_comment'></div>当敌之冲，人莫不守，我以疑兵，彼愕不进，虽告之曰「此无人」，彼不信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165011_comment'></div>度彼所袭，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1165011", 1165011, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>潜兵</span>以备，彼不我测，谓我有馀，夫何患兵少？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165011_comment'></div>偃旗仆鼓，寂若无气，严戢兵士，敢哗者斩，时令老弱登埤示怯，乘懈突击，其众可走，夫何患城小？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165011_comment'></div>背城而战，陈欲方、欲踞、欲密、欲缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165011_comment'></div>夫方而踞，密而缓，则士心固，固则不慑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165011_comment'></div>背城而战，欲其不慑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165011_comment'></div>面城而战，阵欲直、欲锐、欲疏、欲速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165011_comment'></div>夫直而锐，疏而速，则士心危，危则致死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165011_comment'></div>面城而战，欲其致死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165011_comment'></div>夫能静而自观者，可以用人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165011_comment'></div>吾何为而怒，吾何为则喜，吾何为则勇，吾何为则怯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165011_comment'></div>夫人岂异于我？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165011_comment'></div>天下之人，孰不能自观其一身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165011_comment'></div>是以知此理者，涂之人皆可以将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165011_comment'></div>平居与人言，一语不循故，犹且𥈭而忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165011_comment'></div>敌以形形我，恬而不怪，亦已固矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165011_comment'></div>是故智者视敌有无故之形，必谨察之，勿动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165011_comment'></div>疑形二：可疑于心，则疑而为之谋，心固得其实也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1165011_comment'></div>可疑于目，勿疑，彼敌疑我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1165011_comment'></div>是故心疑以谋应，目疑以静应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1165011_comment'></div>彼诚欲有所为邪，不使吾得之目矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1165011_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165012' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165012' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165012?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>强弱</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165012_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165012'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165012'>知有所甚爱，知有所不足爱，可以用兵矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165012_comment'></div>故夫善将者，以其所不足爱者，养其所甚爱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165012_comment'></div>士之不能皆锐，马之不能皆良，器械之不能皆利，固也，处之而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165012_comment'></div>兵之有上、中、下也，是兵之有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1165012", 1165012, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>三权</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165012_comment'></div>孙膑有言曰：「以君下驷与彼上驷，取君上驷与彼中驷，取君中驷与彼下驷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165012_comment'></div>此兵说也，非马说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165012_comment'></div>下之不足以与其上也，吾既知之矣，吾既知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165012_comment'></div>中之不足以与吾上，下之不足以与吾中，吾不既再胜矣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165012_comment'></div>得之多于弃也，吾斯从之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165012_comment'></div>彼其上之不得其中、下之援也，乃能独完耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165012_comment'></div>故曰：「兵之有上、中、下也，是兵之有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1165012", 1165012, "Clauses/31/Comments/1")'>三权</span>也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165012_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1165012", 1165012, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>三权</span>也者，以一致三者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165012_comment'></div>管仲曰：「攻坚则瑕者坚，攻瑕则坚者瑕」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165012_comment'></div>呜呼，不从其瑕而攻之，天下皆强敌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165012_comment'></div>汉高帝之忧在项籍耳，虽然，亲以其兵而与之角者，盖无几也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165012_comment'></div>随何取九江，韩信取魏、取代、取赵、取齐，然后高帝起而取项籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165012_comment'></div>夫不汲汲于其忧之所在，而彷徨乎其不足恤之地，彼盖所以孤项氏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165012_comment'></div>秦之忧在六国，蜀最僻最小，最先取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165012_comment'></div>楚最强，最后取，非其忧在蜀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165012_comment'></div>诸葛孔明一出其兵，乃与魏氏角，其亡宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165012_comment'></div>取天下，取一国，取一阵，皆如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165012_comment'></div>范蠡曰：「凡阵之道，益左以为牡，设右以为牝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165012_comment'></div>春秋时楚伐隋，季梁曰：「楚人上左，君必左，无与王遇，且攻其右，右无良焉，必败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165012_comment'></div>偏败，众乃携」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165012_comment'></div>盖一阵之间，必有牝牡左右，要当以吾强攻其弱耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165012_comment'></div>唐太宗曰：「吾自兴兵，习观行阵形势，每战视敌强其左，吾亦强吾左；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165012_comment'></div>弱其右，吾亦弱吾右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165012_comment'></div>使弱常遇强，强常遇弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165012_comment'></div>敌犯吾弱，追奔不过数十百步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165012_comment'></div>吾击敌弱，常<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1165012", 1165012, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>突出</span>自背反攻之，以是必胜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165012_comment'></div>后之庸将，既不能处其强弱以败，而又曰：「吾兵有老弱杂其间，非举军精锐，以故不能胜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165012_comment'></div>不知老弱之兵，兵家固亦不可无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165012_comment'></div>无之，是无以耗敌之强兵，而全吾之锐锋，败可俟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165012_comment'></div>故智者轻弃吾弱，而使敌轻用其强，忘其小丧，而志于大得，夫固要其终而已矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1165012_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165013' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165013' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165013?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>攻守</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165013_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165013'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165013'>古之善攻者，不尽兵以攻坚城；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165013_comment'></div>善守者，不尽兵以守敌冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165013_comment'></div>夫尽兵以攻坚城，则钝兵费粮而缓于成功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165013_comment'></div>尽兵以守敌冲，则兵不分，而彼间行，袭我无备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165013_comment'></div>故攻敌所不守，守敌所不攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165013_comment'></div>攻者有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>三道</span>焉，守者有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>三道</span>焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165013_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>三道</span>：一曰正，二曰奇，三曰伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165013_comment'></div>坦坦之路，车毂击，人肩摩，出亦此，入亦此，我所必攻，彼所必守者，曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>正道</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165013_comment'></div>大兵攻其南，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>锐兵</span>出其北，大兵攻其东，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>锐兵</span>出其西者，曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>奇道</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165013_comment'></div>大山<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>峻谷</span>，中盘绝径，潜师其间，不鸣金，不挝鼓，突出乎平川，以冲敌人腹心者，曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>伏道</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165013_comment'></div>故兵出于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>正道</span>，胜败未可知也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165013_comment'></div>出于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>奇道</span>，十出而五胜矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165013_comment'></div>出于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>伏道</span>，十出而十胜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165013_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165013_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>正道</span>之城，坚城也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165013_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>正道</span>之兵，精兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165013_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>奇道</span>之城，不必坚也，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>奇道</span>之兵，不必精也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165013_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>伏道</span>则无城也，无兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165013_comment'></div>攻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>正道</span>而不知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/56/Comments/1")'>奇道</span>与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/56/Comments/2")'>伏道</span>焉者，其将木偶人是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165013_comment'></div>守<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>正道</span>而不知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/58/Comments/1")'>奇道</span>与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/58/Comments/2")'>伏道</span>焉者，其将亦木偶人是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165013_comment'></div>今夫盗之于人，抉门斩关而入者有焉，他户之不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>扃键</span>而入者有焉，乘坏垣、坎墙趾而入者有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165013_comment'></div>抉门斩关，而主人不知察，几希矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165013_comment'></div>他户之不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>扃键</span>，而主人不知察，太半矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165013_comment'></div>乘坏垣、坎墙趾而主人不知察，皆是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165013_comment'></div>为主人者，宜无曰门之固，而他户墙隙之不恤焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165013_comment'></div>夫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>正道</span>之兵，抉门之盗也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165013_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>奇道</span>之兵，他户之盗也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165013_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>伏道</span>之兵，乘垣之盗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165013_comment'></div>所谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>正道</span>者，若秦之函谷，吴之长江，蜀之剑阁是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165013_comment'></div>昔者六国尝攻函谷矣，而秦将败之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165013_comment'></div>曹操尝攻长江矣，而周瑜走之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165013_comment'></div>钟会尝攻剑阁矣，而姜维拒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165013_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165013_comment'></div>其为之守备者素也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165013_comment'></div>刘濞反，攻大梁，田禄伯请以五万人别循江淮，收淮南、长沙以与濞会武关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165013_comment'></div>岑彭攻公孙述，自江州溯都江，破侯丹兵，径拔武阳，绕出延岑军后，疾以精骑赴广都，距成都不数十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165013_comment'></div>李愬攻蔡，蔡悉精卒以抗李光颜而不备愬，愬自文成破张柴，疾驰二百里，夜半到蔡，黎明擒元济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165013_comment'></div>此用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/110/Comments/0")'>奇道</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165013_comment'></div>汉武攻南越，唐蒙请发夜郎兵，浮船牂牁江，道番禺城下，以出越人不意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165013_comment'></div>邓艾攻蜀，自阴平由景谷攀木缘磴，鱼贯而进，至江油而降马邈，至绵竹而斩诸葛瞻，遂降刘禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165013_comment'></div>田令孜守潼关，关之左有谷曰禁，而不知之备，林言、尚让入之，夹攻关而关兵溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1165013_comment'></div>此用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/127/Comments/0")'>伏道</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1165013_comment'></div>吾观古之善用兵者，一阵之间，尚犹有正兵、奇兵、伏兵三者以取胜，况守一国，攻一国，而社稷之安危系焉者，其可以不知此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1165013", 1165013, "Clauses/134/Comments/0")'>三道</span>而欲使之将耶？</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1165013_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165014' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165014' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165014?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>用间</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165014_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165014'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165014'>孙武既言五间，则又有曰：「商之兴也，伊摰在夏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165014_comment'></div>周之兴也，吕牙在商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165014_comment'></div>故明君贤将能以上智为间者，必成大功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165014_comment'></div>此兵之要，三军所恃而动也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165014_comment'></div>按《书》：伊尹适夏，丑夏归亳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165014_comment'></div>《史》：太公常事纣，去之归周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165014_comment'></div>所谓在夏在商诚矣，然以为间，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165014_comment'></div>汤、文王固使人间夏、商邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165014_comment'></div>伊、吕固与人为间邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165014_comment'></div>桀、纣固待间而后可伐邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165014_comment'></div>是虽甚庸，亦知不然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165014_comment'></div>然则吾意天下存亡寄于一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165014_comment'></div>伊尹之在夏也，汤必曰：「桀虽暴，一旦用伊尹，则民心复安，吾何病焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165014_comment'></div>及其归亳也，汤必曰：「桀得伊尹不能用，必亡矣，吾不可以安视民病」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165014_comment'></div>遂与天下共亡之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165014_comment'></div>吕牙之在商也，文王必曰：「纣虽虐，一旦用吕牙，则天禄必复，吾何忧焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165014_comment'></div>及其归周也，文王必曰：「纣得吕牙不能用，必亡矣，吾不可以久遏天命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165014_comment'></div>遂命武王与天下共亡之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165014_comment'></div>然则夏、商之存亡，待伊、吕用否而决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165014_comment'></div>今夫问将之贤者，必曰能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1165014", 1165014, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>逆知</span>敌国之胜败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165014_comment'></div>问其所以知之之道，必曰不爱千金，故能使人为之出万死以间敌国，或曰能因敌国之使而探其阴计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165014_comment'></div>呜呼，其亦劳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165014_comment'></div>伊、吕一归，而夏商之国为决亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165014_comment'></div>使汤、武无用间之名，与用间之劳，而得用间之实，此非上智，其谁能之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165014_comment'></div>夫兵虽诡道，而本于正者，终亦必胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165014_comment'></div>今五间之用，其归于诈，成则为利，败则为祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165014_comment'></div>且与人为诈，人亦将且诈我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165014_comment'></div>故能以间胜者，亦或以间败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165014_comment'></div>吾间不忠，反为敌用，一败也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165014_comment'></div>不得敌之实，而得敌之所伪示者以为信，二败也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165014_comment'></div>受吾财而不能得敌之阴计，惧而以伪告我，三败也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165014_comment'></div>夫用心于正，一振而群纲举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165014_comment'></div>用心于诈，百补而千穴败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165014_comment'></div>智于此，不足恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165014_comment'></div>故五间者，非明君贤将之所上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165014_comment'></div>明君贤将之所上者，上智之间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165014_comment'></div>是以淮阴、曲逆，义不事楚，而高祖擒籍之计定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165014_comment'></div>左车、周叔不用于赵、魏，而淮阴进兵之谋决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165014_comment'></div>呜呼，是亦间也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1165014_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165015?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>孙武</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165015_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165015'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165015'>求之而不穷者，天下奇才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165015_comment'></div>天下之士，与之言兵，而曰我不能者几人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165015_comment'></div>求之于言而不穷者几人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165015_comment'></div>言不穷矣，求之于用而不穷者几人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165015_comment'></div>呜呼，至于用而不穷者，吾未之见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165015_comment'></div>《孙武十三篇》，兵家举以为师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165015_comment'></div>然以吾评之，其言兵之雄乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165015_comment'></div>今其书论奇权<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1165015", 1165015, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>密机</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1165015", 1165015, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>出入神鬼</span>，自古以兵著书者罕所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165015_comment'></div>以是而揣其为人，必谓有应敌无穷之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165015_comment'></div>不知武用兵乃不能必克，与书所言远甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165015_comment'></div>吴王阖庐之入郢也，武为将军，及秦、楚交败其兵，越王入践其国，外祸内患，一旦迭发，吴王奔走，自救不暇，武殊无一谋以弭斯乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165015_comment'></div>若按武之书以责武之失，凡有三焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165015_comment'></div>《九地》曰：「威加于敌，则交不得合」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165015_comment'></div>而武使秦，得听包胥之言，出兵救楚，无忌吴之心，斯不威之甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165015_comment'></div>其失一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165015_comment'></div>《作战》曰：「久暴师则钝兵挫锐，屈力殚货，则诸侯乘其弊而起」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165015_comment'></div>且武以九年冬伐楚，至十年秋始还，可谓久暴矣，越人能无乘间入国乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165015_comment'></div>其失二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165015_comment'></div>又曰：「杀敌者，怒也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165015_comment'></div>今武纵子胥、伯嚭鞭平王尸，复一夫之私忿，以激怒敌，此司马戌、子西、子斯所以必死雠吴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165015_comment'></div>勾践不颓旧冢而吴服，田单谲燕掘墓而齐奋，知谋与武远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165015_comment'></div>武不达此，其失三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165015_comment'></div>然始吴能以入郢，乃因胥、嚭、唐、蔡之怒，及乘楚瓦之不仁，武之功盖亦鲜耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165015_comment'></div>夫以武自为书，尚不能自用，以取败北，况区区祖其故智馀论者而能将乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165015_comment'></div>且吴起与武，一体之人也，皆著书言兵，世称之曰孙、吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165015_comment'></div>然而吴起之言兵也，轻法制，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1165015", 1165015, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>草略</span>无所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1165015", 1165015, "Clauses/77/Comments/1")'>统纪</span>，不若武之书词约而意尽，天下之兵说皆归其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165015_comment'></div>然吴起始用于鲁，破齐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165015_comment'></div>及入魏，又能制秦兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165015_comment'></div>入楚，楚复霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165015_comment'></div>而武之所为反如是，书之不足信也固矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165015_comment'></div>今夫外御一隶，内治一妾，是贱丈夫亦能，夫岂必有人而教之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165015_comment'></div>及夫御三军之众，阖营而自固，或且有乱，然则是三军之众惑之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165015_comment'></div>故善将者，视三军之众与视一隶一妾无加焉，故其心常若有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165015_comment'></div>夫以一人之心，当三军之众，而其中恢恢然犹有馀地，此韩信之所以多多而益善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165015_comment'></div>故夫用兵，岂有异术哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165015_comment'></div>能勿视其众而已矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1165015_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165016' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165016' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165016?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span>子贡</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165016_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165016'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165016'>君子之道，智信难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165016_comment'></div>信者，所以正其智也，而智常至于不正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165016_comment'></div>智者，所以通其信也，而信常至于不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165016_comment'></div>是故君子慎之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165016_comment'></div>世之儒者曰：徒智可以成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165016_comment'></div>人见乎徒智之可以成也，则举而弃乎信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165016_comment'></div>吾则曰：徒智可以成也，而不可以继也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165016_comment'></div>子贡之以乱齐、灭吴、存鲁也，吾悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165016_comment'></div>彼子贡者，游说之士，茍以邀一时之功，而不以可继为事，故不见其祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165016_comment'></div>使夫王公大人而计出于此，则吾未见其不旋踵而败也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165016_comment'></div>吾闻之：王者之兵，计万世而动；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165016_comment'></div>霸者之兵，计子孙而举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165016_comment'></div>强国之兵，计终身而发；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165016_comment'></div>求可继也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165016_comment'></div>子贡之兵，是明日不可用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165016_comment'></div>故子贡之出也，吾以为鲁可存也，而齐可无乱，吴可无灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165016_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165016_comment'></div>田常之将篡也，惮高、国、鲍、晏，故使移兵伐鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165016_comment'></div>为赐计者，莫若抵高、国、鲍、晏吊之，彼必愕而问焉，则对曰：「田常遣子之兵伐鲁，吾窃哀子之将亡也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165016_comment'></div>彼必诘其故，则对曰：「齐之有田氏，犹人之养虎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165016_comment'></div>子之于齐，犹肘股之于身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165016_comment'></div>田氏之欲肉齐久矣，然未敢逞志者，惧肘股之捍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165016_comment'></div>今子出伐鲁，肘股去矣，田氏孰惧哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165016_comment'></div>吾见身将磔裂，而肘股随之，所以吊也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165016_comment'></div>彼必惧而咨计于我，因教之曰：「子悉甲趋鲁，压境而止，吾请为子潜约鲁侯以待田氏之变，帅其兵从子入讨之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165016_comment'></div>彼惧田氏之祸，其势不得不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165016_comment'></div>归以约鲁侯，鲁侯惧齐伐，其势亦不得不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165016_comment'></div>因使练兵蒐乘以俟齐衅，诛乱臣而定新主，齐必德鲁，数世之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165016_comment'></div>吾观仲尼以为齐人不与田常者半，故请哀公讨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165016_comment'></div>今诚以鲁之众，从高、国、鲍、晏之师，加齐之半，可以轘田常于都市，其势甚便，其成功甚大，惜乎赐之不出于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165016_comment'></div>齐哀王举兵诛吕氏，吕氏以灌婴为将拒之，至荥阳，婴使使谕齐及诸侯连和，以待吕氏变，共诛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165016_comment'></div>今田氏之势，何以异此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165016_comment'></div>有鲁以为齐，有高、国、鲍、晏以为灌婴，惜乎赐之不出于此也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1165016_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165017' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165017' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165017?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span>六国</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165017_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165017'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165017'>六国破灭，非兵不利，战不善，弊在赂秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165017_comment'></div>赂秦而力亏，破灭之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165017_comment'></div>或曰：六国互丧，率赂秦耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165017_comment'></div>曰：不赂者以赂者丧，盖失强援，不能独完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165017_comment'></div>故曰弊在赂秦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165017_comment'></div>秦以攻取之外，小则获邑，大则得城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165017_comment'></div>较秦之所得，与战胜而得者，其实<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1165017", 1165017, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>百倍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165017_comment'></div>诸侯之所亡，与战败而亡者，其实亦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1165017", 1165017, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>百倍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165017_comment'></div>则秦之所大欲，诸侯之所大患，固不在战矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165017_comment'></div>思厥先祖父暴霜露，斩荆棘，以有尺寸之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165017_comment'></div>子孙视之不甚惜，举以予人，如弃草芥，今日割五城，明日割十城，然后得一夕安寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165017_comment'></div>起视四境，而秦兵又至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165017_comment'></div>然则诸侯之地有限，暴秦之欲无厌，奉之弥繁，侵之愈急，故不战而强弱胜负已判矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165017_comment'></div>至于颠覆，理固宜然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165017_comment'></div>古人云：「以地事秦，犹抱薪救火，薪不尽，火不灭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165017_comment'></div>此言得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165017_comment'></div>齐人未尝赂秦，终继五国<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1165017", 1165017, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>迁灭</span>，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165017_comment'></div>与嬴而不助五国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165017_comment'></div>五国既丧，齐亦不免矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165017_comment'></div>燕赵之君，始有远略，能守其土，义不赂秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165017_comment'></div>是故燕虽小国而后亡，斯用兵之效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165017_comment'></div>至丹以荆卿为计，始速祸焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165017_comment'></div>赵尝五战于秦，二败而三胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165017_comment'></div>后秦击赵者再，李牧连却之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165017_comment'></div>洎牧以谗诛，邯郸为郡，惜其用武而不终也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165017_comment'></div>且燕、赵处秦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1165017", 1165017, "Clauses/71/Comments/1")'>革灭</span>殆尽之际，可谓智力孤危，战败而亡，诚不得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165017_comment'></div>向使三国各爱其地，齐人勿附于秦，刺客不行，良将犹在，则胜负之数，存亡之理，当与秦相较，或未易量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165017_comment'></div>呜呼，以赂秦之地封天下之谋臣，以事秦之心礼天下之奇才，并力西向，则吾恐秦人食之不得下咽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165017_comment'></div>悲夫，有如此之势，而为秦人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1165017", 1165017, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>积威</span>之所劫，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1165017", 1165017, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>日削月割</span>，以趋于亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165017_comment'></div>为国者无使为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1165017", 1165017, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>积威</span>之所劫哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165017_comment'></div>夫六国与秦皆诸侯，其势弱于秦，而犹有可以不赂而胜之之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165017_comment'></div>茍以天下之大，下而从六国破亡之故事，是又在六国下矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1165017_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165018' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165018' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165018?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span>项籍</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165018_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165018'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165018'>吾尝论项籍有取天下之才，而无取天下之虑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165018_comment'></div>曹操有取天下之虑，而无取天下之量；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165018_comment'></div>刘备有取天下之量，而无取天下之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165018_comment'></div>故三人者，终其身无成焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165018_comment'></div>且夫不有所弃，不可以得天下之势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165018_comment'></div>不有所忍，不可以尽天下之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165018_comment'></div>是故地有所不取，城有所不攻，胜有所不就，败有所不避，其来不喜，其去不怒，肆天下之所为而徐制其后，乃克有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165018_comment'></div>呜呼，项籍有百战百胜之才，而死于垓下，无惑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165018_comment'></div>吾观其战于钜鹿也，见其虑之不长，量之不大，未尝不怪其死于垓下之晚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165018_comment'></div>方籍之渡河，沛公始整兵向关，籍于此时若急引军趋秦，及其锋而用之，可以据咸阳，制天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165018_comment'></div>不知出此，而区区与秦将争一旦之命，既全钜鹿，而犹徘徊河南、新安间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165018_comment'></div>至函谷，则沛公入咸阳数月矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165018_comment'></div>夫秦人既已安沛公而雠籍，则其势不得强而臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165018_comment'></div>故籍虽迁沛公汉中，而卒都彭城，使沛公得还定三秦，则天下之势在汉不在楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165018_comment'></div>楚虽百战百胜，尚何益哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165018_comment'></div>故曰：兆垓下之死者，钜鹿之战也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165018_comment'></div>或曰：虽然，籍必能入秦乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165018_comment'></div>曰：项梁死，章邯谓楚不足虑，故移兵伐赵，有轻楚心，而良将劲兵尽于钜鹿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165018_comment'></div>籍诚能以必死之士，击其轻敌寡弱之师，入之易耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165018_comment'></div>且亡秦之守关，与沛公之守，善否可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165018_comment'></div>沛公之攻关，与籍之攻，善否又可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165018_comment'></div>以秦之守而沛公攻入之，沛公之守而籍攻入之，然则亡秦之守，籍不能入哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165018_comment'></div>或曰：秦可入矣，如救赵何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165018_comment'></div>曰：虎方捕鹿，罴据其穴，搏其子，虎安得不置鹿而返？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165018_comment'></div>返则碎于罴明矣，军志所谓攻其必救也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165018_comment'></div>使籍入关，王离、涉间必释赵自救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165018_comment'></div>籍据关逆击其前，赵与诸侯救者十馀壁蹑其后，覆之必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165018_comment'></div>是籍一举解赵之围，而收功于秦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165018_comment'></div>战国时魏伐赵，齐救之，田忌引兵疾走大梁，因存赵而破魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165018_comment'></div>彼宋义号知兵，殊不达此，屯安阳不进，而曰待秦敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165018_comment'></div>吾恐秦未敝，而沛公先据关矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165018_comment'></div>籍与义俱失焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165018_comment'></div>是故古之取天下者，常先图所守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165018_comment'></div>诸葛孔明弃荆州而就西蜀，吾知其无能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165018_comment'></div>且彼未尝见大险也，彼以为剑门者可以不亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165018_comment'></div>吾尝观蜀之险，其守不可出，其出不可继，兢兢而自完，犹且不给，而何足以制中原哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165018_comment'></div>若夫秦汉之故都，沃土千里，洪河大山，真可以控天下，又乌事夫不可以措足如剑门者而后曰险哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165018_comment'></div>今夫富人必居四通五达之都，使其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1165018", 1165018, "Clauses/119/Comments/0")'>财布</span>出于天下，然后可以收天下之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165018_comment'></div>有小丈夫者，得一金，椟而藏诸家，拒户而守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165018_comment'></div>呜呼，是求不失也，非求富也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165018_comment'></div>大盗至，劫而取之，又焉知其果不失也？</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1165018_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165019' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165019' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165019?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span>高祖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165019_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165019'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165019'>汉高祖挟数用术，以制一时之利害，不如陈平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165019_comment'></div>揣摩天下之势，举指摇目以劫制项羽，不如张良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165019_comment'></div>微此二人，则天下不归汉，而高帝乃木彊之人而止耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165019_comment'></div>然天下已定，后世子孙之计，陈平、张良智之所不及，则高帝常先为之规画处置，以中后世之所为，晓然如目见其事而为之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165019_comment'></div>盖高帝之智，明于大而暗于小，至于此而后见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165019_comment'></div>帝尝语吕后曰：「周勃厚重少文，然安刘氏必勃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165019_comment'></div>可令为太尉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165019_comment'></div>方是时，刘氏既安矣，勃又将谁安邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165019_comment'></div>故吾之意曰：高帝之以太尉属勃也，知有吕氏之祸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165019_comment'></div>虽然，其不去吕后，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165019_comment'></div>势不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165019_comment'></div>昔者武王没，成王幼，而三监叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165019_comment'></div>帝意百岁后将相大臣及诸侯王有武庚禄父者，而无有以制之也，独计以为家有主母，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1165019", 1165019, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>豪奴</span>悍婢不敢与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1165019", 1165019, "Clauses/38/Comments/1")'>弱子</span>抗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165019_comment'></div>吕后佐帝定天下，为大臣素所畏服，独此可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1165019", 1165019, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>镇压</span>其邪心，以待嗣子之壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165019_comment'></div>故不去吕后者，为惠帝计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165019_comment'></div>吕后既不可去，故削其党以损其权，使虽有变而天下不摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165019_comment'></div>是故以樊哙之功，一旦遂欲斩之而无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165019_comment'></div>呜呼，彼岂独于哙不仁耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165019_comment'></div>且哙与帝偕起，拔城陷阵，功不为少矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165019_comment'></div>方亚父嗾项庄时，微哙诮让羽，则汉之为汉，未可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165019_comment'></div>一旦人有恶哙欲灭戚氏者，时哙出伐燕，立命平、勃即斩之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165019_comment'></div>夫哙之罪未形也，恶之者诚伪未必也，且高帝之不以一女子斩天下之功臣，亦明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165019_comment'></div>彼其娶于吕氏，吕氏之族若产、禄辈，皆庸才不足恤，独哙豪健，诸将所不能制，后世之患，无大于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165019_comment'></div>夫高帝之视吕后也，犹医者之视堇也，使其毒可以治病，而无至于杀人而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165019_comment'></div>樊哙死，则吕氏之毒将不至于杀人，高帝以为是足以死而无忧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165019_comment'></div>彼平、勃者，遗其忧者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165019_comment'></div>哙之死于惠之六年也，天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165019_comment'></div>使其尚在，则吕禄不可绐，太尉不得入北军矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165019_comment'></div>或谓哙于帝最亲，使之尚在，未必与产、禄叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165019_comment'></div>夫韩信、黥布、卢绾皆南面称孤，而绾又最为亲幸，然及高祖之未崩也，皆相继以逆诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165019_comment'></div>谁谓百岁之后，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1165019", 1165019, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>椎埋屠狗</span>之人，见其亲戚乘势为帝王而不欣然从之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165019_comment'></div>吾故曰彼平、勃者遗其忧者也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1165019_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　在眉山。苏洵上成都府通判吴照邻书，陈蜀中三患并清患之法，并上《兵论》（即《权书》）三篇。作品：《上府倅吴职方书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《成都文类》（宋程遇孙编，影印《四库全书》文渊阁本）卷二十一；此文收入曾枣庄、刘琳主编《全宋文》（上海辞书出版社、安徽教育出版社2006年版第43册第48页））</span><div id='poem_1164998' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164998' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164998?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上府倅吴职方书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164998")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164998_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164998'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164998'>洵窃谓蜀之土，墙万山，堑大江，膏田百同，蟠乎其中，故天下之地，险固沃美无如蜀者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164998_comment'></div>即蜀而言，益，诸郡之纲领；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164998_comment'></div>嘉，诸蛮之孔道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164998_comment'></div>故蜀之地大且要，无如益与嘉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164998_comment'></div>执事始受诏天子相益，尝受命大司权领嘉事，未几归益，今又以事如嘉而还矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164998_comment'></div>是益徯执事以治，而嘉徯执事以安，一身而二任焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164998_comment'></div>故蜀之吏自府漕刑外，职大责重无如执事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164998_comment'></div>职大责重，古君子居之，未尝不竭己之才，而又得择群言舆谋以辅其志，广其聪，远其明，而能成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164998_comment'></div>故蜀之吏宜不以贵故忽卑贱之言，亦无如执事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164998_comment'></div>洵通义穷百姓，读经史、学计策外无他长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164998_comment'></div>执事爱弟里行君气质刚正，非妄许可者，不知洵不肖，读其文而怜其穷，故尝幸过之，而又尝使人以书而候问其死生，若故旧然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164998_comment'></div>洵常德之，思有以报，而未获其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164998_comment'></div>执事之始如嘉也，前郡尉张君谓洵曰：「吴公经是，语及子，且知子矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164998_comment'></div>夫其弟待之如故旧，其兄未识而语及之，且知之焉，然则如洵者宜如何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164998_comment'></div>不效其所有于执事以补万一，而以浅陋为解，则非执事待洵意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164998_comment'></div>况执事职大任重，必不以贵故忽其言耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164998_comment'></div>今洵之所有，而执事之所当闻者，蜀之利害也，请为执事言其略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164998_comment'></div>夫蜀有三患，其二将形，其一既萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164998_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164998_comment'></div>人性骄侈，耀宝贿，盛纨锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164998_comment'></div>赀蓄未能百金，而衒诸外已若古程、卓辈，故使穷民恶盗得以萌窥劫心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164998_comment'></div>李顺之乱实根于此，今又何知草莽间无李顺耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164998_comment'></div>此将形之一患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164998_comment'></div>疲兵怯弱，或有变故，常恃客军，故客军常曰：「有他盗能御我者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164998_comment'></div>少不若意，则瞠视大叫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164998_comment'></div>疲兵畏避不暇，何敢议斗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164998_comment'></div>王均、刘旰之乱，实根于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164998_comment'></div>今又何知军伍中无王均、刘旰耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164998_comment'></div>此将形之患二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164998_comment'></div>去岁邕管逋寇，南诏为之囊橐，倡言于其国曰：「砥尔戈，秣尔马，吾将逞志于蜀」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164998_comment'></div>今郡县欲广其备具，多其戍役，则民不堪，否则惧其乘我虚隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164998_comment'></div>此既萌之患一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164998_comment'></div>夫一方而三患具，安危缓急宜曰何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164998_comment'></div>而昧者犹谓今之患独在南诏，而又曰残虏非吾敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164998_comment'></div>不知是三患幸而不发则已，不幸而有一起，二者必从而兴，其势如大鼎弱足之折，馀必随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164998_comment'></div>茍有位者不皇皇汲汲蚤夜思其谋，则亦见坐漏船之中，而不知茹焉𨟉𨟉焉者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164998_comment'></div>然则何为而可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164998_comment'></div>曰西南民性与东北尤异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164998_comment'></div>怯不能守，嗜利而好荡，是以易乱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164998_comment'></div>勇不能固，慑刑而重迁，是以易制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164998_comment'></div>今其骄侈之风，虽欲化以俭德，固未可岁月待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164998_comment'></div>得强明吏擿其奸，发其非，诛之徙之，则盗可以消矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164998_comment'></div>疲兵虽号怯弱，然武王以之而克商，诸葛孔明以之服西南蛮，抑魏氏兵不敢出战，杨仪乘其馀尚能走孟达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164998_comment'></div>今之人亦古之人耳，何强弱之远乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164998_comment'></div>盖不训练之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164998_comment'></div>窃见疲兵惟忠勇、宁远二军粗识教令，他不过负担而役，捆履而食，奈何责其斗耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164998_comment'></div>今欲为之计，莫若择客军之精锐者为之师而教之，明其号令，一其勇怯，信其赏罚，不旬月可与之赴汤火、蹈白刃，则客军知所顾忌，不敢动矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164998_comment'></div>犍为之西南，汉源之东南，庐山之西北，沿边杂虏，自汉以降，肆逆效勇，犹可历数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164998_comment'></div>然则非有雄谋大志，惟暴之则逆，惠之则顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164998_comment'></div>譬之狗然，临之以箠，鲜不吠噬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164998_comment'></div>豢之以食，可使捍盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164998_comment'></div>西汉以钩町兵破姑缯、叶榆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164998_comment'></div>后公孙述窃据，大姓龙、傅、董、尹氏为汉保境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1164998_comment'></div>由是观之，其人盖有时而忠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1164998_comment'></div>况今数百年来，慑服帖息，茍重之以惠，则彼独忠于古哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1164998_comment'></div>所宜密委边守常加宽恤，其人之商于吾境者，严讥而薄征之，疾则医之，死则殡之，使其至如归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1164998_comment'></div>彼将益乐吾德而求为我用矣，则向所谓邕管逋寇之在南诏者，又安能数千里越求为我用之虏而犯我哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1164998_comment'></div>纵使尽力能攻而越之，则其锐兵坚甲固已缺顿于沿边杂虏，而我坐收其弊，擒之易耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1164998_comment'></div>今郡县大修攻守战斗之具，而愚民汹汹惊顾间，有瘗金而囊糗以待窜匿者，故洵敢以此说为献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1164998_comment'></div>执事幸置之胸中，异日府公漕刑必将咨计执事，执事择其说之可者发之，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1164998_comment'></div>吁，执事权略智调，视措置岷蜀，其犹指挥仆妾辈耳，何待洵言耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1164998_comment'></div>虽然，居山者知虎豹之迹，居泽者识蛟蜃之穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1164998_comment'></div>洵诚惧执事不若洵家于此，闻见习熟，而得之之详也，以是不敢缄默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1164998_comment'></div>平生所学《春秋》、《洪范》、礼乐律历，皆著之书，非遇执事閒燕讲道时，未敢以贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1164998_comment'></div>《兵论》三篇，冀执事观之，而知洵与夫迂儒腐生盖少异矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1164998_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年11月</a>　十一月，张方平到知成都府任。曾访知苏洵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年12月</a>　十二月甲寅（二十五日），益州布衣张詧为本州助教，詧辞不拜。詧深于扬雄《太玄经》。苏洵亦深于《太玄经》，当有詧之影响。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　在眉山。吴照邻赴阙，苏洵作引送之。照邻携洵文，欧阳修（文忠）见而知之。作品：《送吴侯职方赴阙引》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165004?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送吴侯职方赴阙引</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165004")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165004_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165004'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165004'>因天地万物有可以如此之势，而寓之于事，则其始不强而易成，其成也穷万物而不可变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165004_comment'></div>圣人见天地之间以物加物，而不能皆长，不能皆短，于是有度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165004_comment'></div>见一人之手不能盛江河之沙砾，而泰山之谷纳一石而不加浅，于是有量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165004_comment'></div>见物横于空中，首重而末举，于是有权衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165004_comment'></div>长短之相形，大小之相盛，轻重之相抑昂，皆物之所自有，而度量权衡者因焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165004_comment'></div>故度量权衡，家有之而不可阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165004_comment'></div>至于后世，有作者出，以为因物之自然以成物，不足以见吾智，于是作器，使之不击而自鸣，不触而自转，虚而欹，水实其中，〔满〕而覆，半而端，如常器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165004_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165004_comment'></div>殆矣，吾见其朝作而暮废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165004_comment'></div>夫不忍而谓之仁，忍而谓之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165004_comment'></div>见蹈水者不忍而拯其手，而仁存焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165004_comment'></div>见井中之人，度不能出，忍而不从，而义存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165004_comment'></div>无伤其身而活一人，人心有之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165004_comment'></div>不肯杀其身以济必不能生之人，人心有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165004_comment'></div>有人焉，以为人心之所自有，而不足以惊人也，乃曰：「杀吾身虽不能生人，吾为之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165004_comment'></div>此人心之所自有邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165004_comment'></div>强之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165004_comment'></div>强不能以及远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165004_comment'></div>使人之心不忍杀人，而亦不以无故杀其身，是亦足以为仁矣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165004_comment'></div>呜呼，有馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165004_comment'></div>谁能不忍视人之死，而亦不肯妄杀其身者，然则异世惊众之行，亦无有以加之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165004_comment'></div>吴侯职方有名于当时，其胸中泊然无崖岸限隔，又无翘然跃然务出奇怪之操，以震撼世俗之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165004_comment'></div>是诚使刻厉险薄之人，见之将不识其所以与常人异者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165004_comment'></div>然使之退而思其平生大方，则淳淳浑浑不可遽测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165004_comment'></div>此所谓能充其心之所自有，而天下之君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165004_comment'></div>吴侯有名于世三十年，而犹于此为远官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165004_comment'></div>今其东归，其不碌碌为此官也哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1165004_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　苏洵尝诵欧阳修谢表文，命轼拟作。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　苏轼娶王弗为妻。先是轼少时本欲居山林学道，不愿婚宦，然为以苏洵为代表之家族势力所强，不得不改变初衷，而家族亦略予轼择偶以宽容。至是与王弗成婚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　苏洵长姊约卒于今年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年1月</a>　正月朔旦，蜀人相庆如他日。十五日元宵观灯，城门皆通夕不闭。盖自张方平镇蜀后，局势迅速平静、稳定。苏洵纪其事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　在眉山。苏洵与雷简夫（太简）纳拜，作书。作品：《与雷太简纳拜书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注·佚文》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年9月</a>　九月，在眉山。苏洵成《族谱后录上篇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十四。）</span><div id='poem_1165087' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165087' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165087?labeling=true' target='_blank'>族谱后录上篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165087")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165087_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165087'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165087'>苏氏之先出于高阳，高阳之子曰称，称之子曰老童，老童生重黎及吴回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165087_comment'></div>重黎为帝喾火正，曰祝融，以罪诛，其后为司马氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165087_comment'></div>而其弟吴回复为火正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165087_comment'></div>吴回生陆终，陆终生子六人：长曰樊，为昆吾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165087_comment'></div>次曰惠连，为参胡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165087_comment'></div>次曰篯，为彭祖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165087_comment'></div>次曰求言，为会人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165087_comment'></div>次曰安，为曹姓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165087_comment'></div>季曰季连，为芈姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165087_comment'></div>六人者皆有后，其后各分为数姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165087_comment'></div>昆吾始姓己氏，其后为苏、顾、温、董。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165087_comment'></div>当夏之时，昆吾为诸侯伯，历商而昆吾之后无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165087_comment'></div>至周有忿生，为司寇，能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1165087", 1165087, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>平刑</span>以教百姓，周公称之，盖《书》所谓司寇苏公者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165087_comment'></div>司寇苏公与檀伯达皆封于河，世世仕周，家于其封，故河南、河内皆有苏氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165087_comment'></div>六国之际，秦及代、厉，其苗裔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165087_comment'></div>至汉兴，而苏氏始徙入秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165087_comment'></div>或曰：高祖徙天下豪杰以实关中，而苏氏迁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165087_comment'></div>其后曰建，家于长安杜陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165087_comment'></div>武帝时为将，以击匈奴有功，封平陵侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165087_comment'></div>其后世遂家于其封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165087_comment'></div>建生三子：长曰嘉，次曰武，次曰贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165087_comment'></div>嘉为奉车都尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165087_comment'></div>其六世孙纯，为南阳太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165087_comment'></div>生子曰章，当顺帝时为冀州刺史，又迁为并州，有功于其人，其子孙遂家于赵郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165087_comment'></div>其后至唐武后之世，有味道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165087_comment'></div>味道，圣历初为凤阁侍郎，以贬为眉州刺史，迁为益州长史，未行而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165087_comment'></div>有子一人不能归，遂家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165087_comment'></div>自是眉始有苏氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165087_comment'></div>故眉之苏，皆宗益州长史味道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165087_comment'></div>赵郡之苏，皆宗并州刺史章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165087_comment'></div>扶风之苏，皆宗平陵侯建；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165087_comment'></div>河南、河内之苏，皆宗司寇忿生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165087_comment'></div>而凡苏氏皆宗昆吾樊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165087_comment'></div>昆吾樊宗祝融、吴回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165087_comment'></div>盖自昆吾樊至司寇忿生，自司寇忿生至平陵侯建，自平陵侯建至并州刺史章，自并州刺史章至益州长史味道，自益州长史味道至吾之高祖，其间世次皆不可纪，而洵始为《族谱》以纪其族属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165087_comment'></div>《谱》之所记，上至于吾之高祖，下至于吾之昆弟，昆弟死而及昆弟之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165087_comment'></div>曰：呜呼，高祖之上不可详矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165087_comment'></div>自吾之前，而吾莫之知焉，已矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165087_comment'></div>自吾之后，而莫之知焉，则从吾《谱》而益广之，可以至于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165087_comment'></div>盖高祖之子孙，家授一《谱》而藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165087_comment'></div>其法曰：凡嫡子而后得为谱，为谱者皆存其高祖，而迁其高祖之父，世世存其先人之谱，无废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1165087_comment'></div>而其不及高祖者，自其得为谱者之父始，而存其所宗之谱，皆以吾《谱》冠焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1165087_comment'></div>其说曰：此古之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1165087", 1165087, "Clauses/119/Comments/0")'>小宗</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1165087_comment'></div>古者有大宗，有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1165087", 1165087, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>小宗</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1165087_comment'></div>传曰：「别子为祖，继别为宗，继祢者为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1165087", 1165087, "Clauses/125/Comments/0")'>小宗</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1165087_comment'></div>有百世不迁之宗，有五世则迁之宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1165087_comment'></div>百世不迁者，别子之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1165087_comment'></div>宗其继别子之所自出者，百世不迁者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1165087_comment'></div>宗其继高祖者，五世则迁者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1165087_comment'></div>别子者，公子及士之始为大夫者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1165087_comment'></div>别子不得祢其父，而自使其嫡子后之，则为大宗，故曰：「继别为宗」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1165087_comment'></div>族人宗之，虽百世，而大宗死，则为之齐衰三月，其母妻亡亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1165087_comment'></div>死而无子，则支子以其昭穆后之，此所谓百世不迁之宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1165087_comment'></div>别子之庶子又不得祢别子，而自使其嫡子为后，则为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1165087", 1165087, "Clauses/151/Comments/0")'>小宗</span>，故曰：「继祢者为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1165087", 1165087, "Clauses/153/Comments/2")'>小宗</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1165087_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1165087", 1165087, "Clauses/154/Comments/0")'>小宗</span>五世之外，则易宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1165087_comment'></div>其继祢者，亲兄弟宗之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1165087_comment'></div>其继祖者，从兄弟宗之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1165087_comment'></div>其继曾祖者，再从兄弟宗之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1165087_comment'></div>其继高祖者，三从兄弟宗之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1165087_comment'></div>死而无子，则支子亦以其昭穆后之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1165087_comment'></div>此所谓五世则迁之宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1165087_comment'></div>凡今天下之人，惟天子之子与始为大夫者，而后可以为大宗，其馀则否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1165087_comment'></div>独<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1165087", 1165087, "Clauses/171/Comments/0")'>小宗</span>之法，犹可施于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1165087_comment'></div>故为族谱，其法皆从<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1165087", 1165087, "Clauses/174/Comments/0")'>小宗</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1165087_comment'></div>凡吾之宗，其继高祖者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1165087_comment'></div>高祖之嫡子祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1165087_comment'></div>祈死无子，天下之宗法不立，族人莫克以其子为之后，是以继高祖之宗亡而虚存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1165087_comment'></div>其继曾祖者，曾祖之嫡子宗善，宗善之嫡子昭图，昭图之嫡子惟益，惟益之嫡子允元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1165087_comment'></div>其继祖者，祖之嫡子讳序，序之嫡子澹，澹之嫡子位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1165087_comment'></div>其继祢者，祢之嫡子澹，澹之嫡子位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1165087_comment'></div>曰：呜呼，始可以详之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1165087_comment'></div>百世之后，凡吾高祖之子孙，得其家之《谱》而观之，则为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1165087", 1165087, "Clauses/200/Comments/0")'>小宗</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1165087_comment'></div>得吾高祖之子孙之《谱》而合之，而以吾《谱》考焉，则至于无穷而不可乱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1165087_comment'></div>是为谱之志云尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_73_1165087_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年9月</a>　九月，在眉山。苏洵成《族谱后录下篇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十四。）</span><div id='poem_1165088' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165088' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165088?labeling=true' target='_blank'>族谱后录下篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165088")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165088_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165088'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165088'>苏氏之先自昆吾以来，其最显者司寇忿生，三代之事，其闻于今不详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165088_comment'></div>周公作《立政》而特称之，以教太史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165088_comment'></div>其后周室衰，司寇之子孙亦曰苏公，遭谗作诗以刺暴公，名曰《彼何人斯》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165088_comment'></div>惟此二人，见于《诗》、《书》，是以其传至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165088_comment'></div>自苏氏入秦，而平陵侯建，典属国武始显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165088_comment'></div>迁于赵，而并州刺史章、益州长史味道始有闻于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165088_comment'></div>迁于眉，而至于今无闻，夫是惟谱不立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165088_comment'></div>自昆吾至《书》之苏公，五百有馀年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165088_comment'></div>自《书》之苏公至《诗》之苏公，二百有馀年，自《诗》之苏公至平陵侯建、典属国武，七百有馀年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165088_comment'></div>自平陵侯建、典属国武，至并州刺史章，二百有馀年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165088_comment'></div>自并州刺史章，至益州长史味道，五百有馀年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165088_comment'></div>自益州长史味道，至吾之高祖，二百有馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165088_comment'></div>以三十年而一易世，则七十有馀世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165088_comment'></div>七十有馀世，亦容有贤不贤焉，不贤者随世磨灭，不可得而闻，而贤者独有七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165088_comment'></div>七十有馀世，其贤者亦容不止于七人矣，而其馀不传，则谱不立之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165088_comment'></div>故洵既为《族谱》，又从而记其所闻先人之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165088_comment'></div>昔吾先子尝有言曰：「吾年少而亡吾先人，先世之行，吾不及有闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165088_comment'></div>盖尝闻其略曰：苏氏自迁于眉而家于眉山，自高祖泾则已不详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165088_comment'></div>自曾祖釿而后稍可记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165088_comment'></div>曾祖娶黄氏，以侠气闻于乡闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165088_comment'></div>生子五人，而吾祖祜最少最贤，以才干精敏见称，生于唐哀帝之天祐二年，而殁于周世宗之显德五年，盖与五代相终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165088_comment'></div>殁之一年，而吾太祖始受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165088_comment'></div>是时王氏、孟氏相继据蜀，蜀之高才大人皆不肯出仕，曰不足辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165088_comment'></div>仕于蜀者皆其年少轻锐之士，故蜀以再亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165088_comment'></div>至太祖受命，而吾祖不及见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165088_comment'></div>吾祖娶于李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165088_comment'></div>李氏，唐之苗裔，太宗之子曹王明之后世，曰瑜，为遂州长江尉，失官，家于眉之丹棱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165088_comment'></div>祖母严毅，居家肃然，多才略，犹有窦太后、柴氏主之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1165088", 1165088, "Clauses/85/Comments/1")'>遗烈</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165088_comment'></div>生子五人，其才皆不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165088_comment'></div>宗善、宗晏、宗昪，循循无所毁誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165088_comment'></div>少子宗晁，轻侠难制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165088_comment'></div>而吾父杲最好善，事父母极于孝，与兄弟笃于爱，与朋友笃于信，乡闾之人，无亲疏皆敬爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165088_comment'></div>娶宋氏夫人，事上甚孝谨，而御下甚严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165088_comment'></div>生子九人，而吾独存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165088_comment'></div>善治生，有馀财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165088_comment'></div>时蜀新破，其达官争弃其田宅以入觐，吾父独不肯取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165088_comment'></div>曰：『吾恐累吾子』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165088_comment'></div>终其身，田不满二顷，屋弊陋不葺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165088_comment'></div>好施与，曰：『多财而不施，吾恐他人谋我，然施而使人知之，人将以我为好名』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165088_comment'></div>是以施而尤恶使人知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165088_comment'></div>族叔父玩尝有重狱，将就逮，曰：『入狱而死，妻子以累兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1165088_comment'></div>请为我诇狱之轻重，轻也以肉馈我，重也以菜馈我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1165088_comment'></div>馈我以菜，吾将不食而死』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1165088_comment'></div>既而得释，玩曰：『吾非无他兄弟，可以寄死生者惟子』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1165088_comment'></div>及将殁，太夫人犹执吾手曰：『盍以是属子之兄弟』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1165088_comment'></div>笑曰：『而子贤，虽非吾兄弟，亦将与之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1165088_comment'></div>不贤，虽吾兄弟，亦将与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1165088_comment'></div>属之何益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1165088_comment'></div>善教之而已』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1165088_comment'></div>遂卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1165088_comment'></div>卒之岁，盖淳化五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1165088_comment'></div>推其生之年，则晋少帝之开运元年也」。<div class='inline'
