id='poem_sentence_30_1165028_comment'></div>曰：古者五刑之尤轻者止于墨，而墨之罚百锾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165028_comment'></div>逆而数之，极于大辟，而大辟之罚千锾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165028_comment'></div>此穆王之罚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165028_comment'></div>周公之时，则又重于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165028_comment'></div>然千锾之重，亦已当今三百七十斤有奇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165028_comment'></div>方今大辟之赎，不能当其三分之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165028_comment'></div>古者以之赦疑罪而不及公族，今也贵人近戚皆赎，而疑罪不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165028_comment'></div>《记》曰：「公族有死罪，致刑于甸人，虽君命宥，不听」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165028_comment'></div>今欲贵人近戚之刑举从于此，则非所以自尊之道，故莫若使得与疑罪皆重赎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165028_comment'></div>且彼虽号为富强，茍数犯法而数重困于赎金之间，则不能不敛手畏法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1165028_comment'></div>彼罪疑者，虽或非其辜，而法亦不至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1165028", 1165028, "Clauses/132/Comments/0")'>残溃</span>其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1165028", 1165028, "Clauses/132/Comments/1")'>肌体</span>，若其有罪，则法虽不刑，而彼固亦已困于赎金矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1165028_comment'></div>夫使有罪者不免于困，而无辜者不至陷于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1165028", 1165028, "Clauses/137/Comments/0")'>笞戮</span>，一举而两利，斯智者之为也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1165028_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1165028'>者：原无，据经进本补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1165028_comment'></div>按上文「而其所以不若三代者，亦有由矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1165028_comment'></div>此句与之对应，当有「者」字。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1165028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1165028'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_42_1165028_0'>⑴ 《苏老泉先生全集》卷五。又见《国朝二百家名贤文粹》卷二七。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1165028_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1165029' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165029' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165029?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span>兵制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165029_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165029'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165029'>三代之时，举天下之民皆兵也，兵民之分自秦汉始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165029_comment'></div>三代之时，闻有诸侯抗天子之命矣，未闻有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1165029", 1165029, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>卒伍</span>叫呼衡行者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165029_comment'></div>秦汉以来，诸侯之患不减于三代，而御<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1165029", 1165029, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>卒伍</span>者乃如蓄虎豹，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1165029", 1165029, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>圈槛</span>一缺，咆勃四出，其故何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165029_comment'></div>三代之兵耕而食，蚕而衣，故劳，劳则善心生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165029_comment'></div>秦、汉以来，所谓兵者，皆坐而衣食于县官，故骄，骄则无所不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165029_comment'></div>三代之兵皆齐民，老幼相养，疾病相救，出相礼让，入相慈孝，有忧相吊，有喜相庆，其风俗优柔而和易，故其兵畏法而自重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165029_comment'></div>秦、汉以来，号齐民者，比之三代，则既已薄矣，况其所谓兵者，乃其齐民之中尤为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1165029", 1165029, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>凶悍</span>桀黠者也，故常慢法而自弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165029_comment'></div>夫民耕而食，蚕而衣，虽不幸而不给，犹不我咎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165029_comment'></div>今谓之曰：尔毋耕，尔毋蚕，为我兵，吾衣食尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165029_comment'></div>他日一不充其欲，彼将曰：向谓我毋耕毋蚕，今而不我给也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165029_comment'></div>然则怨从是起矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165029_comment'></div>夫以有善心之民，畏法自重而不我咎，欲其为乱，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165029_comment'></div>既骄矣，又慢法而自弃，以怨其上，欲其不为乱，亦不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165029_comment'></div>且夫天下之地不加于三代，天下之民衣食乎其中者，又不减于三代，平居无事，占军籍，畜妻子，而仰给于斯民者，则遍天下不知其数，奈何民之不日剥月割，以至于流亡而无告也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165029_comment'></div>其患始于废井田，开阡陌，一坏而不可复收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165029_comment'></div>故虽有明君贤臣焦思极虑，而求以救其弊，卒不过开屯田，置府兵，使之无事则耕而食耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165029_comment'></div>呜呼，屯田府兵，其利既不足以及天下，而后世之君又不能循而守之，以至于废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165029_comment'></div>陵夷及于五代，燕帅刘守光又从而为之黥面<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1165029", 1165029, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>涅手</span>之制，天下遂以为常法，使之判然不得与齐民齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165029_comment'></div>故其人益复自弃，视齐民如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1165029", 1165029, "Clauses/88/Comments/0")'>越人</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165029_comment'></div>太祖既受命，惩唐季、五代之乱，聚重兵京师，而边境亦不曰无备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165029_comment'></div>损节度之权，而藩镇亦不曰无威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165029_comment'></div>周与汉、唐，邦镇之兵强；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165029_comment'></div>秦郡县之兵弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165029_comment'></div>兵强故末大不掉，兵弱故天下孤睽，周与汉、唐则过，而秦则不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165029_comment'></div>得其中者，惟吾宋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165029_comment'></div>虽然，置帅之方则远过于前代，而制兵之术吾犹有疑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165029_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165029_comment'></div>自汉迄唐，或开屯田，或置府兵，使之无事则耕而食，而民犹且不胜其患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165029_comment'></div>今屯田盖无几，而府兵亦已废，欲民之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1165029", 1165029, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>丰阜</span>，势不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165029_comment'></div>国家治平日久，民之趋于农者日益众，而天下无莱田矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165029_comment'></div>以此观之，谓斯民宜如生三代之盛时，而乃戚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1165029", 1165029, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>戚嗟</span>嗟无终岁之畜者，兵食夺之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165029_comment'></div>三代井田，虽三尺童子知其不可复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165029_comment'></div>虽然，依仿古制，渐而图之，则亦庶乎其可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165029_comment'></div>方今天下之田在官者惟二：职分也，籍没也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165029_comment'></div>职分之田，募民耕之，敛其租之半而归诸吏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165029_comment'></div>籍没则鬻之，否则募民耕之，敛其租之半而归诸公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165029_comment'></div>职分之田遍于天下，自四京以降至于大藩镇，多至四十顷，下及一县亦能千亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165029_comment'></div>籍没之田不知其数，今可勿复鬻，然后量给其所募之民，家三百亩以为率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165029_comment'></div>前之敛其半者，今可损之，三分而取其一，以归诸吏与公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165029_comment'></div>使之家出一夫为兵，其不欲者，听其归田而他募。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165029_comment'></div>谓之新军，毋黥其面，毋涅其手，毋拘之营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1165029_comment'></div>三时纵之，一时集之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1165029_comment'></div>授之器械，教之战法，而择其技之精者以为长，在野督其耕，在阵督其战，则其人皆良农也，皆精兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1165029_comment'></div>夫籍没之田既不复鬻，则岁益多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1165029_comment'></div>田益多则新军益众，而向所谓仰给于斯民者，虽有废疾死亡，可勿复补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1165029_comment'></div>如此数十年，则天下之兵，新军居十九而皆力田不事他业，则其人必纯固朴厚，无叫呼衡行之忧，而斯民不复知有馈饷供亿之劳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1165029_comment'></div>或曰：昔者敛其半，今三分而取一，其无乃薄于吏与公乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1165029_comment'></div>曰：古者公卿大夫之有田也以为禄，而其取之亦不过什一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1165029_comment'></div>今吏既禄矣，给之田则已甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1165029_comment'></div>况三分而取一，则不既优矣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1165029_comment'></div>民之田不幸而籍没，非官之所待以为富也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1165029_comment'></div>三分而取一，不犹愈于无乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1165029_comment'></div>且不如是，则彼不胜为兵故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1165029_comment'></div>或曰：古者什一而税，取之薄，故民胜为兵，今三分而取一，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1165029_comment'></div>曰：古者一家之中，一人为正卒，其馀为羡卒，田与追胥竭作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1165029_comment'></div>今家止一夫为兵，况诸古则为逸，故虽取之差重而无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1165029_comment'></div>此与周制稍甸县都役少轻，而税十二无异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1165029_comment'></div>夫民家出一夫而得安坐以食数百亩之田，征繇科敛不及其门，然则彼亦优为之矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1165029_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165030' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165030' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165030?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span>田制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165030_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165030'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165030'>古之税重乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165030_comment'></div>今之税重乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165030_comment'></div>周公之制，园廛二十而税一，近郊十一，远郊二十而三，稍甸县都皆无过十二，漆林之征二十而五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165030_comment'></div>盖周之盛时，其尤重者至四分而取一，其次者乃五而取一，然后以次而轻，始至于十一，而又有轻者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165030_comment'></div>今之税虽不啻十一，然而使县官无急征，无横敛，则亦未至乎四而取一与五而取一之为多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165030_comment'></div>是今之税与周之税，轻重之相去无几也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165030_comment'></div>虽然，当周之时，天下之民歌舞以乐其上之盛德，而吾之民反戚戚不乐，常若擢筋剥肤以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1165030", 1165030, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>供亿</span>其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165030_comment'></div>周之税如此，吾之税亦如此，而其民之哀乐何如此之相远也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165030_comment'></div>其所以然者，盖有由矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165030_comment'></div>周之时用井田，井田废，田非耕者之所有，而有田者不耕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165030_comment'></div>耕者之田资于富民，富民之家地大业广，阡陌连接，募召<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1165030", 1165030, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>浮客</span>，分耕其中，鞭笞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1165030", 1165030, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>驱役</span>，视以奴仆，安坐四顾，指麾于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165030_comment'></div>而役属之民，夏为之耨，秋为之穫，无有一人违其节度以嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165030_comment'></div>而田之所入，己得其半，耕者得其半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165030_comment'></div>有田者一人，而耕者十人，是以田主日累其半以至于富强，耕者日食其半以至于穷饿而无告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165030_comment'></div>夫使耕者至于穷饿，而不耕不穫者坐而食富强之利，犹且不可；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165030_comment'></div>而况富强之民输租于县官，而不免于怨叹嗟愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165030_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165030_comment'></div>彼以其半而供县官之税，不若周之民以其全力而供其上之税也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165030_comment'></div>周之十一，以其全力而供十一之税也，使以其半供十一之税，犹用十二之税然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165030_comment'></div>况今之税，又非特止于十一而已，则宜乎其怨叹嗟愤之不免也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165030_comment'></div>噫，贫民耕而不免于饥，富民坐而饱以嬉，又不免于怨，其弊皆起于废井田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165030_comment'></div>井田复，则贫民有田以耕，谷食粟米不分于富民，可以无饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165030_comment'></div>富民不得多占田以锢贫民，其势不耕则无所得食，以地之全力供县官之税，又可以无怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165030_comment'></div>是以天下之士争言复井田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165030_comment'></div>既又有言者曰：夺富民之田以与无田之民，则富民不伏，此必生乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165030_comment'></div>如乘大乱之后，土旷而人稀，可以一举而就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165030_comment'></div>高祖之灭秦，光武之承汉，可为而不为，以是为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165030_comment'></div>吾又以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165030_comment'></div>今虽使富民皆奉其田而归诸公，乞为井田，其势亦不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165030_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165030_comment'></div>井田之制，九天为井，井间有沟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165030_comment'></div>四井为邑，四邑为丘，四丘为甸，甸方八里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165030_comment'></div>旁加一里为一成，成间有洫，其地百井而方十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165030_comment'></div>四甸为县，四县为都，四都方八十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165030_comment'></div>旁加十里为一同，同间有浍，其地万井而方百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165030_comment'></div>百里之间为浍者一，为洫者百，为沟者万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165030_comment'></div>既为井田，又必兼修沟洫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165030_comment'></div>沟洫之制：夫间有遂，遂上有径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165030_comment'></div>十夫有沟，沟上有畛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165030_comment'></div>百夫有洫，洫上有涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165030_comment'></div>千夫有浍，浍上有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1165030_comment'></div>万夫有川，川上有路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1165030_comment'></div>万夫之地，盖三十二里有半，而其间为川为路者一，为浍为道者九，为洫为涂者百，为沟为畛者千，为遂为径者万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1165030_comment'></div>此二者非塞溪壑，平涧谷，夷丘陵，破坟墓，坏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1165030", 1165030, "Clauses/142/Comments/0")'>庐舍</span>，徙城郭，易疆垄，不可为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1165030_comment'></div>纵使能尽得平原广野而遂规画于其中，亦当驱天下之人，竭天下之粮，穷数百年专力于此，不治他事，而后可以望天下之地尽为井田，尽为沟洫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1165030_comment'></div>已而，又为民作屋庐于其中，以安其居，而后可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1165030_comment'></div>吁，亦已迂矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1165030_comment'></div>井田成而民之死，其骨已朽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1165030_comment'></div>古者井田之兴，其必始于唐虞之世乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1165030_comment'></div>非唐虞之世，则周之世无以成井田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1165030_comment'></div>唐虞启之，至于夏商稍稍葺治，至周而大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1165030_comment'></div>周公承之，因遂申定其制度，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1165030", 1165030, "Clauses/170/Comments/0")'>疏整</span>其疆界，非一日而遽能如此也，其所由来者渐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1165030_comment'></div>夫井田虽不可为，而其实便于今，今诚有能为近井田者而用之，则亦可以苏民矣乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1165030_comment'></div>闻之董生曰：「井田虽难卒行，宜少近古，限民名田以赡不足」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1165030_comment'></div>名田之说，盖出于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1165030_comment'></div>而后世未有行者，非以不便民也，惧民不肯损其田以入吾法，而遂因之以为变也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1165030_comment'></div>孔光、何武曰：「吏民名田无过三十顷，期尽三年，而犯者没入官」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1165030_comment'></div>夫三十顷之田，周民三十夫之田也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1165030_comment'></div>纵不能尽如周制，一人而兼三十夫之田，亦已过矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1165030_comment'></div>而期之三年，是又迫蹙平民，使自坏其业，非人情，难用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1165030_comment'></div>吾欲少为之限，而不禁其田尝已过吾限者，但使后之人不敢多占田以过吾限耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1165030_comment'></div>要之数世，富者之子孙，或不能保其地以复于贫，而彼尝已过吾限者，散而入于他人矣，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1165030", 1165030, "Clauses/209/Comments/0")'>或者</span>子孙出而分之以无几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1165030_comment'></div>如此，则富民所占者少而馀地多，馀地多则贫民易取以为业，不为人所役属，各食其地之全利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1165030_comment'></div>利不分于人，而乐输于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1165030_comment'></div>夫端坐于朝廷，下令于天下，不惊民，不动众，不用井田之制，而获井田之利，虽周之井田，何以远过于此哉？</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1165030_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《六经论》作品：《六经论·易论》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷六。）</span>《六经论·礼论》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷六。）</span>《六经论·乐论》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷六。）</span>《六经论·诗论》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷六。）</span>《六经论·书论》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷六。）</span>《六经论·春秋论》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1165031' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165031' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165031?labeling=true' target='_blank'>六经论<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>易论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165031")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165031_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165031'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165031'>圣人之道，得《礼》而信，得《易》而尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165031_comment'></div>信之而不可废，尊之而不敢废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165031_comment'></div>故圣人之道所以不废者，《礼》为之明，而《易》为之幽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165031_comment'></div>生民之初，无贵贱，无尊卑，无长幼，不耕而不饥，不蚕而不寒，故其民逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165031_comment'></div>民之苦劳而乐逸也，若水之走下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165031_comment'></div>而圣人者，独为之君臣，而使天下贵役贱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165031_comment'></div>为之父子，而使天下尊役卑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165031_comment'></div>为之兄弟，而使天下长役幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165031_comment'></div>蚕而后衣，耕而后食，率天下而劳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165031_comment'></div>一圣人之力，固非足以胜天下之民之众，而其所以能夺其乐而易之以其所苦，而天下之民亦遂肯弃逸而即劳，欣然戴之以为君师，而遵蹈其法制者，《礼》则使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165031_comment'></div>圣人之始作《礼》也，其说曰：天下无贵贱，无尊卑，无长幼，是人之相杀无已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165031_comment'></div>不耕而食鸟兽之肉，不蚕而衣鸟兽之皮，是鸟兽与人相食无已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165031_comment'></div>有贵贱，有尊卑，有长幼，则人不相杀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165031_comment'></div>食吾之所耕，而衣吾之所蚕，则鸟兽与人不相食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165031_comment'></div>人之好生也甚于逸，而恶死也甚于劳，圣人夺其逸、死，而与之劳、生，此虽三尺竖子知所趋避矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165031_comment'></div>故其道之所以信于天下而不可废者，《礼》为之明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165031_comment'></div>虽然，明则易达，易达则亵，亵则易废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165031_comment'></div>圣人惧其道之废，而天下复于乱也，然后作《易》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165031_comment'></div>观天地之象以为爻，通阴阳之变以为卦，考鬼神之情以为辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165031_comment'></div>探之茫茫，索之冥冥，童而习之，白首而不得其源，故天下视圣人如神之幽，如天之高，尊其人而其教亦随而尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165031_comment'></div>故其道之所以尊于天下而不敢废者，《易》为之幽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165031_comment'></div>凡人之所以见信者，以其中无所不可测者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165031_comment'></div>人之所以获尊者，以其中有所不可窥者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165031_comment'></div>是以《礼》无所不可测，而《易》有所不可窥，故天下之人信圣人之道而尊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165031_comment'></div>不然，则《易》者岂圣人务为新奇秘怪以夸后世邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165031_comment'></div>圣人不因天下之至神，则无所施其教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165031_comment'></div>卜筮者，天下之至神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165031_comment'></div>而卜者，听乎天而人不预焉者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165031_comment'></div>筮者，决之天而营之人者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165031_comment'></div>龟，漫而无理者也，灼荆而钻之，方功义弓，惟其所为，而人何预焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165031_comment'></div>圣人曰：是纯乎天技耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165031_comment'></div>技何所施吾教？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165031_comment'></div>于是取筮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165031_comment'></div>夫筮之所以或为阳，或为阴者，必自分而为二始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165031_comment'></div>挂一，吾知其为一而挂之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165031_comment'></div>揲之以四，吾知其为四而揲之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165031_comment'></div>归奇于扐，吾知其为一、为二、为三、为四而归之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165031_comment'></div>人也分而为二，吾不知其为几而分之也，天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165031_comment'></div>圣人曰：是天人参焉，道也，道有所施吾教矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165031_comment'></div>于是因而作《易》，以神天下之耳目，而其道遂尊而不废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165031_comment'></div>此圣人用其机权以持天下之心，而济其道于无穷也。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1165031'></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1165031_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165032' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165032' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165032?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>礼论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165032_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165032'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165032'>夫人之情，安于其所常为，无故而变其俗，则其势必不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165032_comment'></div>圣人之始作礼也，不因其势之可以危亡困辱之者以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1165032", 1165032, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>厌服</span>其心，而徒欲使之轻去其旧，而乐就吾法，不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165032_comment'></div>故无故而使之事君，无故而使之事父，无故而使之事兄，彼其初，非如今之人知君父兄之不事则不可也，而遂翻然以从我者，吾以耻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1165032", 1165032, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>厌服</span>其心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165032_comment'></div>彼为吾君，彼为吾父，彼为吾兄，圣人曰：彼为吾君父兄，何以异于我？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165032_comment'></div>于是坐其君与其父以及其兄，而己立于其旁，且俛首屈膝于其前以为礼，而谓之拜，率天下之人，而使之拜其君父兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165032_comment'></div>夫无故而使之拜其君，无故而使之拜其父，无故而使之拜其兄，则天下之人将复嗤笑，以为迂怪而不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165032_comment'></div>而君父兄又不可以不得其臣子弟之拜而徒为其君父兄，于是圣人者又有术焉，以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1165032", 1165032, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>厌服</span>其心，而使之肯拜其君父兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165032_comment'></div>然则圣人者，果何术也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165032_comment'></div>耻之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165032_comment'></div>古之圣人将欲以礼治天下之民，故先自治其身，使天下皆信其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165032_comment'></div>曰：此人也，其言如是，是必不可不如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165032_comment'></div>故圣人曰：天下有不拜其君父兄者，吾不与之齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165032_comment'></div>而使天下之人亦曰：彼将不与我齿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165032_comment'></div>于是相率以拜其君父兄，以求齿于圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165032_comment'></div>虽然，彼圣人者，必欲天下之拜其君父兄，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165032_comment'></div>其微权也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165032_comment'></div>彼为吾君，彼为吾父，彼为吾兄，圣人之拜不用于世，吾与之皆坐于此，皆立于此，比肩而行于此，无以异也，吾一旦而怒，奋手举梃而搏逐之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165032_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165032_comment'></div>彼其心常以为吾侪也，不见其异于吾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165032_comment'></div>圣人知人之安于逸而苦于劳，故使贵者逸而贱者劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165032_comment'></div>且又知坐之为逸，而立且拜者之为劳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165032_comment'></div>故举其君父兄坐之于上，而使之立且拜于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165032_comment'></div>明日彼将有怒作于心者，徐而自思之，必曰：此吾向之所坐而拜之，且立于其下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165032_comment'></div>圣人固使之逸而使我劳，是贱于彼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165032_comment'></div>奋手举梃以搏逐之，吾心不安焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165032_comment'></div>刻木而为人，朝夕而拜之，他日析之以为薪，而犹且忌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165032_comment'></div>彼其始木焉，已拜之犹且不敢以为薪，故圣人以其微权而使天下尊其君父兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165032_comment'></div>而权者又不可以告人，故先之以耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165032_comment'></div>呜呼，其事如此，然后君父兄得以安其尊而至于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165032_comment'></div>今之匹夫匹妇，莫不知拜其君父兄，乃曰拜起坐立，礼之末也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165032_comment'></div>不知圣人其始之教民拜起坐立，如此之劳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165032_comment'></div>此圣人之所虑，而作《易》以神其教也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1165032_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165033' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165033' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165033?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>乐论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165033_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165033'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165033'>礼之始作也，难而易行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165033_comment'></div>既行也，易而难久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165033_comment'></div>天下未知君之为君，父之为父，兄之为兄，而圣人为之君父兄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165033_comment'></div>天下未有以异其君父兄，而圣人为之拜起坐立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165033_comment'></div>天下未肯靡然以从我拜起坐立，而圣人身先之以耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165033_comment'></div>呜呼，其亦难矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165033_comment'></div>天下恶夫死也久矣，圣人招之曰：来，吾生尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165033_comment'></div>既而其法果可以生天下之人，天下之人视其向也如此之危，而今也如此之安，则宜何从？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165033_comment'></div>故当其时，虽难而易行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165033_comment'></div>既行也，天下之人视君父兄，如头足之不待别白而后识，视拜起坐立如寝食之不待告语而后从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165033_comment'></div>虽然，百人从之，一人不从，则其势不得遽至乎死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165033_comment'></div>天下之人，不知其初之无礼而死，而见其今之无礼而不至乎死也，则曰圣人欺我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165033_comment'></div>故当其时，虽易而难久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165033_comment'></div>呜呼，圣人之所恃以胜天下之劳逸者，独有死生之说耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165033_comment'></div>死生之说不信于天下，则劳逸之说将出而胜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165033_comment'></div>劳逸之说胜，则圣人之权去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165033_comment'></div>酒有鸩，肉有堇，然后人不敢饮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165033_comment'></div>药可以生死，然后人不以苦口为讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165033_comment'></div>去其鸩，彻其堇，则酒肉之权固胜于药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165033_comment'></div>圣人之始作礼也，其亦逆知其势之将必如此也，曰：告人以诚，而后人信之，幸今之时吾之所以告人者，其理诚然，而其事亦然，故人以为信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165033_comment'></div>吾知其理，而天下之人知其事，事有不必然者，则吾之理不足以折天下之口，此告语之所不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165033_comment'></div>告语之所不及，必有以阴驱而潜率之，于是观之天地之间，得其至神之机，而窃之以为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165033_comment'></div>雨，吾见其所以湿万物也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165033_comment'></div>日，吾见其所以燥万物也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165033_comment'></div>风，吾见其所以动万物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165033_comment'></div>隐隐谹谹，而谓之雷者，彼何用也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165033_comment'></div>阴凝而不散，物蹙而不遂，雨之所不能湿，日之所不能燥，风之所不能动，雷一震焉而凝者散，蹙者遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165033_comment'></div>曰雨者，曰日者，曰风者，以形用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165033_comment'></div>曰雷者，以神用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165033_comment'></div>用莫神于声，故圣人因声以为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165033_comment'></div>为之君臣、父子、兄弟者，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165033_comment'></div>礼之所不及，而乐及焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165033_comment'></div>正声入乎耳，而人皆有事君、事父、事兄之心，则礼者固吾心之所有也，而圣人之说，又何从而不信乎？</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1165033_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165034' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165034' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165034?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>诗论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165034_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165034'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165034'>人之嗜欲，好之有甚于生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165034_comment'></div>而愤憾怨怒，有不顾其死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165034_comment'></div>于是礼之权又穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165034_comment'></div>礼之法曰：好色不可为也，为人臣，为人子，为人弟，不可以有怨于其君父兄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165034_comment'></div>使天下之人皆不好色，皆不怨其君父兄，夫岂不善？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165034_comment'></div>使人之情皆泊然而无思，和易而优柔，以从事于此，则天下固亦大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165034_comment'></div>而人之情，又不能皆然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165034_comment'></div>好色之心驱诸其中，是非不平之气攻诸其外，炎炎而生，不顾利害，趋死而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165034_comment'></div>噫，礼之权止于死生，天下之事不至乎可以博生者，则人不敢触死以违吾法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165034_comment'></div>今也，人之好色与人之是非不平之心，勃然而发于中，以为可以博生也，而先以死自处其身，则死生之机固已去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165034_comment'></div>死生之机去，则礼为无权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165034_comment'></div>区区举无权之礼以强人之所不能，则乱益甚，而礼益败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165034_comment'></div>今吾告人曰：必无好色，必无怨而君父兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165034_comment'></div>彼将遂从吾言，而忘其中心所自有之情邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165034_comment'></div>将不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165034_comment'></div>彼既已不能纯用吾法，将遂大弃而不顾吾法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165034_comment'></div>既已大弃而不顾，则人之好色与怨其君父兄之心，将遂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1165034", 1165034, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>荡然</span>无所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1165034", 1165034, "Clauses/50/Comments/1")'>隔限</span>，而易内窃妻之变，与弑其君父兄之祸，必反公行于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165034_comment'></div>圣人忧焉，曰：禁人之好色而至于淫，禁人之怨其君父兄而至于叛，患生于责人太详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165034_comment'></div>好色之不绝，而怨之不禁，则彼将反不至于乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165034_comment'></div>故圣人之道，严于礼而通于《诗》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165034_comment'></div>礼曰必无好色，必无怨而君父兄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165034_comment'></div>《诗》曰好色而无至于淫，怨而君父兄而无至于叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165034_comment'></div>严以待天下之贤人，通以全天下之中人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165034_comment'></div>吾观《国风》婉娈柔媚而卒守以正，好色而不至于淫者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165034_comment'></div>《小雅》悲伤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1165034", 1165034, "Clauses/72/Comments/2")'>诟讟</span>，而君臣之情卒不忍去，怨而不至于叛者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165034_comment'></div>故天下观之，曰圣人固许我以好色，而不尤我之怨吾君父兄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165034_comment'></div>许我以好色，不淫可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165034_comment'></div>不尤我之怨吾君父兄，则彼虽以虐遇我，我明讥而明怨之，使天下明知之，则吾之怨亦得当焉，不叛可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165034_comment'></div>夫背圣人之法而自弃于淫叛之地者，非断不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165034_comment'></div>断之始，生于不胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165034_comment'></div>人不自胜其忿，然后忍弃其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165034_comment'></div>故《诗》之教，不使人之情至于不胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165034_comment'></div>夫桥之所以为安于舟者，以有桥而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165034_comment'></div>水潦大至，桥必解，而舟不至于必败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165034_comment'></div>故舟者，所以济桥之所不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165034_comment'></div>吁，礼之权穷于易达，而有《易》焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165034_comment'></div>穷于后世之不信，而有《乐》焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165034_comment'></div>穷于强人，而有《诗》焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165034_comment'></div>吁，圣人之虑事也盖详。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1165034_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165035?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>书论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165035'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165035'>风俗之变，圣人为之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165035_comment'></div>圣人因风俗之变而用其权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165035_comment'></div>圣人之权用于当世，而风俗之变益甚，以至于不可复反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165035_comment'></div>幸而又有圣人焉，承其后而维之，则天下可以复治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165035_comment'></div>不幸其后无圣人，其变穷而无所复入，则已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165035_comment'></div>昔者，吾尝欲观古之变而不可得也，于《诗》见商与周焉而不详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165035_comment'></div>及观《书》，然后见尧舜之时，与三代之相变如此之亟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165035_comment'></div>自尧而至于商，其变也皆得圣人而承之，故无忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165035_comment'></div>至于周，而天下之变穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165035_comment'></div>忠之变而入于质，质之变而入于文，其势便也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165035_comment'></div>及夫文之变，而又欲反之于忠也，是犹欲移江河而行之山也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165035_comment'></div>人之喜文而恶质与忠也，犹水之不肯避下而就高也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165035_comment'></div>彼其始未尝文焉，故忠质而不辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165035_comment'></div>今吾日食之以太牢，而欲使之复茹其菽哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165035_comment'></div>呜呼，其后无圣人，其变穷而无所复入，则已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165035_comment'></div>周之后而无王焉，固也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165035_comment'></div>其始之制其风俗也，固不容为其后者计也，而又适不值乎圣人，固也，后之无王者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165035_comment'></div>当尧之时，举天下而授之舜，舜得尧之天下，而又授之禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165035_comment'></div>方尧之未授天下于舜也，天下未尝闻有如此之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165035_comment'></div>度其当时之民，莫不以为大怪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165035_comment'></div>然而舜与禹也，受而居之，安然若天下固其所有，而其祖宗既已为之累数十世者，未尝与其民道其所以当得天下之故也，又未尝悦之以利，而开之以丹朱、商均之不肖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165035_comment'></div>其意以为天下之民以我为当在此位也，则亦不俟乎援天以神之，誉己以固之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165035_comment'></div>汤之伐桀也，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1165035", 1165035, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>嚣嚣</span>然数其罪而以告人，如曰彼有罪，我伐之宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165035_comment'></div>既又惧天下之民不己悦也，则又<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1165035", 1165035, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>嚣嚣</span>然以言柔之曰：「万方有罪，在予一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165035_comment'></div>予一人有罪，无以尔万方」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165035_comment'></div>如曰我如是而为尔之君，尔可以许我焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165035_comment'></div>吁，亦既薄矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165035_comment'></div>至于武王而又自言其先祖父偕有显功，既已受命而死，其大业不克终，今我奉承其志，举兵而东伐，而东国之士女束帛以迎我，纣之兵倒戈以纳我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165035_comment'></div>吁，又甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165035_comment'></div>如曰吾家之当为天子久矣，如此乎，民之欲我速入商也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165035_comment'></div>伊尹之在商也，如周公之在周也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165035_comment'></div>伊尹摄位三年而无一言以自解，周公为之纷纷乎急于自疏其非篡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165035_comment'></div>夫固由风俗之变而后用其权，权用而风俗成，吾安坐而镇之，夫孰知夫风俗之变而不复反也？</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1165035_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165036' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165036' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165036?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>春秋论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165036_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165036'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165036'>赏罚者，天下之公也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165036_comment'></div>是非者，一人之私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165036_comment'></div>位之所在，则圣人以其权为天下之公，而天下以惩以劝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165036_comment'></div>道之所在，则圣人以其权为一人之私，而天下以荣以辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165036_comment'></div>周之衰也，位不在夫子，而道在焉，夫子以其权是非天下可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165036_comment'></div>而《春秋》赏人之功，赦人之罪，去人之族，绝人之国，贬人之爵，诸侯而或书其名，大夫而或书其字，不惟其法，惟其意，不徒曰此是此非，而赏罚加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165036_comment'></div>则夫子固曰：我可以赏罚人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165036_comment'></div>赏罚人者，天子、诸侯事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165036_comment'></div>夫子病天下之诸侯、大夫僭天子诸侯之事，而作《春秋》，而己则为之，其何以责天下？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165036_comment'></div>位，公也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165036_comment'></div>道，私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165036_comment'></div>私不胜公，则道不胜位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165036_comment'></div>位之权得以赏罚，而道之权不过于是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165036_comment'></div>道在我矣，而不得为有位者之事，则天下皆曰位之不可僭也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165036_comment'></div>不然，天下其谁不曰道在我？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165036_comment'></div>则是道者，位之贼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165036_comment'></div>曰：夫子岂诚赏罚之邪，徒曰赏罚之耳，庸何伤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165036_comment'></div>曰：我非君也，非吏也，执涂之人而告之曰：某为善，某为恶，可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165036_comment'></div>继之曰：某为善，吾赏之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165036_comment'></div>某为恶，吾诛之，则人有不笑我者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165036_comment'></div>夫子之赏罚何以异此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165036_comment'></div>然则，何足以为夫子？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165036_comment'></div>何足以为《春秋》？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165036_comment'></div>曰：夫子之作《春秋》也，非曰孔氏之书也，又非曰我作之也，赏罚之权不以自与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165036_comment'></div>曰：此鲁之书也，鲁作之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165036_comment'></div>有善而赏之，曰鲁赏之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165036_comment'></div>有恶而罚之，曰鲁罚之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165036_comment'></div>何以知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165036_comment'></div>曰：夫子系《易》谓之《系辞》，言孝谓之《孝经》，皆自名之，则夫子私之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165036_comment'></div>而《春秋》者，鲁之所以名史，而夫子托焉，则夫子公之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165036_comment'></div>公之以鲁史之名，则赏罚之权固在鲁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165036_comment'></div>《春秋》之赏罚自鲁而及于天下，天子之权也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165036_comment'></div>鲁之赏罚不出境，而以天子之权与之，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165036_comment'></div>曰：天子之权在周，夫子不得已而以与鲁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165036_comment'></div>武王之崩也，天子之位当在成王，而成王幼，周公以为天下不可以无赏罚，故不得已而摄天子之位，以赏罚天下，以存周室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165036_comment'></div>周之东迁也，天子之权当在平王，而平王昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165036_comment'></div>故夫子亦曰：天下不可以无赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165036_comment'></div>而鲁，周公之国也，居鲁之地者，宜如周公不得已而假天子之权以赏罚天下，以尊周室，故以天子之权与之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165036_comment'></div>然则，假天子之权宜如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165036_comment'></div>曰：如齐桓、晋文可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165036_comment'></div>夫子欲鲁如齐桓、晋文，而不遂以天子之权与齐、晋者，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1165036_comment'></div>齐桓、晋文阳为尊周，而实欲富强其国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1165036_comment'></div>故夫子与其事而不与其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1165036_comment'></div>周公心存王室，虽其子孙不能继，而夫子思周公而许其假天子之权以赏罚天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1165036_comment'></div>其意曰：有周公之心，而后可以行桓、文之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1165036_comment'></div>此其所以不与齐、晋而与鲁也，夫子亦知鲁君之才不足以行周公之事矣，顾其心以为今之天下无周公，故至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1165036_comment'></div>是故以天子之权与其子孙，所以见思周公之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1165036_comment'></div>吾观《春秋》之法，皆周公之法，而又详内而略外，此其意欲鲁法周公之所为，且先自治而后治人也，明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1165036_comment'></div>夫子叹礼乐征伐自诸侯出，而田常弑其君，则沐浴而请讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1165036_comment'></div>然则天子之权，夫子固明以与鲁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1165036_comment'></div>子贡之徒不达夫子之意，续《经》而书孔丘卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1165036_comment'></div>夫子既告老矣，大夫告老而卒不书，而夫子独书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1165036_comment'></div>夫子作《春秋》以公天下，而岂私一孔丘哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1165036_comment'></div>呜呼，夫子以为鲁国之书，而子贡之徒以为孔氏之书也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1165036_comment'></div>迁、固之史有是非而无赏罚，彼亦史臣之体宜尔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1165036_comment'></div>后之效夫子作《春秋》者，吾惑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1165036_comment'></div>《春秋》有天子之权，天下有君，则《春秋》不当作；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1165036_comment'></div>天下无君，则天下之权吾不知其谁与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1165036_comment'></div>天下之人，乌有如周公之后之可与者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1165036_comment'></div>与之而不得其人则乱，不与人而自与则僭，不与人、不自与而无所与则散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1165036_comment'></div>呜呼，后之《春秋》，乱邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1165036_comment'></div>僭邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1165036_comment'></div>散邪？</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1165036_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《太玄论》作品：《太玄论·太玄论上》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷七。）</span>《太玄论·太玄论中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷七。）</span>《太玄论·太玄论下》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷七。）</span>《太玄论·太玄总例（并引）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1165038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太玄论<span class='inlineComment2'>（中）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165038")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165038'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165038'>四分日之一，或曰一百分日之二十五，在四以为一，在百以为二十五，唯其所在而加之，岂有常数哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165038_comment'></div>六日七分者，以八十言者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165038_comment'></div>茍有以适于用，吾斯从而加之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165038_comment'></div>《坎》、《离》、《震》、《兑》各守其方，而六十卦之爻分散于三百六十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165038_comment'></div>圣人不以五日四分日之一者害其为《易》，而以七分者加焉，此非有所法乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165038_comment'></div>日月星辰之度，天地五行之数也，以其上之不可以八，而下之不可以六，故以七分者加之，使夫《易》者亦不为无用于历而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165038_comment'></div>夫八十分与夫七分者，皆非其所以为《易》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165038_comment'></div>上下而为卦，九、六而为爻，此其所以为《易》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165038_comment'></div>圣人不于其所以为《易》者加之，故加焉而不害其为《易》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165038_comment'></div>若夫四位而为首，九行而为赞，此正其所以为《太玄》者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165038_comment'></div>而雄于此加焉，故吾不知其为《太玄》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165038_comment'></div>始于《中》之一，而讫于《养》之九，阙焉而未见者，四分日之三而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165038_comment'></div>以一百八分而为日，以一分而加之，一首之外尽八十一首，而四分日之三者可以见矣，观《周》之一，知昼夜之不在乎奇偶，而在其所承；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165038_comment'></div>观《中》之九，知休咎之不在乎昼夜，而在其所处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165038_comment'></div>故积其分至于《养》之九，而可以无患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165038_comment'></div>盖《易》之本六日以为卦，《太玄》之初四日有半以为首，而皆以四百八十七分，求合乎二十八宿之度，加分而其数定，去《踦》、《赢》而其道胜，吾无憾焉耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1165038_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165040' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165040' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165040?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太玄总例<span class='inlineComment2'>（并引）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165040")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165040_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165040'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165040'>吾既作《太玄论》，或者读扬子之书未知其详，而以意诘吾说，病辞之不给也，为作此例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165040_comment'></div>凡雄之法与夫先儒之论，其可取者皆在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165040_comment'></div>有未尽，传之己意，曰姑观是焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165040_comment'></div>盖雄者好奇而务深，故辞多夸大，而可观者鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165040_comment'></div>始之以十八策，中之以三十六，终之以七十二，积之以二万六千二百四十四，张而不已，谁不能然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165040_comment'></div>盖总例之外无观焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1165040_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《洪范论》作品：《洪范论·洪范论叙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷八。）</span>《洪范论·洪范上》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷八。）</span>《洪范论·洪范中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷八。）</span>《洪范论·洪范下》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷八。）</span>《洪范论·洪范后序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1165053' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165053' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165053?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪范论 洪范论叙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165053")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165053_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165053'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165053'>《洪范》其不可行欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165053_comment'></div>何说者之多，而行者之寡也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165053_comment'></div>曰：诸儒使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165053_comment'></div>譬诸律令，其始作者非不欲人之难犯而易避矣，及吏胥舞之，则千机百阱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165053_comment'></div>吁，可畏也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165053_comment'></div>夫《洪范》亦犹是耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165053_comment'></div>吾病其然，因作三论，大抵斥末而归本，褒经而击传，刬磨瑕垢，以见圣秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165053_comment'></div>复列二图，一以指其谬，一以形吾意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165053_comment'></div>噫，人吾知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165053_comment'></div>不吾知，其谓吾求异夫先儒，而以为新奇也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1165053_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪范论 洪范后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165059")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165059'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165059'>吾论《洪范》以五福六极系皇极之建与不建，而且不与二刘之增眊与阴，或者犹以刘向、夏侯胜之说为惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165059_comment'></div>刘向之言：「皇极之建，总为五福；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165059_comment'></div>皇极之不建，不能主五事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165059_comment'></div>下与五事齿而均获一极，犹平王之诗降而为《国风」》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165059_comment'></div>夏侯胜之言曰：「天久阴不雨，臣下将有谋上者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165059_comment'></div>已而果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165059_comment'></div>以刘向之说则皇极之不建，不可系以六极；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165059_comment'></div>以夏侯胜之说，则眊与阴不可废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165059_comment'></div>是皆不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165059_comment'></div>夫福、极之于五事，非若庶验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165059_comment'></div>阴阳而推之，律历而求之，人事而揆之，庶验之通于五事，可指而言也，且圣人之所可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165059_comment'></div>今指人而谓之曰：尔为某事，明日必有某福；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165059_comment'></div>尔为某事，明日必有某极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165059_comment'></div>是巫觋卜相之事也，而圣人何由知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165059_comment'></div>故吾以为皇极之建，五事皆得，而五福皆应；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165059_comment'></div>不曰应某事者，必某福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165059_comment'></div>皇极不建，五事皆失，而六极皆应；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165059_comment'></div>不曰应某事者，必某极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165059_comment'></div>五事之间得与失参焉，则亦不曰必某福，必某极应也，亦曰福与极参焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165059_comment'></div>今刘以为皇极建而为五事主，故加之五福；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165059_comment'></div>及其不建也，不加之以六极，而以平王之诗为说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165059_comment'></div>其意以为不建则不能为五事主，故不加之六极以为贬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165059_comment'></div>今有人有九命之爵，及有罪而曰削其爵，使至一命以贬之，曰贬可也，此犹平王之诗降而为《国风》，曰降可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165059_comment'></div>若夫有罪人当具五刑，而曰是人也，罪大不当加之以五刑，姑以墨辟论，以重其责，是得为重其责耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165059_comment'></div>今欲重不建之罪，不曰六极皆应，而曰独弱之极应，乃引平王之诗以为说，平王之诗固不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165059_comment'></div>且彼圣人者，岂以天下之福与极止于五与六而已哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165059_comment'></div>盖亦举其大概耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165059_comment'></div>夫天地之间，非人力所为而可以为验者多矣，圣人取其尤大而可以有所兼者五，而使其馀者可以遂见焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165059_comment'></div>今也，力分其一端以为二，而必曰阴为阴，雨为雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165059_comment'></div>且《经》之庶验有曰旸矣，而岂独遗阴哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165059_comment'></div>盖阴之极盛于雨，而圣人举其极者言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165059_comment'></div>吾观二刘之传「金不从革」，与传「常雨」也，乃言雷电雨雪皆在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165059_comment'></div>而独于此别雨与阴，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165059_comment'></div>然则夏侯胜之言何以必应？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165059_comment'></div>曰事固有幸而中者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165059_comment'></div>公孙臣以汉为土德而黄龙当见，黄龙则见矣，而汉乃火德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165059_comment'></div>可以一黄龙而必谓汉为土德耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165059_comment'></div>必不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165059_comment'></div>其所谓眊者蒙矣，胡复多言哉？</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1165059_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《史论》作品：《史论引》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷九。）</span>《史论上》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷九。）</span>《史论中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷九。）</span>《史论下》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1165060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165060?labeling=true' target='_blank'>史论<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>史论引</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165060")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165060'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165060'>史之难其人久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165060_comment'></div>魏、晋、宋、齐、梁、隋间，观其文则亦固当然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165060_comment'></div>所可怪者，唐三百年，文章非三代两汉无敌，史之才宜有如丘明、迁、固辈，而卒无一人可与范晔、陈寿比肩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165060_comment'></div>巢子之书，世称其详且博，然多俚辞俳状，使之纪事，当复甚乎其尝所讥诮者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165060_comment'></div>惟子餗例为差愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165060_comment'></div>吁，其难而然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165060_comment'></div>夫知其难，故思之深，思之深，故有得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165060_comment'></div>因作《史论》三篇。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1165060_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《谏论》作品：《谏论上》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷九。）</span>《谏论下》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　在眉山。任君馈颜真卿（鲁公）《邠州碑》，苏洵作《颜书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134171' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134171' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134171?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颜书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134171")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134171_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134171'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134171'>任君北方来，手出《邠州碑》。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134171'>为是鲁公写，遗我我不辞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134171'>鲁公实豪杰，慷慨忠义姿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134171'>忆在天宝末，变起渔阳师。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134171'>猛士不敢当，儒生横义旗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134171'>感激数十郡，连衡斗羌夷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134171'>新造势尚弱，胡为力未衰。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134171'>用兵竟不胜，叹息真数奇。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134171'>杲兄死常山，烈士泪满颐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134171'>鲁公不死敌，天下皆熙熙。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134171'>奈何不爱死，再使踏鲸鳍。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134171'>公固不畏死，吾实悲当时。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134171'>缅邈念高谊，惜哉我生<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作生我）</span>迟。<div id='poem_sentence_12_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_134171'>近日见异说，不知作者谁。<div id='poem_sentence_13_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_134171'>云公本不死，此事亦已奇<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_134171'>大抵天下心，人人属公思。<div id='poem_sentence_15_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_134171'>加以不死状，慰此苦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_134171", 134171, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>叹悲</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_134171'>我欲哭公墓，莽莽不可知。<div id='poem_sentence_17_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_134171'>爱其平生迹，往往或孑遗。<div id='poem_sentence_18_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_134171'>此字出公手，一见减<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_134171", 134171, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>叹咨</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_134171'>使公不善书，笔墨纷讹痴。<div id='poem_sentence_20_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_134171'>思其平生事，岂忍弃路歧。<div id='poem_sentence_21_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_134171'>况此字颇怪，堂堂伟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_134171", 134171, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>形仪</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_22_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_134171'>骏极有深稳，骨老成支离。<div id='poem_sentence_23_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_134171'>点画乃应和，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_134171", 134171, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>关连</span>不相违。<div id='poem_sentence_24_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_134171'>有如一人身，鼻口耳目眉。<div id='poem_sentence_25_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_134171'>彼此异状貌，各自相结维。<div id='poem_sentence_26_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_134171'>离离天上星，分如不相持。<div id='poem_sentence_27_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_134171'>左右自缀会，或作斗与箕。<div id='poem_sentence_28_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_134171'>骨严体端重，安置无攲危。<div id='poem_sentence_29_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_134171'>篆鼎兀大腹，高屋无弱楣。<div id='poem_sentence_30_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_134171'>古器合尺度，法相<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>应矩规。<div id='poem_sentence_31_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_134171'>想其始下笔，庄重不自卑。<div id='poem_sentence_32_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_134171'>虞柳岂不好，结束烦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_134171", 134171, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>絷羁</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_33_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_134171'>笔法未离俗，庸手尚敢窥。<div id='poem_sentence_34_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_134171'>自我见此字，得纸无所施。<div id='poem_sentence_35_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_134171'>一车会百木，后斤斧<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作斤斧所）</span>易为。<div id='poem_sentence_36_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_134171'>团团彼明月，欲画形终非。<div id='poem_sentence_37_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_134171'>谁知忠义心，馀力尚及斯。<div id='poem_sentence_38_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_134171'>因此数幅纸，使我重<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_134171", 134171, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>叹嘻</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_39_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_134171'></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_134171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_134171'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_134171_0'>⑴ 自注：或云公尸解，虽见杀而实不死。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_134171_0'>⑵ 康熙本、四部丛刊本作物</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_134171_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　苏辙作《缸砚赋》，父洵称之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　苏洵命辙以轼为师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《忆山送人》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。此诗作于本年，但具体时间不详，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_134144' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134144' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134144?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忆山送人</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134144")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134144_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134144'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134144'>少年喜奇迹，落拓鞍马间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134144'>纵目视天下，爱此宇宙宽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134144'>山川看不厌，浩然遂忘还。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134144'>岷峨最先见，晴光厌西川。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134144'>远望未及上，但爱青若鬟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134144'>大雪冬没胫，夏秋多蛇蚖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134144'>乘春乃敢去，匍匐攀孱颜。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134144'>有路不容足，左右号鹿猿。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134144'>阴崖雪如石，迫暖成高澜。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134144'>经日到绝顶，目眩手足颠。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134144'>自恐不得下，抚膺忽长叹。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134144'>坐定聊四顾，风色非人寰。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134144'>仰面嗫云霞，垂手抚百山。<div id='poem_sentence_12_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_134144'>临风弄襟袖，飘若风中仙。<div id='poem_sentence_13_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_134144'>朅来游荆渚，谈笑登峡船。<div id='poem_sentence_14_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_134144'>峡山无平冈，峡水多悍湍。<div id='poem_sentence_15_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_134144'>长风送轻帆，瞥过难详观。<div id='poem_sentence_16_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_134144'>其间最可爱，巫庙十数巅。<div id='poem_sentence_17_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_134144'>耸耸青玉干，折首不见端。<div id='poem_sentence_18_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_134144'>其馀亦诡怪，土老崖石顽。<div id='poem_sentence_19_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_134144'>长江浑浑流，触齧不可拦。<div id='poem_sentence_20_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_134144'>苟非峡山壮，浩浩无隅边。<div id='poem_sentence_21_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_134144'>恐是造物意，特使险且坚。<div id='poem_sentence_22_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_134144'>江山两相值，后世无水患。<div id='poem_sentence_23_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_134144'>水行月馀日，泊舟事征鞍。<div id='poem_sentence_24_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_134144'>烂熳走尘土，耳嚣目眵昏。<div id='poem_sentence_25_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_134144'>中路逢汉水，乱流爱清渊。<div id='poem_sentence_26_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_134144'>道逢尘土<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>客，洗濯无瑕痕。<div id='poem_sentence_27_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_134144'>振鞭入京师，累岁不得官。<div id='poem_sentence_28_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_134144'>悠悠故乡念，中夜成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_134144", 134144, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>惨然</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_29_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_134144'>《五噫》不复留，驰车走轘辕。<div id='poem_sentence_30_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_134144'>自是识嵩岳，荡荡容貌尊。<div id='poem_sentence_31_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_134144'>不入众山列，体如镇中原。<div id='poem_sentence_32_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_134144'>几日至华下，秀色碧照天。<div id='poem_sentence_33_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_134144'>上下数十里，映睫青巑巑。<div id='poem_sentence_34_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_134144'>迤逦见终南，魁岸蟠长安。<div id='poem_sentence_35_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_134144'>一月看三岳，怀抱斗以骞。<div id='poem_sentence_36_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_134144'>渐渐大道尽，倚山栈夤缘。<div id='poem_sentence_37_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_134144'>下瞰不测溪，石齿交戈鋋。<div id='poem_sentence_38_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_134144'>虚阁怖马足，险崖摩吾肩。<div id='poem_sentence_39_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_134144'>左山右绝涧，中如一绳悭。<div id='poem_sentence_40_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_134144'>傲睨驻鞍辔，不妨驱以鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_41_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_134144'>累累<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_134144", 134144, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>斩绝</span>峰，兀不相属联。<div id='poem_sentence_42_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_134144'>背出或逾峻，远骛如争先。<div id='poem_sentence_43_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_134144'>或时度冈岭，下马步险艰<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作■（亻坚），据康熙本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_44_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_134144'>怪事看愈好，勤劬变清欢。<div id='poem_sentence_45_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_134144'>行行上剑阁，勉强踵不前。<div id='poem_sentence_46_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_134144'>矫首望故国，漫漫但青烟。<div id='poem_sentence_47_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_134144'>及下鹿头坂，始见平沙田。<div id='poem_sentence_48_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_134144'>归来顾妻子，壮抱难留连。<div id='poem_sentence_49_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_134144'>遂使十馀载，此路常周旋。<div id='poem_sentence_50_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_134144'>又闻吴越山<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本、四部丛刊本作中）</span>，中<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>明水澄鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_51_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_134144'>百金买骏马，往意不自存。<div id='poem_sentence_52_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_134144'>投身入庐岳，首挹瀑布源。<div id='poem_sentence_53_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_134144'>飞下二千丈<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本、四部丛刊本作尺）</span>，强烈不可干。<div id='poem_sentence_54_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_134144'>馀润散为雨，遍作山中寒。<div id='poem_sentence_55_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_134144'>次入二林寺，遂获高僧言。<div id='poem_sentence_56_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_134144'>问以绝胜境，导我同跻攀。<div id='poem_sentence_57_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_134144'>逾月不倦厌，岩谷行欲殚。<div id='poem_sentence_58_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_134144'>下山复南迈，不知已南虔。<div id='poem_sentence_59_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_134144'>五岭望可见，欲往苦不难。<div id='poem_sentence_60_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_134144'>便拟去登玩，因得窥群蛮。<div id='poem_sentence_61_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_134144'>此意竟不偿，归抱愁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_134144", 134144, "Clauses/125/Comments/0")'>煎煎</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_62_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_134144'>到家不再出，一顿俄十年。<div id='poem_sentence_63_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_134144'>昨闻庐山郡，太守雷君贤。<div id='poem_sentence_64_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_134144'>往求与识面，复见山<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_134144", 134144, "Clauses/131/Comments/0")'>郁蟠</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_65_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_134144'>绝壁横三方，有类大破镮。<div id='poem_sentence_66_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_134144'>包裹五六州，倚之为长垣。<div id='poem_sentence_67_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_134144'>大抵蜀山峭，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_134144", 134144, "Clauses/137/Comments/0")'>巉刻</span>气不温。<div id='poem_sentence_68_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_134144'>不类嵩华背，气象多<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_134144", 134144, "Clauses/139/Comments/0")'>浓繁</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_69_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_70_134144'>吴君颍川秀，六载为蜀官。<div id='poem_sentence_70_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_134144'>簿书苦为累，天鹤囚笼樊。<div id='poem_sentence_71_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_134144'>岷山青城县，峨眉亦南犍。<div id='poem_sentence_72_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_134144'>黎雅又可到，不见宜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_134144", 134144, "Clauses/147/Comments/0")'>悒然</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_73_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_134144'>有如烹脂牛，过眼不得餐。<div id='poem_sentence_74_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_134144'>始谓泛峡去，此约今又愆。<div id='poem_sentence_75_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_134144'>只有东北山，依然送归轩。<div id='poem_sentence_76_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_134144'>他山已不见，此可著意看。<div id='poem_sentence_77_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_134144'></div><div id='poem_sentence_78_134144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_134144'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_27_134144_0'>⑴ 原作上，据康熙本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_51_134144_0'>⑵ 康熙本、四部丛刊本作山</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_134144_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年1月</a>　在眉山。正月，苏洵作《张益州画像记》，颂张方平治蜀之绩。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165078' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165078' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165078?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张益州画像记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165078")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165078_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165078'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165078'>至和元年秋，蜀人传言有寇至边，军夜呼，野无居人，妖言流闻，京师震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165078_comment'></div>方命择帅，天子曰：「毋养乱，毋助变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165078_comment'></div>众言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1165078", 1165078, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>朋兴</span>，朕志自定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165078_comment'></div>外乱不作，变且中起，不可以文令，又不可以武竞，惟朕一二大吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165078_comment'></div>孰为能处兹文武之间，其命往抚朕师」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165078_comment'></div>乃推曰：张公方平其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165078_comment'></div>天子曰：「然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165078_comment'></div>公以亲辞，不可，遂行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165078_comment'></div>冬十一月至蜀，至之日，归屯军，撤守备，使谓郡县：「寇来在吾，无尔劳苦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165078_comment'></div>明年正月朔旦，蜀人相庆如他日，遂以无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165078_comment'></div>又明年正月，相告留公像于净众寺，公不能禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165078_comment'></div>眉阳苏洵言于众曰：「未乱，易治也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165078_comment'></div>既乱，易治也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165078_comment'></div>有乱之萌，无乱之形，是谓将乱，将乱难治，不可以有乱急，亦不可以无乱弛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165078_comment'></div>是惟元年之秋，如器之欹，未坠于地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165078_comment'></div>惟尔张公，安坐于其旁，颜色不变，徐起而正之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165078_comment'></div>既正，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1165078", 1165078, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>油然</span>而退，无矜容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165078_comment'></div>为天子牧小民不倦，惟尔张公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165078_comment'></div>尔繄以生，惟尔父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165078_comment'></div>且公尝为我言：『民无常性，惟上所待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165078_comment'></div>人皆曰蜀人多变，于是待之以待盗贼之意，而绳之以绳盗贼之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165078_comment'></div>重足屏息之民，而以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1165078", 1165078, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>砧斧</span>令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165078_comment'></div>于是民始忍以其父母妻子之所仰赖之身，而弃之于盗贼，故每每大乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165078_comment'></div>夫约之以礼，驱之以法，惟蜀人为易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165078_comment'></div>至于急之而生变，虽齐、鲁亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165078_comment'></div>吾以齐、鲁待蜀人，而蜀人亦自以齐、鲁之人待其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165078_comment'></div>若夫肆意于法律之外，以威劫其民，吾不忍为也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165078_comment'></div>呜呼，爱蜀人之深，待蜀人之厚，自公而前，吾未始见也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165078_comment'></div>皆再拜稽首曰：「然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165078_comment'></div>苏洵又曰：「公之恩在尔心，尔死在尔子孙，其功业在史官，无以像为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165078_comment'></div>且公意不欲，如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165078_comment'></div>皆曰：「公则何事于斯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165078_comment'></div>虽然，于我心有不释焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165078_comment'></div>今夫平居闻一善，必问其人之姓名与乡里之所在，以至于其长短大小美恶之状，甚者或诘其平生所嗜好，以想见其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165078_comment'></div>而史官亦书之于其传，意使天下之人，思之于心，则存之于目；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165078_comment'></div>存之于目，故其思之于心也固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165078_comment'></div>由此观之，像亦不为无助」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165078_comment'></div>苏洵无以诘，遂为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165078_comment'></div>公，南京人，为人慷慨有大节，以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1165078", 1165078, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>度量</span>容天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165078_comment'></div>天下有大事，公可属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165078_comment'></div>系之以诗曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1165078'>天子在祚，岁在甲午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1165078_comment'></div>西人传言，有寇在垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1165078_comment'></div>庭有武臣，谋夫如云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1165078_comment'></div>天子曰嘻，命我张公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1165078_comment'></div>公来自东，旗纛<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1165078", 1165078, "Clauses/134/Comments/0")'>舒舒</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1165078_comment'></div>西人聚观，于巷于涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1165078_comment'></div>谓公暨暨，公来于于。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1165078_comment'></div>公谓西人：「安尔室家，无敢或讹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1165078_comment'></div>讹言不祥，往即尔常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1165078_comment'></div>春尔条桑，秋尔涤场」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1165078_comment'></div>西人稽首，公我父兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1165078_comment'></div>公在西囿，草木<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1165078", 1165078, "Clauses/149/Comments/0")'>骈骈</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1165078_comment'></div>公宴其僚，伐鼓渊渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1165078_comment'></div>西人来观，祝公万年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1165078_comment'></div>有女<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1165078", 1165078, "Clauses/154/Comments/0")'>娟娟</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1165078", 1165078, "Clauses/155/Comments/0")'>闺闼</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1165078", 1165078, "Clauses/155/Comments/1")'>闲闲</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1165078_comment'></div>有童<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1165078", 1165078, "Clauses/156/Comments/0")'>哇哇</span>，亦既能言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1165078_comment'></div>昔公未来，期汝弃捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1165078_comment'></div>禾麻芃芃，仓庚崇崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1165078_comment'></div>嗟我妇子，乐此岁丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1165078_comment'></div>公在朝廷，天子股肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1165078_comment'></div>天子曰归，公敢不承？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1165078_comment'></div>作堂严严，有庑有庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1165078_comment'></div>公像在中，朝服冠缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1165078_comment'></div>西人相告，无敢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1165078", 1165078, "Clauses/173/Comments/0")'>逸荒</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1165078_comment'></div>公归京师，公像在堂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1165078_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年1月</a>　在眉山。正月，苏洵作《苏氏族谱亭记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十四。）</span><div id='poem_1165077' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165077' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165077?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏氏族谱亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165077")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165077_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165077'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165077'>匹夫而化乡人者，吾闻其语矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165077_comment'></div>国有君，邑有大夫，而争讼者诉于其门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165077_comment'></div>乡有庠，里有学，而学道者赴于其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165077_comment'></div>乡人有为不善于室者，父兄辄相与恐曰：「吾夫子无乃闻之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165077_comment'></div>呜呼，彼独何修而得此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165077_comment'></div>意者其积之有本末，而施之有次第耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165077_comment'></div>今吾族人犹有服者不过百人，而岁时蜡社不能相与尽其欢欣爱洽，稍远者至不相往来，是无以示吾乡党邻里也，乃作《苏氏族谱》，立亭于高祖坟茔之西南而刻石焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165077_comment'></div>既而告之曰：「凡在此者，死必赴，冠、娶妻必告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165077_comment'></div>少而孤则老者字之，贫而无归则富者收之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165077_comment'></div>而不然者，族人之所共诮让也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165077_comment'></div>岁正月，相与拜奠于墓下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165077_comment'></div>既奠，列坐于亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165077_comment'></div>其老者顾少者而叹曰：「是不及见吾乡邻风俗之美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165077_comment'></div>自吾少时，见有为不义者，则众相与疾之，如见怪物焉，慄然而不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165077_comment'></div>其后少衰也，犹相与笑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165077_comment'></div>今也则相与安之耳，是起于某人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165077_comment'></div>夫某人者，是乡之望人也，而大乱吾俗焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165077_comment'></div>是故其诱人也速，其为害也深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165077_comment'></div>自斯人之逐其兄之遗孤子而不恤也，而骨肉之恩薄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165077_comment'></div>自斯人之多取其先人之赀田而欺其诸孤子也，而孝悌之行缺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165077_comment'></div>自斯人之为其诸孤子之所讼也，而礼义之节废；<div class='inline'
