id='poem_sentence_20_1165077_comment'></div>自斯人之以妾加其妻也，而嫡庶之别混；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165077_comment'></div>自斯人之笃于声色，而父子杂处，欢哗不严也，而闺门之政乱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165077_comment'></div>自斯人之渎财无厌，惟富者之为贤也，而廉耻之路塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165077_comment'></div>此六行者，吾往时所谓大惭而不容者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165077_comment'></div>今无知之人皆曰：某人何人也，犹且为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165077_comment'></div>其舆马赫奕，婢妾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1165077", 1165077, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>靓丽</span>，足以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1165077", 1165077, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>荡惑</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1165077", 1165077, "Clauses/71/Comments/1")'>里巷</span>之小人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165077_comment'></div>其官爵货力，足以摇动府县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165077_comment'></div>其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1165077", 1165077, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>矫诈</span>修饰言语，足以欺罔君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165077_comment'></div>是州里之大盗也，吾不敢以告乡人，而私以告族人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165077_comment'></div>髣髴于斯人之一节者，愿无过吾门也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165077_comment'></div>予闻之惧，而请书焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165077_comment'></div>老人曰：「书其事而阙其姓名，使他人观之，则不知其为谁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165077_comment'></div>而夫人之观之，则面热内惭，汗出而食不下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165077_comment'></div>且无名之，庶其有悔乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165077_comment'></div>予曰：「然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165077_comment'></div>乃记之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1165077_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='48a798f204c54c07ae6d1444d5197a2d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("48a798f204c54c07ae6d1444d5197a2d");'><span id='48a798f204c54c07ae6d1444d5197a2d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，48岁</div><div id='48a798f204c54c07ae6d1444d5197a2d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　苏洵友人史沆（子凝）卒。先是沆坐事系狱，沦落荆楚，至是卒。洵尝与吴中复书，望恤凝之骨肉。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1eac05bc6113434888ef540dd199ad6b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1eac05bc6113434888ef540dd199ad6b");'><span id='1eac05bc6113434888ef540dd199ad6b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，48岁</div><div id='1eac05bc6113434888ef540dd199ad6b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《我客至止》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134177' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134177' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134177?labeling=true' target='_blank'>我客至止</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134177")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_134177_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134177'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134177'>我客至止，我逆<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作迎）</span>于门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134177'>来升我堂，来饮我樽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134177'>羞鳖不时，詈我不勤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134177'>求我何多，请辞不能。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134177'>客谓主人，唯子我然。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134177'>求子之多，责子之深，期子于贤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_134177_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在眉山。苏洵《木假山记》约作于今年出蜀前。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165081' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165081' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165081?labeling=true' target='_blank'>木假山记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165081")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165081_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165081'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165081'>木之生，或檗而殇，或拱而夭，幸而至于任为栋梁则伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165081_comment'></div>不幸而为风之所拔，水之所漂，或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1165081", 1165081, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>破折</span>，或腐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165081_comment'></div>幸而得不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1165081", 1165081, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>破折</span>，不腐，则为人之所材，而有斧斤之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165081_comment'></div>其最幸者，漂沉汩没于湍沙之间，不知其几百年，而其激射齧食之馀，或髣髴于山者，则为好事者取去，强之以为山，然后可以脱泥沙而远斧斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165081_comment'></div>而荒江之濆，如此者几何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165081_comment'></div>不为好事者所见，而为樵夫野人所薪者，何可胜数！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165081_comment'></div>则其最幸者之中，又有不幸者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165081_comment'></div>予家有三峰，予每思之，则疑其有数存乎其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165081_comment'></div>且其檗而不殇，拱而不夭，任为栋梁而不伐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165081_comment'></div>风拔水漂而不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1165081", 1165081, "Clauses/33/Comments/1")'>破折</span>、不腐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165081_comment'></div>不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1165081", 1165081, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>破折</span>，不腐，而不为人所材，以及于斧斤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165081_comment'></div>出于湍沙之间，而不为樵夫野人之所薪，而后得至乎此，则其理似不偶然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165081_comment'></div>然予之爱之，则非徒爱其似山，而又有所感焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165081_comment'></div>非徒爱之，而又有所敬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165081_comment'></div>予见中峰魁岸<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1165081", 1165081, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>踞肆</span>，意气端重，若有以服其旁之二峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165081_comment'></div>二峰者庄栗<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1165081", 1165081, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>刻峭</span>，凛乎不可犯，虽其势服于中峰，而岌然无阿附意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165081_comment'></div>吁，其可敬也夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165081_comment'></div>其可以有所感也夫<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165081_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1165081'>峭：原脱，据覆宋本、二黄本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1165081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1165081'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_17_1165081_0'>⑴ 《苏老泉先生全集》卷一五。又见《皇朝文鉴》卷七九，《崇古文诀》卷二二，《东莱集注类编观澜文丙集》卷七，《古今事文类聚》前集卷一四，《记纂渊海》卷六，《文编》卷五七，《文翰类选大成》卷一一二，《名世文宗》卷二五，《文章辨体汇选》卷六一○，《古今图书集成》草木典卷六。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1165081_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年3月</a>　约三月，苏洵携二子轼、辙别妻程氏赴京师。轼、辙念母氏抚敎劳苦，思所报之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　苏洵父子离眉山，史经臣（彦辅）送行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='cd6e2f9a725f4a2895c6f8817d8a0e78_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cd6e2f9a725f4a2895c6f8817d8a0e78");'><span id='cd6e2f9a725f4a2895c6f8817d8a0e78_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1059')">1057-1059年</a>，49-51岁</div><div id='cd6e2f9a725f4a2895c6f8817d8a0e78' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　苏洵与二子轼、辙回抵眉山，轼、辙哭涕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　在眉山。苏洵到家月余，上欧阳修书。旋复与修书。作品：《上欧阳内翰第三书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十二。此文为“旋复与修书”所指，“上欧阳修书”所指书简已佚。）</span><div id='poem_1164982' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164982' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164982?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上欧阳内翰第三书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164982")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164982_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164982'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164982'>洵启：昨出京仓惶，遂不得一别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164982_comment'></div>去后数日，始知悔恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164982_comment'></div>盖一时间变出不意，遂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164982", 1164982, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>扰乱</span>如此，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164982", 1164982, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>怏怅</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164982", 1164982, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>怏怅</span>！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164982_comment'></div>不审日来尊履何似？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164982_comment'></div>二子轼、辙竟不免丁忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164982_comment'></div>今已到家月馀，幸且存活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164982_comment'></div>洵道途奔波，老病侵陵，成一翁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164982_comment'></div>自思<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164982", 1164982, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>平生</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164982", 1164982, "Clauses/16/Comments/1")'>羁蹇</span>不遇，年近五十，始识阁下，倾盖晤语，便若<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1164982", 1164982, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>平生</span>，非徒欲援之于贫贱之中，乃与切磨议论，共为不朽之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164982_comment'></div>而事未及成，辄闻此变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164982_comment'></div>孟轲有云：「行或使之，止或尼之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164982_comment'></div>岂信然邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164982_comment'></div>洵离家时，无壮子弟守舍，归来屋庐倒坏，篱落破漏，如逃亡人家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164982_comment'></div>今且谢绝过从，杜门不出，亦稍稍取旧书读之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164982_comment'></div>时有所怀，辄欲就阁下评议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164982_comment'></div>忽惊相去已四千里，思欲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164982", 1164982, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>跂首</span>望见君子之门庭，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164982_comment'></div>所示范公碑文，议及申公事节，最为深厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164982_comment'></div>近试以语人，果无有晓者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164982_comment'></div>每念及此，郁郁不乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164982_comment'></div>阁下虽贤俊满门，足以啸歌俯仰，终日不闷，然至于不言而心相谕者，阁下于谁取之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164982_comment'></div>自蜀至秦，山行一月，自秦至京师，又沙行数千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164982_comment'></div>非有名利之所驱，与凡事之不得已者，孰为来哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164982_comment'></div>洵老矣，恐不能复东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164982_comment'></div>阁下当时赐音问，以慰孤耿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164982_comment'></div>病中无聊，深愧疏略，惟千万珍重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1164982_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　欧阳修致书苏洵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年11月28日</a>　在眉山。十一月庚子（二十八日），苏洵葬夫人程氏于眉州彭山县安镇乡可龙里。洵作祭文。作品：《祭亡妻文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165094' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165094' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165094?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭亡妻文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年11月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165094")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165094_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165094'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165094'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165094_comment'></div>与子相好，相期百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165094_comment'></div>不知中道，弃我而先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165094_comment'></div>我徂京师，不远当还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165094_comment'></div>嗟子之去，曾不须臾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165094_comment'></div>子去不返，我怀永哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165094_comment'></div>反覆求思，意子复回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165094_comment'></div>人亦有言，死生短长，茍皆不欲，尔避谁当？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165094_comment'></div>我独悲子，生逢百殃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165094_comment'></div>有子六人，今谁在堂？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165094_comment'></div>唯轼与辙，仅存不亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165094_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1165094", 1165094, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>咻呴</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1165094", 1165094, "Clauses/23/Comments/1")'>抚摩</span>，既冠既昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165094_comment'></div>教以学问，畏其无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165094_comment'></div>昼夜孜孜，孰知子勤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165094_comment'></div>提携东去，出门迟迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165094_comment'></div>今往不捷，后何以归？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165094_comment'></div>二子告我：母氏劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165094_comment'></div>今不汲汲，奈后将悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165094_comment'></div>大寒酷热，崎岖在外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165094_comment'></div>亦既荐名，试于南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165094_comment'></div>文字炜炜，叹惊群公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165094_comment'></div>二子喜跃，我知母心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165094_comment'></div>非官寔好，要以文称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165094_comment'></div>我今西归，有以藉口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165094_comment'></div>故乡千里，期母寿考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165094_comment'></div>归来空堂，哭不见人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165094_comment'></div>伤心故物，感涕慇勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165094_comment'></div>嗟予老矣，四海一身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165094_comment'></div>自子之逝，内失良朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165094_comment'></div>孤居终日，有过谁箴？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165094_comment'></div>昔予少年，游荡不学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165094_comment'></div>子虽不言，耿耿不乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165094_comment'></div>我知子心，忧我泯没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165094_comment'></div>感叹折节，以至今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165094_comment'></div>呜呼死矣，不可再得！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165094_comment'></div>安镇之乡，里名可龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165094_comment'></div>隶武阳县，在州北东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165094_comment'></div>有蟠其丘，惟子之坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165094_comment'></div>凿为二室，期与子同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165094_comment'></div>骨肉归土，魂无不之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165094_comment'></div>我归旧庐，无不改移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1165094_comment'></div>魂兮未泯，不日来归。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1165094_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　在眉山。史经臣（彦辅）卒，苏洵作祭文；并为之立后，治丧；命子轼往吊其丧。作品：《祭史彦辅文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165092' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165092' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165092?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭史彦辅文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165092")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165092_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165092'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165092'>呜呼彦辅，胡为而然，胡负于天？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165092_comment'></div>谁不寿考，而于彦辅，独啬其年？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165092_comment'></div>谁不富贵，使终贱寒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165092_comment'></div>谁无子孙，诜诜戢戢，满眼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1165092", 1165092, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>蚳蝝</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165092_comment'></div>于天何伤，独爱一孺，使殒其传？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165092_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1165092", 1165092, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>幨幨</span>其帷，其下惟谁，有童未冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165092_comment'></div>彦辅从子，带经而哭，稽颡来前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165092_comment'></div>天高茫茫，恸哭不闻，谁知此冤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165092_comment'></div>辍哭长思，念初结交，康定、宝元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165092_comment'></div>子以气豪，纵横放肆，隼击鹏骞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165092_comment'></div>奇文怪论，卓若无敌，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1165092", 1165092, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>悚怛</span>旁观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165092_comment'></div>忆子大醉，中夜过我，狂歌叫欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165092_comment'></div>予不喜酒，正襟危坐，终夕无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165092_comment'></div>他人窃惊，宜若不合，胡为甚欢？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165092_comment'></div>嗟人何知，吾与彦辅，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1165092", 1165092, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>契心</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1165092", 1165092, "Clauses/43/Comments/1")'>忘颜</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165092_comment'></div>飞腾云霄，无有远迩，我后子先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165092_comment'></div>挤排涧谷，无有崄易，我溺子援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165092_comment'></div>破窗孤灯，冷灰冻席，与子无眠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165092_comment'></div>旅游王城，饮食寤寐，相恃以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165092_comment'></div>庆历丁亥，诏策告罢，予将西辕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165092_comment'></div>慨然有怀，吾亲老矣，甘旨未完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165092_comment'></div>往从南公，奔走乞假，遂至于虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165092_comment'></div>子时亦来，止于临江，系马解鞍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165092_comment'></div>爱弟子凝，仓卒就狱，举家<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1165092", 1165092, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>惊喧</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165092_comment'></div>及秋八月，予将北归，亦既具船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165092_comment'></div>有书晨至，开视惊叫，遂丁大艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165092_comment'></div>故乡万里，泣血行役，敢其生还？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165092_comment'></div>中涂逢子，握手相慰，曰无自残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165092_comment'></div>旅宿魂惊，中夜起行，长江大山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165092_comment'></div>前呼后应，告我无恐，相从入关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165092_comment'></div>归来几何，子以病废，手足若挛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1165092_comment'></div>我嘉子心，壮若铁石，益固而坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1165092_comment'></div>瞋目大呼，屋瓦为落，闻者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1165092", 1165092, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>竦肩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1165092_comment'></div>子凝之丧，大临呕血，伤心破肝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1165092_comment'></div>我游京师，强起来饯，相顾留连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1165092_comment'></div>我还自东，二子丧母，归怀辛酸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1165092_comment'></div>子病告革，奔走往问，医云已难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1165092_comment'></div>问以后事，口不能语，悲来塞咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1165092_comment'></div>遗文坠稿，为子收拾，以葺以编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1165092_comment'></div>我知不朽，千载之后，子名长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1165092_comment'></div>呜呼彦辅，天实丧之，予哭寝门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1165092_comment'></div>白发班班，疾病来加，卧不能奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1165092_comment'></div>哭书此文，命轼往奠，以慰斯魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1165092_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1165092_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　在眉山。苏洵与吴中复书。作品：《与吴殿院书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1164994' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164994' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164994?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与吴殿院书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164994")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164994_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164994'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164994'>洵启：京师会遇，殊未及从容，属家有变，故仓遽西走，遂不得奉别，怏怅不可胜言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164994_comment'></div>向每见君侯，谈论辄尽欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164994_comment'></div>而在京师逾年，相见至少，诚恐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164994", 1164994, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>宪官</span>职重，是以不敢数数自通，然亦老懒不出之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164994_comment'></div>及今相去数千里，求复一见，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164994_comment'></div>曩曾议及故友史沆骨肉沦落荆楚间，慨然太息，有收恤之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164994_comment'></div>沆有兄经臣者，虽卧病，而志气卓然，以豪杰称乡里，使得摄尺寸之柄，当不卤莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164994_comment'></div>常以为沆死而有经臣者在，或万一能有所雪，今不幸亦已死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164994_comment'></div>追思沆平生孤直不遇，而经臣亦以刚见废，又皆以无后死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164994_comment'></div>当其生时，举世莫不雠疾，惟君侯一人独为哀闵，而数年间兄弟相继沦丧，使仁人之心不克少施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164994_comment'></div>呜呼，岂其命之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164994", 1164994, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>穷薄</span>至于此耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164994_comment'></div>经臣死，家无一人，后事所属办于朋友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164994_comment'></div>今其家遗孤骨肉存者，独沆有弱女在襄州耳，君侯尚可以庇之，使无失所否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164994_comment'></div>阻远未能一一，伏惟裁悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164994_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164994_comment'></div>洵白。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1164994_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《老翁井铭》，欲居老翁井。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165082' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165082' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165082?labeling=true' target='_blank'>老翁井铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165082")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165082_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165082'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165082'>丁酉岁，余卜葬亡妻，得武阳安镇之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165082_comment'></div>山之所从来甚高大壮伟，其末分而为两股，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1165082", 1165082, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>回转</span>环抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165082_comment'></div>有泉坌然出于两山之间而北附，右股之下畜为大井，可以日饮百馀家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165082_comment'></div>卜者曰吉，是其葬书为神之居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165082_comment'></div>盖水之行常与山俱，山止而泉冽，则山之精气势力自远而至者，皆畜于此而不去，是以可葬无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165082_comment'></div>他日乃问泉旁之民，皆曰是为老翁井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165082_comment'></div>问其所以为名之由，曰：「往岁十年，山空月明，天地<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1165082", 1165082, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>开霁</span>，则常有老人苍颜白发，偃息于泉上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165082_comment'></div>就之，则隐而入于泉，莫可见」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165082_comment'></div>盖其相传以为如此者久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165082_comment'></div>因为作亭于其上，又甃石以御水潦之暴，而往往优游其间，酌泉而饮之，以庶几得见所谓老翁者，以知其信否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165082_comment'></div>然余又闵其老于荒榛岩石之间，千岁而莫知也，今乃始遇我而后得传于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165082_comment'></div>遂为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1165082'>山起东北，翼为南西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165082_comment'></div>涓涓斯泉，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1165082", 1165082, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>坌溢</span>以㳽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165082_comment'></div>敛以为井，可饮万夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165082_comment'></div>汲者告吾，有叟于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165082_comment'></div>里无斯人，将此谓谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165082_comment'></div>山空寂寥，或啸而嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165082_comment'></div>更千万年，自洁自好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165082_comment'></div>谁其知之，乃讫遇我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165082_comment'></div>惟我与尔，将遂不泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165082_comment'></div>无溢无竭，以永千祀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1165082_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《老翁井》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》此诗亦题苏轼作，见《苏轼诗集》卷五十。）</span><div id='poem_250049' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_250049' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/250049?labeling=true' target='_blank'>老翁井<span class='inlineComment2'>（他集互见诗）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_250049")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_250049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_250049'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_250049'>井中老翁误年华，白沙翠石公之家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_250049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_250049'>公来无踪去无迹，井面团团水生花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_250049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_250049'>翁今与世两何与，无事纷纷惊牧竖。<div id='poem_sentence_2_250049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_250049'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_250049", 250049, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>改颜</span>易服与世同，无使世人知有翁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_250049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_250049'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_250049_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年10月</a>　十月，苏洵得雷简夫（太简）书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　朝廷召苏洵试策论舍人院。十一月五日，眉州录到中书劄子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年12月1日</a>　在眉山。十二月一日，苏洵以病辞赴京师试策论，上仁宗皇帝书，论天下事。作品：《上皇帝书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1164972' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164972' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164972?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上皇帝书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年12月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164972")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164972_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164972'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164972'>嘉祐三年十二月一日，眉州布衣臣苏洵谨顿首再拜，冒万死上书皇帝阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164972_comment'></div>臣前月五日，蒙本州录到中书劄子，连牒臣：以两制议上翰林学士欧阳修奏臣所著《权书》、《衡论》、《几策》二十篇，乞赐甄录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164972_comment'></div>陛下过听，召臣试策论舍人院，仍令本州发遣臣赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164972_comment'></div>臣本田野匹夫，名姓不登于州闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164972_comment'></div>今一旦卒然被召，实不知其所以自通于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164972_comment'></div>承命<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>悸恐</span>，不知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164972_comment'></div>以陛下躬至圣之资，又有群公卿之贤，与天下士大夫之众，如臣等辈，固宜不少，有臣无臣，不加损益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164972_comment'></div>臣不幸有负薪之疾，不能奔走道路，以副陛下搜扬之心，忧惶负罪，无所容处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164972_comment'></div>臣本凡才，无路自进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164972_comment'></div>当少年时，亦尝欲侥倖于陛下之科举，有司以为不肖，辄以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>摈落</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164972_comment'></div>盖退而处者，十有馀年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164972_comment'></div>今虽欲勉强扶病戮力，亦自知其疏拙，终不能合有司之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164972_comment'></div>恐重得罪，以辱明诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164972_comment'></div>且陛下所为千里而召臣者，其意以臣为能有所发明，以庶几有补于圣政之万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164972_comment'></div>而臣之所以自结发读书，至于今兹，犬马之齿几已五十，而犹未敢废者，其意亦欲效尺寸于当时，以快平生之志耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164972_comment'></div>今虽未能奔伏阙下，以累有司，而犹不忍默默卒无一言而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164972_comment'></div>天下之事，其深远切至者，臣自惟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>疏贱</span>，未敢遽言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164972_comment'></div>而其近而易行，浅而易见者，谨条为十通，以塞明诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164972_comment'></div>其一曰：臣闻利之所在，天下趋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164972_comment'></div>是故千金之子欲有所为，则百家之市无宁居者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164972_comment'></div>古之圣人，执其大利之权，以奔走天下，意有所向，则天下争先为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164972_comment'></div>今陛下有奔走天下之权而不能用，何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164972_comment'></div>古者赏一人而天下劝，今陛下增秩拜官，动以千计，其人皆以为己所自致，而不知戮力以报上之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164972_comment'></div>至于临事，谁当效用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164972_comment'></div>此由陛下轻用其爵禄，使天下之士积日持久而得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164972_comment'></div>譬如佣力之人，计工而受直，虽与之千万，岂知德其主哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164972_comment'></div>是以虽有能者，亦无所施，以为谨守绳墨，足以自致高位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164972_comment'></div>官吏繁多，溢于局外，使陛下皇皇汲汲求以处之，而不暇择其贤不肖，以病陛下之民，而耗竭大司农之钱谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164972_comment'></div>此议者所欲去而未得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164972_comment'></div>臣窃思之，盖今制天下之吏，自州县令录幕职而改京官者，皆未得其术，是以若此纷纷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164972_comment'></div>今虽多其举官而远其考，重其举官之罪，此适足以隔贤者而容不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164972_comment'></div>且天下无事，虽庸人皆足以无过，一旦改官，无所不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164972_comment'></div>彼其举者曰：「此廉吏，此能吏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164972_comment'></div>朝廷不知其所以为廉与能也，幸而未有败事，则长为廉与能矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164972_comment'></div>虽重其罪，未见有益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164972_comment'></div>上下相蒙，请托公行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164972_comment'></div>涖官六七考，求举主五六人，此谁不能者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164972_comment'></div>臣愚以为，举人者当使明著其迹曰：某人廉吏也，尝有某事以知其廉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164972_comment'></div>某人能吏也，尝有某事以知其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164972_comment'></div>虽不必有非常之功，而皆有可纪之状，其特曰廉能而已者不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164972_comment'></div>如此，则夫庸人虽无罪而不足称者不得入其间，老于州县，不足甚惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164972_comment'></div>而天下之吏必皆务为可称之功，与民兴利除害，惟恐不出诸己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164972_comment'></div>此古之圣人所以驱天下之人，而使争为善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164972_comment'></div>有功而赏，有罪而罚，其实一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164972_comment'></div>今降官罢任者，必奏曰某人有某罪，其罪当然，然后朝廷举而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164972_comment'></div>今若不著其所犯之由，而特曰此不才贪吏也，则朝廷安肯以空言而加之罪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164972_comment'></div>今又何独至于改官而听其空言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164972_comment'></div>是不思之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164972_comment'></div>或以为如此，则天下之吏，务为可称，用意过当，生事以为己功，渐不可长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164972_comment'></div>臣以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164972_comment'></div>盖圣人必观天下之势而为之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164972_comment'></div>方天下初定，民厌劳役，则圣人务为因循之政与之休息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164972_comment'></div>及其久安而无变，则必有不振之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1164972_comment'></div>是以圣人破其茍且之心，而作其怠惰之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1164972_comment'></div>汉之元、成，惟不知此，以至于乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1164972_comment'></div>今天下少惰矣，宜有以激发其心，使踊跃于功名，以变其俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1164972_comment'></div>况乎冗官纷纭如此，不知所以节之，而又何疑于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1164972_comment'></div>且陛下与天下之士相期于功名，而毋茍得，此待之至深也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1164972_comment'></div>若其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/181/Comments/0")'>宏才大略</span>，不乐于小官而无闻焉者，使两制得以非常举之，此天下亦不过几人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1164972_comment'></div>吏之有过而不得迁者，亦使得以功赎，如此，亦以示陛下之有所推恩，而不惟艰之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1164972_comment'></div>其二曰：臣闻古者之制爵禄，必皆孝弟忠信，修絜博习，闻于乡党，而达于朝廷以得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1164972_comment'></div>及其后世不然，曲艺小数，皆可以进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1164972_comment'></div>然其得之也，犹有以取之，其弊不若今之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1164972_comment'></div>今之用人最无谓者，其所谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/203/Comments/0")'>任子</span>乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1164972_comment'></div>因其父兄之资以得大官，而又任其子弟，子将复任其孙，孙又任其子，是不学而得者尝无穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1164972_comment'></div>夫得之也易，则其失之也不甚惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1164972_comment'></div>以不学之人，而居不甚惜之官，其视民如草芥也固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1164972_comment'></div>朝廷自近年始有意于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/214/Comments/0")'>裁节</span>，然皆知损之而未得其所损，此所谓制其末而不穷其源，见其粗而未识其精，侥倖之风少衰而犹在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1164972_comment'></div>夫圣人之举事，不惟曰利而已，必将有以大服天下之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1164972_comment'></div>今欲有所去也，必使天下知其所以去之之说，故虽尽去而无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1164972_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1164972_comment'></div>恃其说明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1164972_comment'></div>夫所谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/227/Comments/0")'>任子</span>者，亦犹曰信其父兄而用其子弟云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1164972_comment'></div>彼其父兄固学而得之也，学者任人，不学者任于人，此易晓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1164972_comment'></div>今之制，茍幸而其官至于可任者，举使任之，不问其始之何从而得之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1164972_comment'></div>且彼任于人不暇，又安能任人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1164972_comment'></div>此犹借资之人，而欲从之丐贷，不已难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1164972_comment'></div>臣愚以为父兄之所任而得官者，虽至正郎，宜皆不听<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/244/Comments/0")'>任子</span>弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1164972_comment'></div>惟其能自修饰，而越录躐次，以至于清显者乃听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1164972_comment'></div>如此，则天下之冗官必大衰少，而公卿之后皆奋志为学，不待父兄之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1164972_comment'></div>其任而得官者，知后不得复任其子弟，亦当勉强，不肯终老自弃于庸人，此其为益岂特一二而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1164972_comment'></div>其三曰：臣闻自设官以来皆有考绩之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1164972_comment'></div>周室既亡，其法废绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1164972_comment'></div>自京房建考课之议，其后终不能行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1164972_comment'></div>夫有官必有课，有课必有赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1164972_comment'></div>有官而无课，是无官也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1164972_comment'></div>有课而无赏罚，是无课也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1164972_comment'></div>无官无课，而欲求天下之大治，臣不识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1164972_comment'></div>然更历千载而终莫之行，行之则益以纷乱，而终不可考，其故何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1164972_comment'></div>天下之吏不可以胜考，今欲人人而课之，必使入于九等之中，此宜其颠倒错谬而不若无之为便也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1164972_comment'></div>臣观自昔行考课者，皆不得其术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1164972_comment'></div>盖天下之官皆有所属之长，有功有罪，其长皆得以举刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1164972_comment'></div>如必人人而课之于朝廷，则其长为将安用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1164972_comment'></div>惟其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_93_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/287/Comments/0")'>大吏</span>无所属，而莫为之长也，则课之所宜加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1164972_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1164972_comment'></div>其位尊，故课一人而其下皆可以整齐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1164972_comment'></div>其数少，故可以尽其能否而不谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1164972_comment'></div>今天下所以不大治者，守令丞尉贤不肖混淆，而莫之辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1164972_comment'></div>夫守令丞尉贤不肖之不辨，其咎在职司之不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1164972_comment'></div>职司之不明，其咎在无所属而莫为之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1164972_comment'></div>陛下以无所属之官，而寄之以一路，其贤不肖当使谁察之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1164972_comment'></div>古之考绩者，皆从司会而至于天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1164972_comment'></div>古之司会，即今之尚书，尚书既废，惟御史可以总察中外之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1164972_comment'></div>臣愚以为可使朝臣议定职司考课之法，而于御史台别立考课之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1164972_comment'></div>中丞举其大纲，而属官之中，选强明者一人，以专治其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1164972_comment'></div>以举刺多者为上，以举刺少者为中，以无所举刺者为下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1164972_comment'></div>因其罢归而奏其治要，使朝廷有以为之赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1164972_comment'></div>其非常之功，不可掩之罪，又当特有以偿之，使职司知有所惩劝，则其下守令丞尉不容复有所依违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1164972_comment'></div>而其所课者又不过数十人，足以求得其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1164972_comment'></div>此所谓用力少而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_109_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/329/Comments/0")'>成功</span>多，法无便于此者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1164972_comment'></div>今天下号为太平，其实远方之民穷困已甚，其咎皆在职司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1164972_comment'></div>臣不敢尽言，陛下试加采访，乃知臣言之不妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1164972_comment'></div>其四曰：臣闻古有诸侯，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/339/Comments/0")'>臣妾</span>其境内，而卿大夫之家亦各有臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1164972_comment'></div>陪臣之事其君，如其君之事天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1164972_comment'></div>此无他，其一境之内，所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_114_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/345/Comments/0")'>生杀予夺</span>，富贵贫贱者，皆自我制之，此固有以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_114_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/348/Comments/0")'>臣妾</span>之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1164972_comment'></div>其后诸侯虽废，而自汉至唐，犹有相君之势，何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1164972_comment'></div>其署置辟举之权，犹足以臣之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1164972_comment'></div>是故太守、刺史坐于堂上，州县之吏拜于堂下，虽奔走顿伏，其谁曰不然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1164972_comment'></div>自太祖受命，收天下之尊，归之京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1164972_comment'></div>一命以上皆上所自署，而大司农衣食之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1164972_comment'></div>自宰相至于州县吏，虽贵贱相去甚远，而其实皆所与比肩而事主耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1164972_comment'></div>是以百馀年间，天下不知有权臣之威，而太守、刺史犹用汉唐之制，使州县之吏事之如事君之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1164972_comment'></div>皆受天子之爵，皆食天子之禄，不知其何以臣之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1164972_comment'></div>小吏之于大官，不忧其有所不从，惟恐其从之过耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1164972_comment'></div>今天下以贵相高，以贱相谄，奈何使州县之吏，趋走于太守之庭，不啻若仆妾，唯唯不给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1164972_comment'></div>故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_125_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/383/Comments/0")'>大吏</span>常恣行不忌其下，而小吏不能正，以至于曲随谄事，助以为虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1164972_comment'></div>其能中立而不挠者，固已难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1164972_comment'></div>此不足怪，其势固使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1164972_comment'></div>夫州县之吏，位卑而禄薄，去于民最近，而易以为奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1164972_comment'></div>朝廷所恃以制之者，特以厉其廉隅，全其节概，而养其气，使知有所耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1164972_comment'></div>且必有异材焉，后将以为公卿，而安可薄哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1164972_comment'></div>其尤不可者，今以县令从州县之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1164972_comment'></div>夫县令官虽卑，其所负一县之责，与京朝官知县等耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1164972_comment'></div>其吏胥人民，习知其官长之拜伏于太守之庭，如是之不威也，故轻之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1164972_comment'></div>轻之，故易为奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1164972_comment'></div>此县令之所以为难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1164972_comment'></div>臣愚以为州县之吏事太守，可恭逊<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_136_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/416/Comments/0")'>卑抑</span>，不敢抗而已，不至于通名赞拜、趋走其下风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1164972_comment'></div>所以全士大夫之节，且以儆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_137_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/420/Comments/0")'>大吏</span>之不法者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1164972_comment'></div>其五曰：臣闻为天下者，必有所不可窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1164972_comment'></div>是以天下有急，不求其素所不用之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1164972_comment'></div>使天下不能幸其仓卒，而取其禄位，惟圣人为能然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1164972_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1164972_comment'></div>其素所用者，缓急足以使也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1164972_comment'></div>临事而取者，亦不足用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1164972_comment'></div>传曰：「宽则宠名誉之人，急则用介胄之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1164972_comment'></div>今者所用非所养，所养非所用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1164972_comment'></div>国家用兵之时，购方略，设武举，使天下屠沽健儿皆能徒手<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_146_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/442/Comments/0")'>攫取</span>陛下之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1164972_comment'></div>而兵休之日，虽有超世之才，而惜斗升之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1164972_comment'></div>臣恐天下有以窥朝廷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1164972_comment'></div>今之任为将帅，卒有急难而可使者，谁也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1164972_comment'></div>陛下之老将，曩之所谓战胜而善守者，今亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1164972_comment'></div>臣愚以为可复武举，而为之新制，以革其旧弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1164972_comment'></div>且昔之所谓武举者盖疏矣，其以弓马得者，不过挽强引重，市井之粗材；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1164972_comment'></div>而以策试中者，亦皆记录章句，区区无用之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1164972_comment'></div>又其取人太多，天下之知兵者不宜如此之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1164972_comment'></div>而待之又甚轻，其第下者不免于隶役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1164972_comment'></div>故其所得皆贪污无行之徒，豪杰之士耻不忍就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1164972_comment'></div>宜因贡士之岁，使两制各得举其所闻，有司试其可者，而陛下亲策之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1164972_comment'></div>权略之外，便于弓马，可以出入险阻，勇而有谋者，不过取一二人，待以不次之位，试以守边之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1164972_comment'></div>文有制科，武有武举，陛下欲得将相，于此乎取之，十人之中，岂无一二？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1164972_comment'></div>斯亦足以济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1164972_comment'></div>其六曰：臣闻法不足以制天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1164972_comment'></div>以法而制天下，法之所不及，天下斯欺之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1164972_comment'></div>且法必有所不及也，先王知其有所不及，是故存其大略，而济之以至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1164972_comment'></div>使天下之所以不吾欺者，未必皆吾法之所能禁，亦其中有所不忍而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1164972_comment'></div>人君御其大臣，不可以用法，如其左右大臣而必待法而后能御也，则其疏远小吏当复何以哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1164972_comment'></div>以天下之大而无可信之人，则国不足以为国矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1164972_comment'></div>臣观今两制以上，非无贤俊之士，然皆奉法供职无过而已，莫肯于绳墨之外为陛下深思远虑，有所建明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1164972_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1164972_comment'></div>陛下待之于绳墨之内也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1164972_comment'></div>臣请得举其一二以言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1164972_comment'></div>夫两府与两制，宜使日夜交于门，以讲论当世之务，且以习知其为人，临事授任，以不失其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1164972_comment'></div>今法不可以相往来，意将以杜其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_172_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/520/Comments/0")'>告谒</span>之私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1164972_comment'></div>君臣之道不同，人臣惟自防，人君惟无防之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1164972_comment'></div>是以欢欣相接而无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1164972_comment'></div>以两府、两制为可信邪，当无所请属，以为不可信邪，彼何患无所致其私意，安在其相往来邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1164972_comment'></div>今两制知举，不免用封弥誊录，既奏而下御史，亲往莅之，凛凛如鞠大狱，使不知谁人之辞，又何其甚也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1164972_comment'></div>臣愚以为如此之类，一切撤去，彼稍有知，宜不忍负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1164972_comment'></div>若其犹有所欺也，则亦天下之不才无耻者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1164972_comment'></div>陛下赫然震威，诛一二人，可以使天下奸吏重足而立，想闻朝廷之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1164972_comment'></div>亦必有倜傥非常之才，为陛下用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1164972_comment'></div>其七曰：臣闻为天下者可以名器授人，而不可以名器许人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1164972_comment'></div>人之不可以一日而知也久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1164972_comment'></div>国家以科举取人，四方之来者如市，一旦使有司第之，此固非真知其才之高下大小也，特以为姑收之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1164972_comment'></div>将试之为政，而观其悠久，则必有大异不然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1164972_comment'></div>今进士三人之中，释褐之日，天下望为卿相，不及十年，未有不为两制者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1164972_comment'></div>且彼以其一日之长，而擅终身之富贵，举而归之，如有所负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1164972_comment'></div>如此，则虽天下之美才，亦或怠而不修；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1164972_comment'></div>其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_188_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/573/Comments/0")'>率意</span>恣行者，人亦望风畏之，不敢按。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1164972_comment'></div>此何为者也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1164972_comment'></div>且又有甚不便者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1164972_comment'></div>先王制其天下，尊尊相高，贵贵相承，使天下仰视朝廷之尊，如太山乔岳，非攀援所能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1164972_comment'></div>茍非有大功与出群之才，则不可以轻得其高位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1164972_comment'></div>是故天下知有所忌，而不敢觊觎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1164972_comment'></div>今五尺童子，斐然皆有意于公卿，得之则不知愧，不得则怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1164972_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1164972_comment'></div>彼习知其一旦之可以侥倖而无难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1164972_comment'></div>如此，则匹夫轻朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1164972_comment'></div>臣愚以为三人之中，茍优与一官，足以报其一日之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1164972_comment'></div>馆阁台省，非举不入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1164972_comment'></div>彼果不才者也，其安以入为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1164972_comment'></div>彼果才者也，其何患无所举？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1164972_comment'></div>此非独以爱惜名器，将以重朝廷耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1164972_comment'></div>其八曰：臣闻古者敌国相观，不观于其山川之险、士马之众，相观于人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1164972_comment'></div>高山大江，必有猛兽怪物，时见其威，故人不敢亵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1164972_comment'></div>夫不必战胜而后服也，使之常有所忌，而不敢发；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1164972_comment'></div>使吾常有所恃，而无所怯耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1164972_comment'></div>今以中国之大，使夷狄视之不甚畏，敢有烦言以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_207_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/622/Comments/0")'>渎乱</span>吾听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1164972_comment'></div>此其心不有所窥，其安能如此之无畏也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1164972_comment'></div>敌国有事，相待以将；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1164972_comment'></div>无事，相观以使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1164972_comment'></div>今之所谓使者亦轻矣，曰此人也，为此官也，则以为此使也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1164972_comment'></div>今岁以某，来岁当以某，又来岁当以某，如县令署役，必均而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1164972_comment'></div>人之才固有所短，而不可强；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1164972_comment'></div>其专对、捷给、勇敢，又非可以学致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1164972_comment'></div>今必使强之，彼有仓惶失次，为夷狄笑而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1164972_comment'></div>古者，大夫出疆，有可以安国家、利社稷则专之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1164972_comment'></div>今法令太密，使小吏执简记其旁，一摇足，辄随而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1164972_comment'></div>虽有奇才辨士，亦安所效用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1164972_comment'></div>彼夷狄观之，以为樽俎谈燕之间，尚不能办，军旅之际，固宜其无人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1164972_comment'></div>如此，将何以破其奸谋，而折其骄气哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1164972_comment'></div>臣愚以为奉使宜有常人，惟其可者，而不必均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1164972_comment'></div>彼其不能者，陛下责之以文学政事，不必强之于言语之间，以败吾事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1164972_comment'></div>而亦稍宽其法，使得有所施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1164972_comment'></div>且今世之患，以奉使为艰危，故必均而后可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1164972_comment'></div>陛下平世使人，而皆得以辞免；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1164972_comment'></div>后有缓急，使之出入死地，将皆逃邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1164972_comment'></div>此臣又非独为出使而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1164972_comment'></div>其九曰：臣闻刑之有赦，其来远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1164972_comment'></div>周制八议，有可赦之人而无可赦之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1164972_comment'></div>自三代之衰，始闻有肆赦之令，然皆因天下有非常之事，凶荒流离之后，盗贼垢污之馀，于是有以沛然洗濯于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1164972_comment'></div>而犹不若今之因郊而赦，使天下之凶民，可以逆知而侥倖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1164972_comment'></div>平时小民畏法，不敢趑趄，当郊之岁，盗贼公行，罪人满狱，为天下者将何利于此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1164972_comment'></div>而又糜散帑廪，以赏无用冗杂之兵，一经大礼，费以万亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1164972_comment'></div>赋敛之不轻，民之不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_234_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/705/Comments/0")'>聊生</span>，皆此之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1164972_comment'></div>以陛下节用爱民，非不欲去此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1164972_comment'></div>顾以为所从来久远，恐一旦去之，天下必以为少恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1164972_comment'></div>而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_237_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/712/Comments/0")'>凶豪</span>无赖之兵，或因以为词而生乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1164972_comment'></div>此其所以重改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1164972_comment'></div>盖事有不可改而遂不改者，其忧必深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1164972_comment'></div>改之，则其祸必速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1164972_comment'></div>惟其不失推恩，而有以救天下之弊者，臣愚以为先郊之岁，可因事为词，特发大号，如郊之赦与军士之赐，且告之曰：「吾于天下非有惜乎推恩也，惟是凶残之民，知吾当赦，辄以犯法，以贼害吾良民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1164972_comment'></div>今而后赦不于郊之岁，以为常制」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1164972_comment'></div>天下之人喜乎非郊之岁而得郊之赏也，何暇虑其后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1164972_comment'></div>其后四五年而行之，七八年而行之，又从而尽去之，天下晏然不知，而日以远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1164972_comment'></div>且此出于五代之后、兵荒之间，所以姑息天下而安反侧耳，后之人相承而不能去，以至于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1164972_comment'></div>法令明具，四方无虞，何畏而不改？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1164972_comment'></div>今不为之计，使奸人猾吏养为盗贼，而复取<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_247_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/749/Comments/0")'>租赋</span>以啖骄兵，乘之以饥馑，鲜不及乱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1164972_comment'></div>当此之时，欲为之计，其犹有及乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1164972_comment'></div>其十曰：臣闻古者所以采庶人之议，为其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_249_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/757/Comments/0")'>疏贱</span>而无嫌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1164972_comment'></div>不知爵禄之可爱，故其言公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1164972_comment'></div>不知君威之可畏，故其言直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1164972_comment'></div>今臣幸而未立于陛下之朝，无所爱惜顾念于其心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1164972_comment'></div>是以天下之事，陛下之诸臣所不敢尽言者，臣请得以僭言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1164972_comment'></div>陛下擢用俊贤，思致太平，今几年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1164972_comment'></div>事垂立而辄废，功未成而旋去，陛下知其所由乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1164972_comment'></div>陛下知其所由，则今之在位者，皆足以有立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1164972_comment'></div>若犹未也，虽得贤臣千万，天下终不可为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1164972_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1164972_comment'></div>小人之根未去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1164972_comment'></div>陛下遇士大夫有礼，凡在位者不敢用亵狎戏嫚，以求<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_260_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/783/Comments/0")'>亲媚</span>于陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1164972_comment'></div>而谗言邪谋之所由至于朝廷者，天下之人皆以为陛下不疏远宦官之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1164972_comment'></div>陛下特以为耳目玩弄之臣，而不知其阴贼险诈，为害最大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1164972_comment'></div>天下之小人，无由至于陛下之前，故皆通于宦官，珠玉锦绣所以为赂者络绎于道，以间关龃龉贤人之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1164972_comment'></div>陛下纵不听用，而大臣常有所顾忌，以不得尽其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1164972_comment'></div>臣故曰：小人之根未去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1164972_comment'></div>窃闻之道路，陛下将有意去而疏之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1164972_comment'></div>若如所言，则天下之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1164972_comment'></div>然臣方以为忧，而未敢贺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1164972_comment'></div>古之小人有为君子之所抑，而反激为天下之祸者，臣每痛伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1164972_comment'></div>盖东汉之衰，宦官用事，阳球为司隶校尉，发愤诛王甫等数人，磔其尸于道中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1164972_comment'></div>常侍曹节过而见之，遂奏诛阳球，而宦官之用事，过于王甫之未诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1164972_comment'></div>其后窦武、何进又欲去之，而反以遇害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1164972_comment'></div>故汉之衰至于扫地而不可救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1164972_comment'></div>夫君子之去小人，惟能尽去，乃无后患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1164972_comment'></div>惟陛下思宗庙社稷之重，与天下之可畏，既去之，又去之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1164972_comment'></div>既疏之，又疏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1164972_comment'></div>刀锯之馀必无忠良，纵有区区之小节，不过<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_277_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/831/Comments/0")'>闱闼</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_277_1164972", 1164972, "Clauses/831/Comments/1")'>扫洒</span>之勤，无益于事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1164972_comment'></div>惟能务绝其权，使朝廷清明，而忠言嘉谟易以入，则天下无事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1164972_comment'></div>惟陛下无使为臣之所料，而后世以臣为知言，不胜大愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1164972_comment'></div>曩臣所著二十篇，略言当世之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1164972_comment'></div>陛下虽以此召臣，然臣观朝廷之意，特以其文采词致稍有可嘉，而未必其言之可用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1164972_comment'></div>天下无事，臣每每狂言，以迂阔为世笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1164972_comment'></div>然臣以为必将有时而不迂阔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1164972_comment'></div>贾谊之策不用于孝文之时，而使主父偃之徒得其馀论，而施之于孝武之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1164972_comment'></div>夫施之于孝武之世，固不如用之于孝文之时之易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1164972_comment'></div>臣虽不及古人，惟陛下不以一布衣之言而忽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1164972_comment'></div>不胜越次忧国之心，效其所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1164972_comment'></div>且非陛下召臣，臣言无以至于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1164972_comment'></div>今老矣，恐后无由复言，故云云之多至于此也，惟陛下宽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1164972_comment'></div>臣洵诚惶诚惧，顿首顿首，谨书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_290_1164972_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　在眉山。岁末，苏洵答雷简夫（太简）书。作品：《答雷太简书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1164992' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164992' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164992?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答雷太简书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164992")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164992_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164992'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164992'>太简足下：前月辱书，承谕朝廷将有召命，且教以东行应诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164992_comment'></div>旋属郡有符，亦以此见遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164992_comment'></div>承命自笑，恐不足以当，遂以疾辞，不果行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164992_comment'></div>计太简亦已知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164992_comment'></div>仆已老矣，固非求仕者，亦非固求不仕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164992_comment'></div>自以閒居田野之中，鱼稻蔬笋之资，足以养生自乐，俯仰世俗之间，窃观当世之太平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164992_comment'></div>其文章议论，亦可以自足于一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164992_comment'></div>何苦乃以衰病之身，委曲以就有司之权衡，以自取轻笑哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164992_comment'></div>然此可为太简道，不可与流俗人言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164992_comment'></div>向者《权书》、《衡论》、《几策》，皆仆閒居之所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164992_comment'></div>其间虽多言今世之事，亦不自求出之于世，乃欧阳永叔以为可进而进之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164992_comment'></div>茍朝廷以为其言之可信，则何所事试？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164992_comment'></div>苟不信其平居之所云，而其一日仓卒之言又何足信邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164992_comment'></div>恐复不信，祇以为笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164992_comment'></div>久居閒处，终岁幸无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164992_comment'></div>昨为州郡所发遣，徒益不乐尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164992_comment'></div>杨旻至今未归，未得所惠书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164992_comment'></div>岁晚，京师寒甚，惟多爱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1164992_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　在眉山。岁末，苏洵与梅尧臣（圣俞）书。作品：《与梅圣俞书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1164991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164991?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与梅圣俞书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164991")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164991'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164991'>圣俞足下：揆间忽复岁晚，昨九月中尝发书，计已达左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164991_comment'></div>洵閒居经岁，益知无事之乐，旧病渐复散去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164991_comment'></div>独恨沦废山林，不得圣俞、永叔相与谈笑，深以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164991", 1164991, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>嗟惋</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164991_comment'></div>自离京师，行已二年，不意朝廷尚未见遗，以其不肖之文犹有可者，前月承本州发遣赴阙就试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164991_comment'></div>圣俞自思，仆岂欲试者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164991_comment'></div>惟其平生不能区区附合有司之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164991", 1164991, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>尺度</span>，是以至此穷困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164991_comment'></div>今乃以五十衰病之身，奔走万里以就试，不亦为山林之士所轻笑哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164991_comment'></div>自思少年尝举茂才，中夜起坐，裹饭携饼，待晓东华门外，逐队而入，屈膝就席，俯首据案。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164991_comment'></div>其后每思至此，即为寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164991_comment'></div>今齿日益老，尚安能使达官贵人复弄其文墨，以穷其所不知邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164991_comment'></div>且以永叔之言与夫三书之所云，皆世之所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164991_comment'></div>今千里召仆而试之，盖其心尚有所未信，此尤不可茍进，以求其荣利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164991_comment'></div>昨适有病，遂以此辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164991_comment'></div>然恐无以答朝廷之恩，因为《上皇帝书》一通以进，盖以自解其不至之罪而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164991_comment'></div>不知圣俞当见之否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164991_comment'></div>冬寒，千万加爱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1164991_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　在眉山。任氏姊卒，苏洵作祭文。作品：《祭任氏姊文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165093' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165093' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165093?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭任氏姊文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165093")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165093_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165093'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165093'>昔我曾祖，子孙满门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165093_comment'></div>姊之先人，实惟其孙，不幸而亡，又不有嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165093_comment'></div>后世飨祀，其托在姊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165093_comment'></div>祭于女家，闻者欷歔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165093_comment'></div>姊不永存，后益以疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165093_comment'></div>姊之未亡，洵作《族谱》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165093_comment'></div>昆弟诸子，可以指数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165093_comment'></div>念姊之先，其后为谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165093_comment'></div>周旋反覆，不见而悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165093_comment'></div>悲其早丧，宜姊寿考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165093_comment'></div>春秋<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1165093", 1165093, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>荐献</span>，终姊之老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165093_comment'></div>今姊永归，遂及良人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165093_comment'></div>皆葬于原，送哭酸辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165093_comment'></div>姊之子孙，恭愿良谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165093_comment'></div>当有达者，以塞此恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165093_comment'></div>跪读此文，告以无憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165093_comment'></div>鬼神有知，尚克来鉴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1165093_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　梅尧臣寄诗题苏洵老人泉（老翁井）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　在眉山。任孜、任伋兄弟来诗，苏洵作诗答之。作品：《答二任》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134162' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134162' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134162?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答二任</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134162")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134162_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134162'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134162'>鲁人贱夫子，呼丘指东家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134162'>当时虽未遇，弟子已如麻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134162'>奈何乡闾人，曾不为叹嗟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134162'>区区吴越间，问骨不惮遐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134162'>习见反不怪，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_134162", 134162, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>海人</span>等龙虾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134162'>嗟我何足道，穷居<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>出无车。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134162'>昨者入京洛，文章彼<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作被）</span>人誇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134162'>故旧未肯信，闻之笑呀呀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134162'>独有两任子，知我有足嘉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134162'>远游苦相念，长篇寄芬葩。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134162'>我道<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作道我）</span>亦未尔，子得无增加。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134162'>贫穷已衰老，短发垂髿髿。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134162'>重禄无意取，思治山中畬。<div id='poem_sentence_12_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_134162'>往岁栽苦竹，细密如蒹葭。<div id='poem_sentence_13_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_134162'>庭前三小山，本为水中楂。<div id='poem_sentence_14_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_134162'>当前凿方池，寒泉照谽谺。<div id='poem_sentence_15_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_134162'>玩此可竟日，胡为踏朝衙。<div id='poem_sentence_16_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_134162'>何当子来会，酒食相邀遮。<div id='poem_sentence_17_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_134162'>愿为久相敬，终始无疵瑕。<div id='poem_sentence_18_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_134162'>闲居各无事，数来饮流霞。<div id='poem_sentence_19_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_134162'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_134162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_134162'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_134162_0'>⑴ 原作车，据康熙本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_134162_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　在眉山。夏，苏洵上欧阳修书。作品：《上欧阳内翰第四书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1164983' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164983' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164983?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上欧阳内翰第四书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164983")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164983_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164983'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164983'>洵启：夏热，伏惟提举内翰尊候万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164983_comment'></div>向为京兆尹，天下谓公当由此得政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164983_comment'></div>其后闻有此授，或以为拂世戾俗，过在于不肯卤莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164983_comment'></div>然此岂足为公损益哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164983_comment'></div>洵久不奉书，非敢有懈，以为用公之奏而得召，恐有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164983", 1164983, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>私谢</span>之嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164983_comment'></div>今者洵既不行，而朝廷又欲必致之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164983_comment'></div>恐听者不察，以为匹夫而要君命，茍以为高而求名，亦且得罪于门下，是故略陈其一二，以晓左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164983_comment'></div>闻之孟轲曰：「仕不为贫，而有时乎为贫」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164983_comment'></div>洵之所为欲仕者，为贫乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164983_comment'></div>实未至于饥寒而不择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164983_comment'></div>以为行道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164983_comment'></div>道固不在我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164983_comment'></div>且朝廷将何以待之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164983_comment'></div>今人之所谓富贵高显而近于君，可以行道者，莫若两制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164983_comment'></div>然犹以为不得为宰相，有所牵制于其上，而不得行其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164983_comment'></div>为宰相者，又以为时不可为，而我将有所待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164983_comment'></div>若洵又可以行道责之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164983_comment'></div>始公进其文，自丙申之秋至戊戌之冬，凡七百馀日而得召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164983_comment'></div>朝廷之事，其节目期限，如此之繁且久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164983_comment'></div>使洵今日治行，数月而至京师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164983_comment'></div>旅食于都市以待命，而数月间得试于所谓舍人院者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164983_comment'></div>然后使诸公专考其文，亦一二年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164983_comment'></div>幸而以为不谬，可以及等而奏之，从中下相府，相与拟议，又须年载间，而后可以庶几有望于一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164983_comment'></div>如此，洵固以老而不能为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164983_comment'></div>人皆曰求仕将以行道，若此者，果足以行道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164983_comment'></div>既不足以行道，而又不至于为贫，是二者皆无名焉，是故其来迟迟，而未甚乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164983_comment'></div>王命且再下，洵若固辞，必将以为沽名而有所希望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164983_comment'></div>今岁之秋，轼、辙已服阕，亦不可不与之俱东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164983_comment'></div>恐内翰怪其久而不来，是以略陈其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164983_comment'></div>拜见尚远，惟千万为国自重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1164983_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《自尤》诗。先是洵之幼女为夫家虐死，洵以为女之死乃己之过，乃作是诗。（并叙）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》、《类编增广老苏先生大全文集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_134146' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134146' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134146?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自尤<span class='inlineComment2'>（并叙）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134146")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134146_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134146'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134146'>五月之旦兹何辰，有女强死无由伸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134146'>嗟予为父亦不武，使汝孤冢埋冤魂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134146'>死生寿夭固无定，我岂以此辄怨人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134146'>当时此事最惊众，行道闻者皆醉<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑当作酸）</span>辛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134146'>余家世世本好学，生女不独治组紃。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134146'>读书未省事华饰，下笔亹亹能属文。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134146'>家贫不敢嫁豪贵，恐彼非偶难为亲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134146'>汝母之兄汝叔舅，求以厥子来结姻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134146'>乡人婚嫁重母族，虽我不肯将安云。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134146'>生年十六亦已嫁，日负忧责无欢欣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134146'>归宁见我悲且泣，告我家事不可陈。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134146'>舅姑叔妹不知道，弃礼自快纷如云。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134146'>人多我寡势不胜，祗欲强学非天真。<div id='poem_sentence_12_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_134146'>昨朝告以此太甚，捩耳不听生怒嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_13_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_134146'>余言如此非乃事，为妇何不善一身。<div id='poem_sentence_14_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_134146'>嗟哉尔夫任此责，可奈狂狠如痴麇。<div id='poem_sentence_15_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_134146'>忠臣汝不见泄治，谏死世不非陈君。<div id='poem_sentence_16_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_134146'>谁知余言果不妄，明年会汝初生孙。<div id='poem_sentence_17_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_134146'>一朝有疾莫肯视，此意岂尚求尔存。<div id='poem_sentence_18_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_134146'>忧惶百计独汝母，复有汝父惊且奔。<div id='poem_sentence_19_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_134146'>此时汝舅拥爱妾，呼卢握槊如隔邻。<div id='poem_sentence_20_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_134146'>狂言发病若有怪，里有老妇能降神。<div id='poem_sentence_21_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_134146'>呼来问讯岂得已，汝舅责我学不纯。<div id='poem_sentence_22_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_134146'>急难造次不可动，坚坐有类天王尊。<div id='poem_sentence_23_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_134146'>导其女妻使为孽，就病索汝襦与裙。<div id='poem_sentence_24_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_134146'>衣之出看又汝告，谬为与汝增殷勤。<div id='poem_sentence_25_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_134146'>多多扰乱莫胜记，咎汝不肯同其尘。<div id='poem_sentence_26_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_134146'>经旬乳药渐有喜，移病余告<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑当作舍）</span>未绝根。<div id='poem_sentence_27_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_134146'>喉中喘息气才属，日使勉强餐肥珍。<div id='poem_sentence_28_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_134146'>舅姑不许再生活，巧计窃发何不仁。<div id='poem_sentence_29_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_134146'>婴儿盈尺未能语，忽然夺去词纷纷。<div id='poem_sentence_30_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_134146'>传言姑怒不归觐，急抱疾走何暇询。<div id='poem_sentence_31_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_134146'>病中忧恐莫能测，起坐无语涕满巾。<div id='poem_sentence_32_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_134146'>须臾病作状如故，三日不救谁缘因。<div id='poem_sentence_33_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_134146'>此惟汝甥汝儿妇，何用负汝漫无恩。<div id='poem_sentence_34_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_134146'>嗟余生女苟不义，虽汝手刃吾何言。<div id='poem_sentence_35_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_134146'>俨然正直好礼让，才敏明辩超无伦。<div id='poem_sentence_36_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_134146'>正应以此获尤谴，汝可以手心自扪。<div id='poem_sentence_37_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_134146'>此虽法律所无奈，尚可仰首披苍旻。<div id='poem_sentence_38_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_134146'>天高鬼神不可信，后世有耳犹或闻。<div id='poem_sentence_39_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_134146'>只今闻者已不服，恨我无勇不复冤。<div id='poem_sentence_40_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_134146'>惟余故人不责汝，问我此事久叹呻。<div id='poem_sentence_41_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_134146'>惨然谓我子无恨，此罪在子何尤人。<div id='poem_sentence_42_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_134146'>虎跑牛触不足怪，当自为计免见吞。<div id='poem_sentence_43_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_134146'>深居高堂闭重键，牛虎岂解逾墙垣。<div id='poem_sentence_44_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_134146'>登山入泽不自爱，安可侥倖遭骐驎。<div id='poem_sentence_45_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_134146'>明珠美玉本无价，弃置沟上多缁磷。<div id='poem_sentence_46_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_134146'>置之失地自当尔，既尔何咎荆与榛。<div id='poem_sentence_47_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_134146'>嗟哉此事余有罪，当使天下重结婚<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上同上书卷二）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_48_134146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_134146'></div><div id='poem_sentence_49_134146_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《彭州圆觉禅院记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165079' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165079' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165079?labeling=true' target='_blank'>彭州圆觉禅院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165079")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165079_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165079'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165079'>人之居乎此也，其必有乐乎此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165079_comment'></div>居斯乐，不乐，不居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165079_comment'></div>居而不乐，不乐而不去，为自欺，且为欺天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165079_comment'></div>盖君子耻食其食而无其功，耻服其服而不知其事，故居而不乐，吾有吐食脱服以逃天下之讥而已耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165079_comment'></div>天之畀我以形，而使我以心驭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165079_comment'></div>今日欲适秦，明日欲适越，天下谁我御？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165079_comment'></div>故居而不乐，不乐而不去，是其心且不能驭其形，而况能以驭他人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165079_comment'></div>自唐以来，天下士大夫争以排释老为言，故其徒之欲求知于吾士大夫之间者，往往自叛其师以求容于吾，而吾士大夫亦喜其来而接之以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165079_comment'></div>灵师、文畅之徒，饮酒食肉以自绝于其教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165079_comment'></div>呜呼，归尔父子，复尔室家，而后吾许尔以叛尔师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165079_comment'></div>父子之不归，室家之不复，而师之叛，是不可以一日立于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165079_comment'></div>传曰：「人臣无外交」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165079_comment'></div>故季布之忠于楚也，虽不如萧、韩之先觉，而比丁公之贰则为愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165079_comment'></div>予在京师，彭州僧保聪来求识予甚勤，及至蜀，闻其自京师归，布衣蔬食以为其徒先，凡若干年，而所居圆觉院大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165079_comment'></div>一日，为予道其先师平润事，与其院之所以得名者，请予为记。<div
