class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165079_comment'></div>予佳聪之不以叛其师悦予也，故为之记曰：彭州龙兴寺僧平润讲《圆觉经》有奇，因以名院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165079_comment'></div>院始弊不葺，润之来，始得隙地以作堂宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165079_comment'></div>凡更二僧，而至于保聪，聪又合其邻之僧屋若干于其院以成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165079_comment'></div>是为记。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1165079'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1165079_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　苏洵与乡杨氏名僧仁庆、元俊、正信（表公）游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《极乐院造六菩萨记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165080' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165080' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165080?labeling=true' target='_blank'>极乐院造六菩萨记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165080")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165080_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165080'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165080'>始予少年时，父母俱存，兄弟妻子备具，终日嬉游，不知有死生之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165080_comment'></div>自长女之夭，不四五年而丁母夫人之忧，盖年二十有四矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165080_comment'></div>其后五年而丧兄希白，又一年而长子死，又四年而幼姊亡，又五年而次女卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165080_comment'></div>至于丁亥之岁，先君去世，又六年而失其幼女，服未既而有长姊之丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165080_comment'></div>悲忧惨怆之气，郁积而未散，盖年四十有九而丧妻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165080_comment'></div>嗟夫，三十年之间，而骨肉之亲零落无几！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165080_comment'></div>逝将南去，由荆楚走大梁，然后访吴、越，适燕、赵，徜徉于四方，以忘其老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165080_comment'></div>将去，慨然顾坟墓，追念死者，恐其魂神精爽，滞于幽阴冥漠之间，而不复旷然游乎逍遥之乡，于是造六菩萨并龛座二所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165080_comment'></div>盖释氏所谓观音、势至、天藏、地藏、解冤结、引路王者，置于极乐院阿弥如来之堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165080_comment'></div>庶几死者有知，或生于天，或生于四方上下，所适如意，亦若余之游于四方而无系云尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1165080_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《祭史亲家祖母文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。“史亲家祖母”为苏辙妻史氏之祖母。）</span><div id='poem_1165096' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165096' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165096?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭史亲家祖母文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165096")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165096_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165096'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165096'>嗟人之生，其久几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165096_comment'></div>百年之间，游者如麻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165096_comment'></div>反顾而思，可泣以悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165096_comment'></div>夫人之孙，归于子辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165096_comment'></div>自初许嫁，以及今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165096_comment'></div>旻天不吊，祸难荐结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165096_comment'></div>始自丁亥，天崩地坼，先君殁世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165096_comment'></div>次及近岁，子妇之母，亦以奄弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165096_comment'></div>顾惟荼毒，谓亦止此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165096_comment'></div>谁知于今，乃或有甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165096_comment'></div>室家不祥，死而莫救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165096_comment'></div>及于夫人，亦罹此咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165096_comment'></div>子丧其妣，妇丧祖母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165096_comment'></div>谁谓人生，而至于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165096_comment'></div>叹嗟伤心，悲不能止！</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1165096_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　在眉山。苏洵尝作《迎祥寺记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　在眉山。苏洵作《云兴于山》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134174' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134174' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134174?labeling=true' target='_blank'>云兴于山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134174")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_134174_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134174'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134174'>云兴于山，霿霿为雾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134174'>匪山不仁，天实不顾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134174'>山川我享，为我百诉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134174'>岂不畏天，哀此下土。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134174'>班班鸤鸠，谷谷晨号。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134174'>天乎未雨，余不告劳。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134174'>谁为山川，不如羽毛。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134174'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_134174_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　苏洵作《王道矩字说》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年10月4日</a>　十月四日（或五日），苏洵离眉州，赴京师，二子轼、辙侍。<br /></div>
-----end

成都（成都府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='eac8edd274da42d7a9253f1e0aedb6c9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eac8edd274da42d7a9253f1e0aedb6c9");'><span id='eac8edd274da42d7a9253f1e0aedb6c9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>，22岁</div><div id='eac8edd274da42d7a9253f1e0aedb6c9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年9月9日</a>　重九，洵至成都玉局观，得张仙画像。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f51a199731ca4aa7ba8bf517b547d750_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f51a199731ca4aa7ba8bf517b547d750");'><span id='f51a199731ca4aa7ba8bf517b547d750_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>，40岁</div><div id='f51a199731ca4aa7ba8bf517b547d750' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　田况自渭州知益州。苏洵尝见于益州，并投之以文。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='745387d911d74157a21761ccd854bef5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("745387d911d74157a21761ccd854bef5");'><span id='745387d911d74157a21761ccd854bef5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>，47岁</div><div id='745387d911d74157a21761ccd854bef5' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在成都。苏洵上张方平书，谢方平之荐举。洵拜谒方平于成都，呈《权书》、《衡论》，得方平盛誉。有上书、谢书。作品：《上张益州书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注·佚文》此文题目，曾枣庄、刘琳主编《全宋文》（上海辞书出版社、安徽教育出版社2006年版第43册第47页）作《谢张文定公书》）</span><div id='poem_1164987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164987?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上张侍郎第二书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164987")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164987'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164987'>省主侍郎执事：洵始至京师时，平生亲旧，往往在此，不见者盖十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164987_comment'></div>惜其老而无成，问所以来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164987_comment'></div>既而皆曰：「子欲有求，无事他人，须张益州来乃济」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164987_comment'></div>且云：「公不惜数千里走表为子求官，茍归，立便殿上，与天子相唯诺，顾不肯邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164987_comment'></div>退自思公之所与我者，盖不为浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164987_comment'></div>所不可知者，惟其力不足而势不便；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164987_comment'></div>不然，公于我无爱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164987_comment'></div>闻之古人：「日中必熭，操刀必割」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164987_comment'></div>当此时也，天子虚席而待公，其言宜无不听用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164987_comment'></div>洵也与公有如此之旧，适在京师，且未甚老，而犹足以有为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164987_comment'></div>此时而无成，亦足以见他人之无足求，而他日之无及也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164987_comment'></div>昨闻车马至此有日，西出百馀里迎见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164987_comment'></div>雪后苦风，晨至郑州，唇黑面烈，僮仆无人色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164987_comment'></div>从逆旅主人得束薪缊火，良久，乃能以见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164987_comment'></div>出郑州十里许，有导骑从东来，惊愕下马立道周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164987_comment'></div>云宋端明且至，从者数百人，足声如雷，已过乃敢上马徐去，私自伤至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164987_comment'></div>伏惟明公所谓洁廉而有文，可以比汉之司马子长者，盖穷困如此，岂不为之动心，而待其多言邪！</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1164987_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏洵至成都，辙从行，游大圣慈寺中和胜相院，见僧惟简（宝月）<br /></div><div class='label1' id='37191efddf7f470a94e3b6b0270d083f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("37191efddf7f470a94e3b6b0270d083f");'><span id='37191efddf7f470a94e3b6b0270d083f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，48岁</div><div id='37191efddf7f470a94e3b6b0270d083f' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春，苏洵至益州（成都），上张方平书，求汲引二子轼、辙。作品：《上张侍郎第一书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1164986' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164986' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164986?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上张侍郎第一书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164986")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164986_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164986'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164986'>侍郎执事：明公之知洵，洵知之，明公知之，他人亦知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164986_comment'></div>洵之所以获知于明公，明公之所以知洵者，虽暴之天下，皆可以无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164986_comment'></div>今也，将有所私告于执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164986_comment'></div>念将以屑屑之私，坏败其至公之节，欲忍而不言而不能，欲言而不果，勃然交于胸中，心不宁而颜忸怩者累月而后决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164986_comment'></div>窃见古之君子，知其人也忧其人，以至于其父母、昆弟、妻子，以至于其亲族、朋友，忧之固其责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164986_comment'></div>虽然，自我求之，则君子讥焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164986_comment'></div>知之而不忧，不忧而求人忧，则君子交讥之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164986_comment'></div>洵之意以为宁在我，而无宁在明公，故用此决其意而发其言，以私告于下执事，明公试一听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164986_comment'></div>洵有二子轼、辙，龆龀授经，不知他习，进趋拜跪，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1164986", 1164986, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>仪状</span>甚野，而独于文字中有可观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164986_comment'></div>始学声律，既成，以为不足尽力于其间，读孟、韩文，一见以为可作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164986_comment'></div>引笔书纸，日数千言，坌然溢出，若有所相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164986_comment'></div>年少狂勇，未尝更变，以为天子之爵禄可以攫取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164986_comment'></div>闻京师多贤士大夫，欲往从之游，因以举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164986_comment'></div>洵今年几五十，以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1164986", 1164986, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>懒钝</span>废于世，誓将绝进取之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164986_comment'></div>惟此二子，不忍使之复为湮沦弃置之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164986_comment'></div>今年三月，将与之如京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164986_comment'></div>一门之中，行者三人，而居者尚十数口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164986_comment'></div>为行者计，则害居者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164986_comment'></div>为居者计，则不能行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164986_comment'></div>恓恓焉无所告诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164986_comment'></div>夫以负贩之夫，左提妻、右挈子，奋身而往，尚不可御；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164986_comment'></div>有明公以为主，夫焉往而不济？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164986_comment'></div>今也望数千里之外，茫然如梯天而航海，蓄缩而不进，洵亦羞见朋友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164986_comment'></div>明公居齐桓、晋文之位，惟其不知洵，惟其知而不忧，则又何说？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164986_comment'></div>不然，何求而不克？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164986_comment'></div>轻之于鸿毛，重之于泰山，高之于九天，远之于万里，明公一言，天下谁议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164986_comment'></div>将使轼、辙求进于下风，明公引而察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164986_comment'></div>有一不如所言，愿赐诛绝，以惩欺罔之罪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1164986_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏洵携二子轼、辙至成都，将赴京师。张方平（安道）撰书荐洵于欧阳修，以六科勉轼兄弟。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>传张方平（文定）尝试苏轼兄弟以制科文字；方平晤苏洵，盛赞轼兄弟。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='0976661ec9ae44a3867d6ff7ba151324_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0976661ec9ae44a3867d6ff7ba151324");'><span id='0976661ec9ae44a3867d6ff7ba151324_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，48岁</div><div id='0976661ec9ae44a3867d6ff7ba151324' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　苏洵父子发成都，过剑门，经凤翔府郿县横渠镇，游崇寿院，经扶风。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
荆门（长林）

id='poem_title_134152' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134152?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆门惠泉</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134152")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134152_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134152'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134152'>古郡带荒山，寒泉出西郭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134152'>嘈嘈幽响远，衮衮清光活。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134152'>当年我少年，系马弄潺湲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134152'>爱此泉旁鹭，高姿不可攀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134152'>今逾二十载，我老泉依旧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134152'>临流照衰颜，始觉老且瘦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134152'>当时同游子，半作泉下尘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134152'>流水去不返，游人岁岁新。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134152'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_134152_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
开封

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年3月</a>　苏洵与本年礼部试，未中。三月甲寅（十七日），仁宗御崇政殿试礼部奏名进士。欧阳修、范镇、司马光、石扬休得中。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='bd84307d3b35470096e8edbe2c082b05_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bd84307d3b35470096e8edbe2c082b05");'><span id='bd84307d3b35470096e8edbe2c082b05_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a
