ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　苏洵与史经臣（彦辅）抵京师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　苏洵与颜太初（醇之、凫绎先生）等卿士大夫游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　是岁，“庆历新政”失败。苏洵仰天叹息，然未丧失希望。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年8月16日</a>　八月癸亥（十六日），仁宗御崇政殿，策试贤良方正能直言极谏。苏洵与史经臣同举制策，不中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　苏洵次女卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　苏洵归蜀，洵仲兄涣赋诗送之。涣时监裁造务。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e7d94dc4f6f641429c23e9e7150efa21_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e7d94dc4f6f641429c23e9e7150efa21");'><span id='e7d94dc4f6f641429c23e9e7150efa21_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，48岁</div><div id='e7d94dc4f6f641429c23e9e7150efa21' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年5月</a>　五六月间，苏洵父子三人抵京师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　苏洵父子馆于兴国寺浴室院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在开封。苏洵拜谒欧阳修，上修书，并献所为《洪范论》、《史论》，始见知于修。作品：《上欧阳内翰第一书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1164980' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164980' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164980?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上欧阳内翰第一书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164980")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164980_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164980'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164980'>内翰执事：洵布衣穷居，尝切有叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164980_comment'></div>以为天下之人不能皆贤，不能皆不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164980_comment'></div>故贤人君子之处于世，合必离，离必合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164980_comment'></div>往者天子方有意于治，而范公在相府，富公为枢密副使，执事与余公、蔡公为谏官，尹公驰骋上下，用力于兵革之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164980_comment'></div>方是之时，天下之人，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>毛发丝粟</span>之才，纷纷然而起，合而为一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164980_comment'></div>而洵也，自度其愚鲁无用之身，不足以自奋于其间，退而养其心，幸其道之将成，而可以复见于当世之贤人君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164980_comment'></div>不幸道未成，而范公西，富公北，执事与余公、蔡公分散四出，而尹公亦失势，奔走于小官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164980_comment'></div>洵时在京师，亲见其事，忽忽仰天叹息，以为斯人之去，而道虽成，不复足以为荣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164980_comment'></div>既复自思，念往者众君子之进于朝，其始也，必有善人焉搂之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164980_comment'></div>今也，亦必有小人焉推之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164980_comment'></div>今之世无复有善人也，则已矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164980_comment'></div>如其不然也，吾何忧焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164980_comment'></div>姑养其心，使其道大有成而待之，何伤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164980_comment'></div>退而处十年，虽未敢自谓其道有成矣，然浩浩乎，其胸中若与曩者异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164980_comment'></div>而余公适亦有成功于南方，执事与蔡公复相继登于朝，富公复自外入为宰相，其势将复合为一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164980_comment'></div>喜且自贺，以为道既已粗成，而果将有以发之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164980_comment'></div>既又反而思其向之所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>慕望</span>爱悦之而不得见之者，盖有六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164980_comment'></div>今将往见之矣，而六人者已有范公、尹公二人亡焉，则又为之潸然出涕以悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164980_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164980_comment'></div>二人者不可复见矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164980_comment'></div>而所恃以慰此心者，犹有四人也，则又以自解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164980_comment'></div>思其止于四人也，则又汲汲欲一识其面，以发其心之所欲言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164980_comment'></div>而富公又为天子之宰相，远方寒士未可遽以言通于其前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164980_comment'></div>余公、蔡公远者又在万里外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164980_comment'></div>独执事在朝廷间，而其位差不甚贵，可以叫呼扳援而闻之以言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164980_comment'></div>而饥寒衰老之病，又锢而留之，使不克自至于执事之庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164980_comment'></div>夫以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>慕望</span>爱悦其人之心，十年而不得见，而其人已死，如范公、尹公二人者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164980_comment'></div>则四人之中，非其势不可遽以言通者，何可以不能自往而遽已也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164980_comment'></div>执事之文章，天下之人莫不知之，然窃自以为洵之知之特深，愈于天下之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164980_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164980_comment'></div>孟子之文，语约而意尽，不为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>巉刻</span>斩绝之言，而其锋不可犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164980_comment'></div>韩子之文，如长江大河，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>浑浩</span>流转，鱼鼋蛟龙，万怪惶惑，而抑遏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/104/Comments/0")'>蔽掩</span>，不使自露，而人自见其渊然之光、苍然之色，亦自畏避，不敢迫视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164980_comment'></div>执事之文，纡馀委备，往复<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/111/Comments/0")'>百折</span>，而条达<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>疏畅</span>，无所间断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164980_comment'></div>气尽语极，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>急言</span>竭论，而容与閒易，无艰难劳苦之态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164980_comment'></div>此三者，皆断然自为一家之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164980_comment'></div>惟李翱之文，其味黯然而长，其光油然而幽，俯仰揖让，有执事之态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164980_comment'></div>陆贽之文，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>遣言措意</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/127/Comments/0")'>切近的当</span>，有执事之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164980_comment'></div>而执事之才，又自有过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164980_comment'></div>盖执事之文，非孟子、韩子之文，而欧阳子之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164980_comment'></div>夫乐道人之善而不为谄者，以其人诚足以当之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164980_comment'></div>彼不知者，则以为誉人以求其悦己也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164980_comment'></div>夫誉人以求其悦己，洵亦不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164980_comment'></div>而其所以道执事光明盛大之德，而不自知止者，亦欲执事之知其知我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164980_comment'></div>虽然，执事之名满于天下，虽不见其文，而固已知有欧阳子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164980_comment'></div>而洵也不幸堕在草野泥涂之中，而其知道之心，又近而粗成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164980_comment'></div>而欲徒手奉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/150/Comments/0")'>咫尺之书</span>，自托于执事，将使执事何从而知之，何从而信之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164980_comment'></div>洵少年不学，生二十五岁，始知读书，从士君子游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164980_comment'></div>年既已晚，而又不遂刻意厉行，以古人自期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164980_comment'></div>而视与己同列者，皆不胜己，则遂以为可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164980_comment'></div>其后困益甚，然后取古人之文而读之，始觉其出言用意，与己大异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164980_comment'></div>时复内顾，自思其才则又似夫不遂止于是而已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164980_comment'></div>由是尽烧曩时所为文数百篇，取《论语》、《孟子》、韩子及其他圣人、贤人之文，而兀然端坐，终日以读之者七八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164980_comment'></div>方其始也，入其中而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/175/Comments/0")'>惶然</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1164980_comment'></div>博观于其外，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/177/Comments/0")'>骇然</span>以惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1164980_comment'></div>及其久也，读之益精，而其胸中<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1164980", 1164980, "Clauses/180/Comments/0")'>豁然</span>以明，若人之言固当然者，然犹未敢自出其言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1164980_comment'></div>时既久，胸中之言日益多，不能自制，试出而书之，已而再三读之，浑浑乎觉其来之易矣，然犹未敢以为是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1164980_comment'></div>近所为《洪范论》、《史论》凡七篇，执事观其如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1164980_comment'></div>嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1164980_comment'></div>区区而自言，不知者又将以为自誉以求人之知己也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1164980_comment'></div>惟执事思其十年之心如是之不偶然也而察之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1164980_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　秋，苏洵二子轼、辙应开封府解。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　秋，苏轼应举时，杜叔元（君懿）以所藏诸葛笔赠轼。洵以兄事叔元。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　开封府解试榜出，苏洵子轼名第二，辙亦中其选。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年9月19日</a>　九月十九日，在开封。苏洵作文送石扬休（昌言）北使。先是八月丙寅（十七日），扬休以刑部员外郎、知制诰为契丹国母生辰使。轼书洵之文。作品：《送石昌言使北引》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165005' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165005' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165005?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送石昌言使北引</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年9月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165005")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165005_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165005'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165005'>昌言举进士时，吾始数岁，未学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165005_comment'></div>忆与群儿戏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1165005", 1165005, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>先府君</span>侧，昌言从旁取枣栗啖我，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1165005", 1165005, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>家居</span>相近，又以亲戚故，甚狎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165005_comment'></div>昌言举进士，日有名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165005_comment'></div>吾后渐长，亦稍知读书，学句读、属对、声律，未成而废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165005_comment'></div>昌言闻吾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1165005", 1165005, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>废学</span>，虽不言，察其意甚恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165005_comment'></div>后十馀年，昌言及第第四人，守官四方，不相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165005_comment'></div>吾以壮大，乃能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1165005", 1165005, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>感悔</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1165005", 1165005, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>摧折</span>复学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165005_comment'></div>又数年，游京师，见昌言长安，相与劳苦如平生欢，出文十数首，昌言甚喜，称善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165005_comment'></div>吾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1165005", 1165005, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>晚学</span>无师，虽日为文，中甚自惭，及闻昌言说，乃颇自喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165005_comment'></div>今十馀年，又来京师，而昌言官两制，乃为天子出使万里外强悍不屈之虏庭，建大旆，从骑数百，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1165005", 1165005, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>送车</span>千乘，出都门，意气慨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165005_comment'></div>自思为儿时，见昌言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1165005", 1165005, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>先府君</span>旁，安知其至此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165005_comment'></div>富贵不足怪，吾于昌言独有感也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165005_comment'></div>丈夫生不为将，得为使，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1165005", 1165005, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>折冲</span>口舌之间足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165005_comment'></div>往年彭任从富公使还，为我言，既出境，宿驿亭，闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1165005", 1165005, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>介马</span>数万骑驰过，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1165005", 1165005, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>剑槊</span>相摩，终夜有声，从者怛然失色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165005_comment'></div>及明，视道上马迹，尚心掉不自禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165005_comment'></div>凡虏所以夸耀中国者多此类，中国之人不测也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165005_comment'></div>故或至于震惧而失辞，以为夷狄笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165005_comment'></div>呜呼，何其不思之甚也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165005_comment'></div>昔者奉春君使冒顿，壮士、大马皆匿不见，是以有平城之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165005_comment'></div>今之匈奴，吾知其无能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165005_comment'></div>孟子曰：「说大人者，藐之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165005_comment'></div>况于夷狄！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165005_comment'></div>请以为赠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1165005_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　秋，欧阳修始进苏洵之文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在开封。乡人陈景回自南来，欲治园囿于蔡，苏洵作诗赠之。作品：《丙申岁余在京师乡人陈景回自南来……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134145' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134145' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134145?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙申岁余在京师乡人陈景回自南来弃其官得太子中允景回旧有地在蔡今将治园囿于其间以自老余尝有意于嵩山之下洛水之上买地筑室以为休息之馆而未果今景回欲余诗遂道此意景回志余言异日可以知余之非戏云尔</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134145")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134145_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134145'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134145'>岷山之阳土如腴，江水清滑多鲤鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134145'>古人居之富者众，我独<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_134145", 134145, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>厌倦</span>思移居。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134145'>平川如手山水蹙，恐我后世鄙且愚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134145'>经行天下爱嵩岳，遂欲买地居妻孥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134145'>晴原漫漫望不尽，山色照野光如濡。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134145'>民生舒缓无夭扎，衣冠堂堂伟丈夫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134145'>吾今隐居未有所，更后十载不可无。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134145'>闻君厌蜀乐上蔡，占地百顷无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_134145", 134145, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>边隅</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134145'>草深野阔足狐兔，水种陆取身不劬。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134145'>谁知李斯顾秦宠，不获牵犬追黄狐。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134145'>今君南去已足老，行看嵩少当吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134145'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_134145_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在开封。苏洵上枢密使韩琦书。作品：《上韩枢密书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1164975' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164975' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164975?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上韩枢密书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164975")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164975_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164975'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164975'>太尉执事：洵著书无他长，及言兵事，论古今形势，至自比贾谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164975_comment'></div>所献《权书》，虽古人已往成败之迹，茍深晓其义，施之于今，无所不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164975_comment'></div>昨因请见，求进<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1164975", 1164975, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>末议</span>，太尉许诺，谨撰其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164975_comment'></div>言语<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1164975", 1164975, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>朴直</span>，非有惊世绝俗之谈，甚高难行之论，太尉取其大纲，而无责其纤悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164975_comment'></div>盖古者非用兵决胜之为难，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1164975", 1164975, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>养兵</span>不用之可畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164975_comment'></div>今夫水激之山，放之海，决之为沟塍，壅之为沼沚，是天下之人能之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164975_comment'></div>委江河，注淮泗，汇为洪波，潴为大湖，万世而不溢者，自禹之后未之见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164975_comment'></div>夫兵者，聚天下不义之徒，授之以不仁之器，而教之以杀人之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164975_comment'></div>夫惟天下之未安，盗贼之未殄，然后有以施其不义之心，用其不仁之器，而试其杀人之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164975_comment'></div>当是之时，勇者无馀力，智者无馀谋，巧者无馀技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164975_comment'></div>故其不义之心变而为忠，不仁之器加之于不仁，而杀人之事施之于当杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164975_comment'></div>及夫天下既平，盗贼既殄，不义之徒聚而不散，勇者有馀力则思以为乱，智者有馀谋则思以为奸，巧者有馀技则思以为诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164975_comment'></div>于是天下之患杂然出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164975_comment'></div>盖虎豹终日而不杀，则跳踉大叫，以发其怒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164975_comment'></div>蝮蝎终日而不蛰，则噬齧草木，以致其毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164975_comment'></div>其理固然，无足怪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164975_comment'></div>昔者刘、项奋臂于草莽之间，秦、楚无赖子弟千百为辈，争起而应者，不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164975_comment'></div>转斗五六年，天下厌兵，项籍死，而高祖亦已老矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164975_comment'></div>方是时，分王诸将，改定律令，与天下休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164975_comment'></div>而韩信、黥布之徒，相继而起者七国，高祖死于介胄之间而莫能止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164975_comment'></div>连延及于吕氏之祸，讫孝文而后定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164975_comment'></div>是何起之易而收之难也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164975_comment'></div>刘、项之势，初若决河，顺流而下，诚有可喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164975_comment'></div>及其崩溃四出，放乎数百里之间，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1164975", 1164975, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>拱手</span>而莫能救也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164975_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164975_comment'></div>不有圣人，何以善其后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164975_comment'></div>太祖、太宗，躬擐甲胄，跋履险阻，以斩刈四方之蓬蒿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164975_comment'></div>用兵数十年，谋臣猛将满天下，一旦卷甲而休之，传四世而天下无变，此何术也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164975_comment'></div>荆、楚、九江之地不分于诸将，而韩信、黥布之徒无以启其心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164975_comment'></div>虽然，天下无变，而兵久不用，则其不义之心蓄而无所发，饱食优游，求逞于良民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164975_comment'></div>观其平居无事，出怨言以邀其上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164975_comment'></div>一日有急，是非人得千金，不可使也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164975_comment'></div>往年诏天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1164975", 1164975, "Clauses/113/Comments/0")'>缮完</span>城池，西川之事，洵实亲见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164975_comment'></div>凡郡县之富民，举而籍其名，得钱数百万，以为酒食<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1164975", 1164975, "Clauses/119/Comments/0")'>馈饷</span>之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164975_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1164975", 1164975, "Clauses/120/Comments/0")'>杵声</span>未绝，城辄随坏，如此者数年而后定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164975_comment'></div>卒事，官吏相贺，卒徒相矜，若战胜凯旋而待赏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164975_comment'></div>比来京师，游阡陌间，其曹往往偶语，无所讳忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164975_comment'></div>闻之土人，方春时，尤不忍闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164975_comment'></div>盖时五六月矣，会京师忧大水，锄耰畚筑列于两河之壖，县官日费千万，传呼劳问之声不绝者数十里，犹且<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1164975", 1164975, "Clauses/139/Comments/0")'>睊睊</span>狼顾，莫肯效用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164975_comment'></div>且夫内之如京师之所闻，外之如西川之所亲见，天下之势今何如也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164975_comment'></div>御将者天子之事也，御兵者将之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164975_comment'></div>天子者，养尊而处优，树恩而收名，与天下为喜乐者也，故其道不可以御兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164975_comment'></div>人臣执法而不求情，尽心而不求名，出死力以捍社稷，使天下之心系于一人，而己不与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164975_comment'></div>故御兵者，人臣之事，不可以累天子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164975_comment'></div>今之所患，大臣好名而惧谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164975_comment'></div>好名则多树私恩，惧谤则执法不坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164975_comment'></div>是以天下之兵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1164975", 1164975, "Clauses/163/Comments/0")'>豪纵</span>至此，而莫之或制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164975_comment'></div>顷者狄公在枢府，号为宽厚爱人，狎昵士卒，得其欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164975_comment'></div>而太尉适承其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164975_comment'></div>彼狄公者知御外之术，而不知治内之道，此边将材也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164975_comment'></div>古者兵在外，爱将军而忘天子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1164975_comment'></div>在内，爱天子而忘将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1164975_comment'></div>爱将军所以战，爱天子所以守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1164975_comment'></div>狄公以其御外之心而施诸其内，太尉不反其道，而何以为治？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1164975_comment'></div>或者以为兵久骄不治，一旦绳以法，恐因以生乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1164975_comment'></div>昔者郭子仪去河南，李光弼实代之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1164975_comment'></div>将至之日，张用济斩于辕门，三军股栗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1164975_comment'></div>夫以临淮之悍，而代汾阳之长者，三军之士，竦然如赤子之脱慈母之怀，而立乎严师之侧，何乱之敢生？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1164975_comment'></div>且夫天子者，天下之父母也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1164975_comment'></div>将相者，天下之师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1164975_comment'></div>师虽严，赤子不以怨其父母；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1164975_comment'></div>将相虽厉，天下不以咎其君，其势然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1164975_comment'></div>天子者，可以生人杀人，故天下望其生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1164975_comment'></div>及其杀之也，天下曰：是天子杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1164975_comment'></div>故天子不可以多杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1164975_comment'></div>人臣奉天子之法，虽多杀，天下无以归怨，此先王所以威怀天下之术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1164975_comment'></div>伏惟太尉思天下所以长久之道，而无幸一时之名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1164975_comment'></div>尽至公之心，而无恤三军之多言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1164975_comment'></div>夫天子推深仁以结其心，太尉厉威武以振其堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1164975_comment'></div>彼其思天子之深仁，则畏而不至于怨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1164975_comment'></div>思太尉之威武，则爱而不至于骄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1164975_comment'></div>君臣之体顺，而畏爱之道立，非太尉吾谁望邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1164975_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1164975_comment'></div>洵再拜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_1164975'></div><div id='poem_sentence_73_1164975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1164975'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_73_1164975_0'>⑴ 《苏老泉先生全集》卷一一。又见《崇古文诀》卷二二，《古文集成》卷一八，《古今合璧事类备要》后集卷一六，《古今事文类聚》新集卷一七，《永乐大典》卷八四一四，《古文奇赏》卷二一，《文章辨体汇选》卷二二六《文翰类选大成》卷一二一，《文编》卷四六。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1164975_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在开封。苏洵上丞相文彦博书。作品：《上文丞相书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1164977' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164977' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164977?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上文丞相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164977")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164977_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164977'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164977'>昭文相公执事：天下之事，制之在始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164977_comment'></div>始不可制，制之在末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164977_comment'></div>是以君子慎始而无后忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164977_comment'></div>救之于其末，而其始不为无谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164977_comment'></div>谋诸其始而邀诸其终，而天下无遗事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164977_comment'></div>是故古者之制其始也，有百年之前而为之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164977_comment'></div>盖周公营乎东周，数百年而待乎平王之东迁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164977_comment'></div>然及其收天下之士，而责其贤不肖之分，则未尝于其始焉，而制其极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164977_comment'></div>盖尝举之于诸侯，考之于太学，引之于射宫而试之弓矢，如此其备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164977_comment'></div>然而管叔、蔡叔，文王之子，而武王，周公之弟也，生而与之居处，习知其性之所好恶，与夫居之于太学，而习之于射宫者，宜愈详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164977_comment'></div>然其不肖之实，卒不见于此时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164977_comment'></div>及其出为诸侯监国，临大事而不克自定，然后败露，以见其不肖之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164977_comment'></div>且夫张弓而射之，一不失容，此不肖者或能焉，而圣人岂以为此足以尽人之才？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164977_comment'></div>盖将为此名以收天下之士，而后观其临事，而黜其不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164977_comment'></div>故曰：始不可制，制之在末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164977_comment'></div>于此有人求金于沙，敛而扬之，惟其扬之也精，是以责金于扬，而敛则无择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164977_comment'></div>不然，金与沙砾皆不录而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164977_comment'></div>故欲求尽天下之贤俊，莫若略其始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164977_comment'></div>欲求责实于天下之官，莫若精其终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164977_comment'></div>今者天下之官自相府而至于一县之丞尉，其为数实不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164977_comment'></div>然而大数已定，馀吏滥于官籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164977_comment'></div>大臣建议减任子、削进士，以求便天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164977_comment'></div>窃观古者之制，略于始而精于终，使贤者易进，而不肖者易犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164977_comment'></div>夫易犯故易退，易进故贤者众，众贤进而不肖者易退，夫何患官冗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164977_comment'></div>今也艰之于其始，窃恐夫贤者之难进，与夫不肖者之无以异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164977_comment'></div>方今进退天下士大夫之权，内则御史，外则转运，而士大夫之间絜然而无过，可任以为吏者，其实无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164977_comment'></div>且相公何不以意推之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164977_comment'></div>往年吴中复在犍为，一月而发二吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164977_comment'></div>中复去职，而吏之以罪免者，旷岁无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164977_comment'></div>虽然，此特洵之所见耳，天下之大则又可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164977_comment'></div>国家法令甚严，洵从蜀来，见凡吏商者皆不征，非追胥调发，皆得役天子之夫，是以知天下之吏犯法者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164977_comment'></div>从其犯而黜之，十年之后将分职之不给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164977_comment'></div>此其权在御史、转运，而御史、转运之权实在相公，顾甚易为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164977_comment'></div>今四方之士会于京师，口语籍籍，莫不为此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164977_comment'></div>然皆莫肯一言于其上，诚以为近于私我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164977_comment'></div>洵，西蜀之人，方不见用于当世，幸又不复以科举为意，是以肆言于其间而可以无嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164977_comment'></div>伏惟相公慨然有忧天下之心，征伐四国以安天下，毅然立朝以威制天下，名著功遂，文武并济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164977_comment'></div>此其享功业之重而居富贵之极，于其平生之所望无复慊然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164977_comment'></div>惟其获天下之多士，而与之皆乐乎，此可以复动其志，故遂以此告其左右，惟相公亮之。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1164977'></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1164977_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在开封。苏洵上丞相富弼书。先是欧阳修有与富弼书，叙洵求见之意。作品：《上富丞相书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1164976' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164976' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164976?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上富丞相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164976")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164976_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164976'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164976'>相公阁下：往年天子震怒，出逐宰相，选用旧臣堪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164976", 1164976, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>付属</span>以天下者，使在相府，与天下更始，而阁下之位实在第三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164976_comment'></div>方是之时，天下咸喜相庆，以为阁下惟不为宰相也，故默默在此；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164976_comment'></div>方今困而后起，起而复为宰相，而又值乎此时也，不为而何为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164976_comment'></div>且吾君之意，待之如此其厚也，不为而何以副吾望？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164976_comment'></div>故咸曰：「后有下令而异于他日者，必吾富公也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164976_comment'></div>朝夕而待之，跂首而望之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164976_comment'></div>望望然而不获见也，戚戚然而疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164976_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164976_comment'></div>其弗获闻也，必其远也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164976_comment'></div>进而及于京师，亦无闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164976_comment'></div>不敢以疑，犹曰：天下之人如此其众也，数十年之间如此其变也，皆曰贤人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164976_comment'></div>或曰：彼其中则有说也，而天下之人则未始见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164976_comment'></div>然而不能无忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164976_comment'></div>盖古之君子，爱其人也则忧其无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164976_comment'></div>且尝闻之，古之君子，相是君也，与是人也，皆立于朝，则使吾皆知其为人皆善者也，而后无忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164976_comment'></div>且一人之身而欲擅天下之事，虽见信于当世，而同列之人一言而疑之，则事不可以成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164976_comment'></div>今夫政出于他人而不惧，事不出于己而不忌，是二者，惟善人为能，然犹欲得其心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164976_comment'></div>若夫众人，政出于他人而惧其害己，事不出于己而忌其成功，是以有不平之心生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164976_comment'></div>夫或居于吾前，或立于吾后，而皆有不平之心焉，则身危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164976_comment'></div>故君子之出处于其间也，不使之不平于我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164976_comment'></div>周公立于明堂以听天下，而召公惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164976_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164976_comment'></div>天下固惑乎大者也，召公犹未能信乎吾之此心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164976_comment'></div>周公定天下，诛管、蔡，告召公以其志，以安其身，以及于成王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164976_comment'></div>故凡安其身者，以安乎周也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164976_comment'></div>召公之于周公，管、蔡之于周公，是二者亦皆有不平之心焉，以为周之天下，公将遂取之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164976_comment'></div>周公诛其不平而不可告语者，告其可以告语者，而和其不平之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164976_comment'></div>然则，非其必不可以告语者，则君子未始不欲和其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164976_comment'></div>天下之人，从士而至于卿大夫，宰相集处其上，欲有所为，何虑而不成？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164976_comment'></div>不能忍其区区之小忿，以成其不平之衅，则害其大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164976_comment'></div>是以君子忍其小忿以容其小过，而杜其不平之心，然后当大事而听命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164976_comment'></div>且吾之小忿，不足以易吾之大事也，故宁小容焉，使无芥蒂于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164976_comment'></div>古之君子与贤者并居而同乐，故其责之也详；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164976_comment'></div>不幸而与不肖者偶，不图其大而治其细，则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1164976", 1164976, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>阔远</span>于事情而无益于当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164976_comment'></div>故天下无事而后可与争此，不然则否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164976_comment'></div>昔者诸吕用事，陈平忧惧，计无所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164976_comment'></div>陆贾入见说之，使交欢周勃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164976_comment'></div>陈平用其策，卒得绛侯入北军之助以灭诸吕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164976_comment'></div>夫绛侯，木强之人也，非陈平致之而谁也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164976_comment'></div>故贤人者致其不贤者，非夫不贤者之能致贤者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164976_comment'></div>曩者，今上即位之初，寇莱公为相，惟其侧有小人不能诛，又不能与之无忿，故终以斥去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164976_comment'></div>及范文正公在相府，又欲以岁月尽治天下事，失于急与不忍小忿，故群小人亦急逐之，一去遂不复用，以殁其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164976_comment'></div>伏惟阁下以不世出之才，立于天子之下，百官之上，此其深谋远虑必有所处，而天下之人犹未获见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164976_comment'></div>洵，西蜀之人也，窃有志于今世，愿一见于堂上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164976_comment'></div>伏惟阁下深思之，无忽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1164976_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在开封。苏洵上枢密副使田况书。并以《策》二道、《权书》十篇为献。作品：《上田枢密书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1164978' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164978' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164978?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上田枢密书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164978")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164978_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164978'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164978'>天之所以与我者，夫岂偶然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164978_comment'></div>尧不得以与丹朱，舜不得以与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164978", 1164978, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>商均</span>，而瞽叟不得夺诸舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164978_comment'></div>发于其心，出于其言，见于其事，确乎其不可易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164978_comment'></div>圣人不得以与人，父不得夺诸其子，于此见天之所以与我者不偶然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164978_comment'></div>夫其所以与我者，必有以用我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164978_comment'></div>我知之不得行之，不以告人，天固用之，我实置之，其名曰弃天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164978_comment'></div>自卑以求幸其言，自小以求用其道，天之所以与我者何如，而我如此也，其名曰亵天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164978_comment'></div>弃天，我之罪也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164978_comment'></div>亵天，亦我之罪也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164978_comment'></div>不弃不亵，而人不我用，非我之罪也，其名曰逆天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164978_comment'></div>然则弃天、亵天者其责在我，逆天者其责在人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164978_comment'></div>在我者，吾将尽吾力之所能为者，以塞夫天之所以与我之意，而求免乎天下后世之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164978_comment'></div>在人者，吾何知焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164978_comment'></div>吾求免夫一身之责之不暇，而暇为人忧乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164978_comment'></div>孔子、孟轲之不遇，老于道涂而不倦不愠不怍不沮者，夫固知夫责之所在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164978_comment'></div>卫灵、鲁哀、齐宣、梁惠之徒之不足相与以有为也，我亦知之矣，抑将尽吾心焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164978_comment'></div>吾心之不尽，吾恐天下后世无以责夫卫灵、鲁哀、齐宣、梁惠之徒，而彼亦将有以辞其责也，然则孔子、孟轲之目将不瞑于地下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164978_comment'></div>夫圣人贤人之用心也固如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164978_comment'></div>如此而生，如此而死，如此而贫贱，如此而富贵，升而为天，沉而为渊，流而为川，止而为山，彼不预吾事，吾事毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164978_comment'></div>窃怪夫后之贤者之不能自处其身也，饥寒穷困之不胜而号于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164978_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164978_comment'></div>使其诚死于饥寒穷困邪，则天下后世之责将必有在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164978_comment'></div>彼其身之责不自任以为忧，而我取而加之吾身，不已过乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164978_comment'></div>今洵之不肖，何敢以自列于圣贤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164978_comment'></div>然其心亦有所不甚自轻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164978_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164978_comment'></div>天下之学者，孰不欲一蹴而造圣人之域，然及其不成也，求一言之几乎道而不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164978_comment'></div>千金之子，可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1164978", 1164978, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>贫人</span>，可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1164978", 1164978, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>富人</span>，非天之所与，虽以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1164978", 1164978, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>贫人</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1164978", 1164978, "Clauses/83/Comments/1")'>富人</span>之权，求一言之几乎道，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164978_comment'></div>天子之宰相，可以生人，可以杀人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164978_comment'></div>非天之所与，虽以生人杀人之权，求一言之几乎道，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164978_comment'></div>今洵用力于圣人贤人之术亦已久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164978_comment'></div>其言语，其文章，虽不识其果可以有用于今而传于后与否，独怪其得之之不劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164978_comment'></div>方其致思于心也，若或起之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164978_comment'></div>得之心而书之纸也，若或相之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164978_comment'></div>夫岂无一言之几乎道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164978_comment'></div>千金之子，天子之宰相，求而不得者，一旦在己，故其心得以自负，或者天其亦有以与我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164978_comment'></div>曩者见执事于益州，当时之文，浅狭可笑，饥寒穷困乱其心，而声律记问又从而破坏其体，不足观也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164978_comment'></div>数年来退居山野，自分永弃，与世俗日疏阔，得以大肆其力于文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164978_comment'></div>诗人之优柔，骚人之精深，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1164978", 1164978, "Clauses/121/Comments/1")'>孟、韩</span>之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1164978", 1164978, "Clauses/121/Comments/2")'>温淳</span>，迁、固之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1164978", 1164978, "Clauses/122/Comments/1")'>雄刚</span>，孙、吴之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1164978", 1164978, "Clauses/123/Comments/1")'>简切</span>，投之所向，无不如意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164978_comment'></div>常以为董生得圣人之经，其失也流而为迂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164978_comment'></div>晁错得圣人之权，其失也流而为诈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164978_comment'></div>有二子之才而不流者，其惟贾生乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164978_comment'></div>惜乎今之世，愚未见其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164978_comment'></div>作策二道，曰《审势》、《审敌》，作书十篇曰《权书》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164978_comment'></div>洵有山田一顷，非凶岁，可以无饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164978_comment'></div>力耕而节用，亦足以自老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164978_comment'></div>不肖之身不足惜，而天之所与者不忍弃，且不敢亵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164978_comment'></div>执事之名满天下，天下之士用与不用在执事，故敢以所谓《策》二道、《权书》十篇者为献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164978_comment'></div>平生之文，远不可多致，有《洪范论》、《史论》七篇，近以献内翰欧阳公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1164978_comment'></div>度执事与之朝夕相从，而议天下之事，则斯文也其亦庶乎得陈于前矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1164978_comment'></div>若夫其言之可用与其身之可贵与否者，执事事也，执事责也，于洵何有哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1164978_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　苏洵尝会遇吴中复。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年10月</a>　在开封。十月，裴煜（如晦）知吴江，欧阳修饯行，王安石（介甫）、梅尧臣（圣俞）及苏洵与其会，分韵赋送行诗。尧臣极称苏轼、苏辙兄弟。作品：《残句·送裴如晦知吴江》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》此诗残缺，仅存一句：“谈诗究乎而。”）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3e9e02c699624a31a8a2314c83edcee2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3e9e02c699624a31a8a2314c83edcee2");'><span id='3e9e02c699624a31a8a2314c83edcee2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1057')">1056-1057年</a>，48-49岁</div><div id='3e9e02c699624a31a8a2314c83edcee2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在开封。张方平至京师，苏洵上书方平。作品：《上张侍郎第二书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1164987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164987?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上张侍郎第二书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164987")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164987'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164987'>省主侍郎执事：洵始至京师时，平生亲旧，往往在此，不见者盖十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164987_comment'></div>惜其老而无成，问所以来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164987_comment'></div>既而皆曰：「子欲有求，无事他人，须张益州来乃济」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164987_comment'></div>且云：「公不惜数千里走表为子求官，茍归，立便殿上，与天子相唯诺，顾不肯邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164987_comment'></div>退自思公之所与我者，盖不为浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164987_comment'></div>所不可知者，惟其力不足而势不便；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164987_comment'></div>不然，公于我无爱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164987_comment'></div>闻之古人：「日中必熭，操刀必割」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164987_comment'></div>当此时也，天子虚席而待公，其言宜无不听用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164987_comment'></div>洵也与公有如此之旧，适在京师，且未甚老，而犹足以有为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164987_comment'></div>此时而无成，亦足以见他人之无足求，而他日之无及也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164987_comment'></div>昨闻车马至此有日，西出百馀里迎见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164987_comment'></div>雪后苦风，晨至郑州，唇黑面烈，僮仆无人色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164987_comment'></div>从逆旅主人得束薪缊火，良久，乃能以见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164987_comment'></div>出郑州十里许，有导骑从东来，惊愕下马立道周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164987_comment'></div>云宋端明且至，从者数百人，足声如雷，已过乃敢上马徐去，私自伤至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164987_comment'></div>伏惟明公所谓洁廉而有文，可以比汉之司马子长者，盖穷困如此，岂不为之动心，而待其多言邪！</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1164987_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　苏洵访张方平（安道），方平询及轼、辙学业。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在开封。苏洵赋《欧阳永叔白兔》。梅尧臣、韩维、刘敞、刘攽、王安石皆有赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134150' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134150' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134150?labeling=true' target='_blank'>欧阳永叔白兔</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134150")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134150_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134150'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134150'>飞鹰搏平原，禽兽乱衰草。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134150'>苍茫就擒执，颠倒莫能保。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134150'>白兔不忍杀，叹息爱其老。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134150'>独生遂长拘，野性始惊矫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134150'>贵人织筠笼，驯扰渐可抱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134150'>谁知山林宽，穴处颇自好。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134150'>高飙动槁叶，群窜迹如扫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134150'>异质不自藏，照野明皓皓。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134150'>猎夫指之笑，自匿苦不早。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134150'>何当骑蟾蜍，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_134150", 134150, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>灵杵</span>手自捣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134150'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_134150_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在开封。李大临（才元）知邛州，苏洵有送行诗。梅尧臣、苏颂、刘敞、司马光、王安石亦有送行诗。大林之行以岁末。作品：《送李才元学士知邛州》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134155' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134155' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134155?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送李才元学士知邛州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134155")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134155_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134155'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134155'>贫贱羞妻子，富贵乐乡关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134155'>不见李夫子，得意今西还。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134155'>白马渡浐水，红旌照蜀山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134155'>归来未解带，故旧已满门。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134155'>平生浪游处，何者哀王孙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134155'>壮士勿龌龊，千金报一飧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134155'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_134155_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　苏洵至京师后，文章为时所推重，然与王安石颇不协。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在开封。苏洵二上欧阳修书。作品：《上欧阳内翰第二书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1164981' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164981' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164981?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上欧阳内翰第二书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164981")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164981_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164981'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164981'>内翰谏议执事：士之能以其姓名闻乎天下后世者，夫岂偶然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164981_comment'></div>以今观之，乃可以见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164981_comment'></div>生而同乡，学而同道，以某问某，盖有曰吾不闻者焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164981_comment'></div>而况乎天下之广，后世之远，虽欲求髣髴，岂易得哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164981_comment'></div>古之以一能称，以一善书者，愚未尝敢忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164981_comment'></div>今夫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164981", 1164981, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>群群</span>焉而生，逐逐焉而死者，更千万人不称不书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164981_comment'></div>彼之以一能称，以一善书者，皆有以过乎千万人者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164981_comment'></div>自孔子没，百有馀年而孟子生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164981_comment'></div>孟子之后，数十年而至荀卿子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164981_comment'></div>荀卿子后乃稍阔远，二百馀年而扬雄称于世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164981_comment'></div>扬雄之死，不得其继，千有馀年，而后属之韩愈氏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164981_comment'></div>韩愈氏没三百年矣，不知天下之将谁与也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164981_comment'></div>且夫以一能称，以一善书者，皆不可忽，则其多称而屡书者，其为人宜尤可贵重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164981_comment'></div>奈何数千年之间，四人而无加，此其人宜何如也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164981_comment'></div>天下病无斯人，天下而有斯人也，宜何以待之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164981_comment'></div>洵一穷布衣，于今世最为无用，思以一能称，以一善书而不可得者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164981_comment'></div>况夫四子者之文章，诚不敢冀其万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164981_comment'></div>顷者张益州见其文，以为似司马子长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164981_comment'></div>洵不悦，辞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164981_comment'></div>夫以布衣，而王公大人称其文似司马迁，不悦而辞，无乃为不近人情？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164981_comment'></div>诚恐天下之人不信，且惧张公之不能副其言，重为世俗笑耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164981_comment'></div>若执事，天下所就而折衷者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164981_comment'></div>不知其不肖，称之曰：「子之《六经论》，荀卿子之文也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164981_comment'></div>平生为文，求于千万人中使其姓名髣髴于后世而不可得，今也一旦而得齿于四人者之中，天下乌有是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164981_comment'></div>意者其失于斯言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164981_comment'></div>执事于文称师鲁，于诗称子美、圣俞，未闻其有此言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164981_comment'></div>意者其戏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164981_comment'></div>惟其愚而不顾，日书其所为文，惟执事之求而致之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164981_comment'></div>既而屡请而屡辞焉，曰：「吾未暇读也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164981_comment'></div>退而处，不敢复见，其惭于朋友，曰：「信矣，其戏也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164981_comment'></div>虽然，天下不知其为戏，将有以议执事，洵亦且得罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164981_comment'></div>执事怜其平生之心，茍以为可教，亦足以慰其衰老，惟无曰荀卿云者，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1164981_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在开封。知制诰韩绛欲见苏洵，洵报之以书，陈愿见之意。作品：《上韩舍人书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1164988' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164988?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上韩舍人书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164988")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164988_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164988'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164988'>舍人执事：方今天下虽号无事，而政化未清，狱讼未衰息，赋敛日重，府库<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164988", 1164988, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>空竭</span>，而大者又有二虏之不臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164988_comment'></div>天子震怒，大臣忧恐，自两制以上宜皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164988", 1164988, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>苦心</span>焦思，日夜思念，求所以解吾君之忧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164988_comment'></div>洵自惟闲人，于国家无丝毫之责，得以优游终岁，咏歌先王之道以自乐，时或作为文章，亦不求人知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164988_comment'></div>以为天下方事事，而王公大人岂暇见我哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164988_comment'></div>是以踰年在京师，而其平生所愿见如君侯者，未尝一至其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164988_comment'></div>有来告洵以所欲见之之意，洵不敢不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164988_comment'></div>然不知君侯见之而何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164988_comment'></div>天子求治如此之急，君侯为两制大臣，岂欲见一闲布衣，与之论闲事邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164988_comment'></div>此洵所以不敢遽见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164988_comment'></div>自闲居十年，人事<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164988", 1164988, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>荒废</span>，渐不喜承迎将逢，拜伏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1164988", 1164988, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>拳跽</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164988_comment'></div>王公大人茍能无以此求之，使得从容坐隅，时出其所学，或亦有足观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164988_comment'></div>今君侯辱先求之，此其必有所异乎世俗者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164988_comment'></div>孟子曰：「段干木踰垣而避之，泄柳闭门而不纳，是皆已甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164988_comment'></div>迫，斯可以见矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164988_comment'></div>呜呼，吾岂斯人之徒欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164988_comment'></div>欲见我而见之，不欲见而徐去之，何伤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164988_comment'></div>况如君侯，平生所愿见者，又何辞焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164988_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164988_comment'></div>洵再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1164988_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年1月</a>　正月，以翰林学士欧阳修知贡举。苏洵子轼、辙应省试。轼之《刑赏忠厚之至论》为梅尧臣、欧阳修所赏，置轼第二。辙同中第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年3月</a>　三月，仁宗御试崇政殿。赐进士章衡等二百六十二人及第，一百二十六人同出身。苏洵二子轼、辙皆进士及第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　苏洵喜二子轼、辙登进士第。轼、辙念母氏抚教，期母寿康。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年4月7日</a>　四月七日，苏洵妻程氏卒。洵父子三人仓惶返蜀。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f7cb3c34d7dd4eeea508df8f4b8591b9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f7cb3c34d7dd4eeea508df8f4b8591b9");'><span id='f7cb3c34d7dd4eeea508df8f4b8591b9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>，52岁</div><div id='f7cb3c34d7dd4eeea508df8f4b8591b9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　苏洵父子吊朱亥墓。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年2月15日</a>　二月十五日，苏洵父子到京师，赁居西冈一宅子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　在开封。苏洵有《上余青州书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十一。此文作于嘉祐五年二月至六年五月之间，但具体时间不详，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1164979' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164979' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164979?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上余青州书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164979")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164979_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164979'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164979'>洵闻之，楚人高令尹子文之行曰：「三以为令尹而不喜，三夺其令尹而不怒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164979_comment'></div>其为令尹也，楚人为之喜，而其去令尹也，楚人为之怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164979_comment'></div>己不期为令尹，而令尹自至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164979_comment'></div>夫令尹子文岂独恶夫富贵哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164979_comment'></div>知其不可以求得，而安其自得，是以喜怒不及其心，而人为之嚣嚣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164979_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164979_comment'></div>岂亦不足以见己大而人小邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164979_comment'></div>脱然为弃于人，而不知弃之为悲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164979_comment'></div>纷然为取于人，而不知取之为乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164979_comment'></div>人自为弃我、取我，而吾之所以为我者如一，则亦不足以高视天下而窃笑矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164979_comment'></div>昔者，明公之初自奋于南海之滨，而为天下之名卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164979_comment'></div>当其盛时，激昂慷慨，论得失，定可否，左摩西羌，右揣契丹，奉使千里，弹压强悍不屈之虏，其辩如决河流而东注诸海，名声四溢于中原，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1164979", 1164979, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>滂薄</span>于戎狄之国，可谓至盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164979_comment'></div>及至中废，而为海滨之匹夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164979_comment'></div>盖其间十有馀年，明公无求于人，而人亦无求于明公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164979_comment'></div>其后，适会南蛮纵横放肆，充斥万里，而莫之或救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164979_comment'></div>明公乃起于民伍之中，折尺箠而笞之，不旋踵而南方乂安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164979_comment'></div>夫明公岂有求而为之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164979_comment'></div>适会事变以成大功，功成而爵禄至，明公之于进退之事，盖亦绰绰乎有馀裕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164979_comment'></div>悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164979_comment'></div>世俗之人纷纷于富贵之间而不知自止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164979_comment'></div>达者安于逸乐而习为高岸之节，顾视四海饥寒穷困之士，莫不颦蹙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1164979", 1164979, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>呕哕</span>而不乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164979_comment'></div>穷者藜藿不饱，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1164979", 1164979, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>布褐</span>不暖，习为贫贱之所摧折，仰望贵人之辉光，则为之颠倒而失措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164979_comment'></div>此二人者，皆不可与语于轻富贵而安贫贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164979_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164979_comment'></div>彼不知贫富贵贱之正味也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164979_comment'></div>夫惟天下之习于富贵之荣，而忸于贫贱之辱者，而后可与语此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164979_comment'></div>今夫天下之所以奔走于富贵者，我知之矣，而不敢以告人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164979_comment'></div>富贵之极，止于天子之相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164979_comment'></div>而天子之相，果谁为之名？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164979_comment'></div>岂天为之名邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164979_comment'></div>其无乃亦人之自相名邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164979_comment'></div>夫天下之官，上自三公，至于卿、大夫，而下至于士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164979_comment'></div>此四人者，皆人之所自为也，而人亦自贵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164979_comment'></div>天下以为此四者绝群离类，特立于天下而不可几近，则不亦大惑矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164979_comment'></div>盍亦反其本而思之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164979_comment'></div>夫此四名者，其初盖出于天下之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164979_comment'></div>出其私意以自相号呼者而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164979_comment'></div>夫此四名者，果出于人之私意所以自相号呼也，则夫世之所谓贤人君子者，亦何以异此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164979_comment'></div>有才者为贤人，而有德者为君子，此二名者夫岂轻也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164979_comment'></div>而今世之士得为君子者，一为世之所弃，则以为不若一命士之贵，而况以与三公争哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164979_comment'></div>且夫明公昔者之伏于南海，与夫今者之为东诸侯也，君子岂有间于其间？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1164979_comment'></div>而明公亦岂有以自轻而自重哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1164979_comment'></div>洵以为明公之习于富贵之荣，而狃于贫贱之辱，其尝之也，盖以多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1164979_comment'></div>是以极言至此，而无所迂曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1164979_comment'></div>洵，西蜀之匹夫，尝有志于当世，因循不遇，遂至于老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1164979_comment'></div>然其尝所欲见者，天下之士盖有五六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1164979_comment'></div>五六人者已略见矣，而独明公之未尝见，每以为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1164979_comment'></div>今明公来朝，而洵适在此，是以不得不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1164979_comment'></div>伏惟加察，幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1164979_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　自江陵至京师，苏洵父子三人途中所为诗文又七十三篇，为《南行后集》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南行后集》原收诗文共七十三篇（首），现存五十二篇（首）。所存诗文中，苏洵诗六首、苏轼诗文三十八篇（首）、苏辙诗八首。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年6月14日</a>　在开封。六月十四日，苏洵作《祭姪位文》作品：《祭侄位文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165095' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165095' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165095?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭侄位文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年6月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165095")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165095_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165095'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165095'>嘉祐五年六月十四日，叔洵以家馔酒果祭于亡侄之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165095_comment'></div>昔汝之生，后余五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165095_comment'></div>余虽汝叔父，而幼与汝同戏，如兄弟然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165095_comment'></div>其后，余日以长，汝亦以壮大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165095_comment'></div>余适四方，而汝留故国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165095_comment'></div>余既归止，汝乃随汝仲叔旅居东都，十有三岁而不还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165095_comment'></div>今余来东，汝遂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1165095", 1165095, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>溘然</span>至死而不救，此岂非天邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165095_comment'></div>嗟夫，数十年之间，与汝出处参差不齐，曾不如其幼之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165095_comment'></div>方将与汝旅于此，汝又一旦而殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165095_comment'></div>人事之变，何其反覆而与人相违？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165095_comment'></div>嗟余伯兄，其后之存者，今日以往，独汝季弟与汝之二孺，此所以使余增悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165095_comment'></div>汝殁之五日，汝家将殡汝于京城之西郊，魂如有知，于此永别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165095_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1165095_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　欧阳修向仁宗皇帝荐举苏洵。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b44bb2e691374bff87b2779bedaf8bb8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b44bb2e691374bff87b2779bedaf8bb8");'><span id='b44bb2e691374bff87b2779bedaf8bb8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1066')">1062-1066年</a>，54-58岁</div><div id='b44bb2e691374bff87b2779bedaf8bb8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　秋，杨克从碑成。碑文苏洵撰，应克从之孙申之请。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年8月</a>　八月乙亥（初一日），苏洵仲兄涣卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　时苏洵、苏辙与黎錞（希声）为邻，居太学前。欧阳修尝盛称“文行苏洵，经术黎錞”，以为蜀士之表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　苏洵父子尝闻欧阳修谈吏事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。吴中复（仲庶）知潭州，苏洵作送行诗。作品：《送吴待制中复知潭州二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134136' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134136' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134136?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送吴待制中复知潭州二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134136")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_134136_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134136'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134136'>十年尝作犍为令，四脉尝闻悯俗诗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134136'>共叹才高堪御史，果能忠谏致戎麾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134136'>会稽特欲荣翁子，冯翊犹将试望之。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134136'>船系河堤无几日，南公应已悭<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作怪）</span>来迟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134136'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_134136_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_134135' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134135' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134135?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_134135_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134135'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134135'>台省留身凡几岁，江湖得郡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>喜今行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134135'>卧听晓鼓朝眠稳，行入淮流乡味生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134135'>细雨满村莼菜长，高风吹旆䌽船狞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134135'>到家应有壶觞劳，倚赖比邻不畏卿。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134135'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_134135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_134135'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_134135_0'>⑴ 原作群，据康熙本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_134135_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　苏洵借人雷琴，弹之。辙有诗，轼次韵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年4月23日</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。四月二十三日，苏洵上宰相韩琦书，论仁宗山陵。作品：《上韩昭文论山陵书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1164990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上韩昭文论山陵书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年4月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164990")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164990_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164990'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164990'>四月二十三日，将仕郎、守霸州文安县主簿、礼院编纂苏洵，惶恐再拜上书昭文相公执事：洵本布衣书生，才无所长，相公不察而辱收之，使与百执事之末，平居思所以仰报盛德，而不获其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164990_comment'></div>今者，先帝新弃万国，天子始亲政事，当海内倾耳之秋，而相公实为社稷柱石莫先之臣，有百世不磨之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164990_comment'></div>伏惟相公将何以处之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164990_comment'></div>古者天子即位，天下之政必有所不及安席而先行之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164990_comment'></div>盖汉昭即位，休息百役，与天下更始，故其为天子曾未逾月，而恩泽下布于海内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164990_comment'></div>窃惟当今之事，天下之所谓最急，而天子之所宜先行者，辄敢以告于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164990_comment'></div>窃见先帝以俭德临天下，在位四十馀年，而宫室游观无所增加，帏簿器皿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164990", 1164990, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>弊陋</span>而不易，天下称颂以为文景之所不若，今一旦奄弃臣下，而有司乃欲以末世葬送无益之费，侵削先帝休息长养之民，掇取厚葬之名而遗之，以累其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1164990", 1164990, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>盛明</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164990_comment'></div>故洵以为当今之议，莫若薄葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164990_comment'></div>窃闻顷者癸酉赦书既出，郡县无以赏兵，例皆贷钱于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164990_comment'></div>民之有钱者，皆莫肯自输，于是有威之以刀剑，驱之以笞箠，为国结怨，仅而得之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164990_comment'></div>小民无知，不知与国同忧，方且狼顾而不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164990_comment'></div>而山陵一切配率之科又以复下，计今不过秋冬之间，海内必将骚然，有不自聊赖之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164990_comment'></div>窃惟先帝平昔之所以爱惜百姓者如此其深，而其所以检身节俭者如此其至也，推其平生之心而计其既没之意，则其不欲以山陵重困天下，亦已明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164990_comment'></div>而臣下乃独为此过当逾礼之费，以拂戾其平生之意，窃所不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164990_comment'></div>且使今府库之中，财用有馀，一物不取于民，尽公力而为之，以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164990", 1164990, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>称遂</span>臣子不忍之心，犹且获讥于圣人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164990_comment'></div>况夫空虚无有，一金以上非取于民则不获，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164990", 1164990, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>冒行</span>不顾，以徇近世失中之礼，亦已惑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164990_comment'></div>然议者必将以为古者君子不以天下俭其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164990_comment'></div>以天下之大，而不足于先帝之葬，于人情有所不顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164990_comment'></div>洵亦以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164990_comment'></div>使今俭葬而用墨子之说，则是过也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164990_comment'></div>不废先王之礼，而去近世无益之费，是不过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164990_comment'></div>子思曰：「三日而殡，凡附于身者必诚必信，勿之有悔焉耳矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164990_comment'></div>三月而葬，凡附于棺者必诚必信，勿之有悔焉耳矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164990_comment'></div>古之人所由以尽其诚信者，不敢有略也，而外是者则略之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164990_comment'></div>昔者华元厚葬其君，君子以为不臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164990_comment'></div>汉文葬于霸陵，木不改列，藏无金玉，天下以为圣明，而后世安于太山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164990_comment'></div>故曰莫若建薄葬之议，上以遂先帝恭俭之诚，下以纾百姓目前之患，内以解华元不臣之讥，而万世之后以固山陵不拔之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164990_comment'></div>洵窃观古者厚葬之由，未有非其时君之不达，欲以金玉厚其亲于地下，而其臣下不能禁止，僶俛而从之者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164990_comment'></div>未有如今日之事，太后至明，天子至圣，而有司信近世之礼，而遂为之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164990_comment'></div>是可深惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164990_comment'></div>且夫相公既已立不世之功矣，而何爱一时之劳而无所建明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164990_comment'></div>洵恐世之清议，将有任其责者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164990_comment'></div>如曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1164990", 1164990, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>诏敕</span>已行，制度已定，虽知不便，而不可复改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164990_comment'></div>则此又过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164990_comment'></div>盖唐太宗之葬高祖也，欲为九丈之坟，而用汉氏长陵之制，百事务从丰厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1164990_comment'></div>及群臣建议以为不可，于是改从光武之陵，高不过六丈，而每事俭约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1164990_comment'></div>夫君子之为政，与其坐视百姓之艰难而重改令之非，孰若改令以救百姓之急？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1164990_comment'></div>不胜区区之心，敢辄以告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1164990_comment'></div>惟恕其狂易之诛，幸甚，幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1164990_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1164990_comment'></div>洵惶恐再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1164990_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　本岁，在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。苏洵作《辨奸论》刺王安石，洵之子轼、辙有“嘻其甚矣”之叹。元丰初，张方平（安道、文定）盛赞之，载其文于洵之《墓表》。苏轼有谢书。清临川人李绂、金溪人蔡上翔以为文非苏洵作。今人邓广铭祖李、王之说，亦以为此文非苏洵作。论争遂起，以迄于今。然此文实为洵所作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1165071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165071?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辨奸论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165071")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165071'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165071'>事有必至，理有固然，惟天下之静者乃能见微而知著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165071_comment'></div>月晕而风，础润而雨，人人知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165071_comment'></div>人事之推移，理势之相因，其疏阔而难知，变化而不可测者，孰与天地阴阳之事，而贤者有不知其故，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165071_comment'></div>好恶乱其中而利害夺其外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165071_comment'></div>昔者山巨源见王衍曰：「误天下苍生者，必此人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165071_comment'></div>郭汾阳见卢杞曰：「此人得志，吾子孙无遗类矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165071_comment'></div>自今而言之，其理固有可见者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165071_comment'></div>以吾观之，王衍之为人，容貌言语固有以欺世而盗名者，然不忮不求，与物浮沉，使晋无惠帝，仅得中主，虽衍百千，何从而乱天下乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165071_comment'></div>卢杞之奸，固足以败国，然而不学无文，容貌不足以动人，言语不足以眩世，非德宗之鄙暗，亦何从而用之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165071_comment'></div>由是言之，二公之料二子，亦容有未必然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165071_comment'></div>今有人口诵孔、老之言，身履夷、齐之行，收召好名之士、不得志之人，相与造作言语，私立名字，以为颜渊、孟轲复出，而阴贼险狠，与人异趣，是王衍、卢杞合而为一人也，其祸岂可胜言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165071_comment'></div>夫面垢不忘洗，衣垢不忘濣，此人之至情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165071_comment'></div>今也不然，衣臣虏之衣，食犬彘之食，囚首丧面而谈《诗》、《书》，此岂其情也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165071_comment'></div>凡事之不近人情者，鲜不为大奸慝，竖刁、易牙、开方是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165071_comment'></div>以盖世之名而济其未形之患，虽有愿治之主，好贤之相，犹将举而用之，则其为天下患必然而无疑者，非特二子之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165071_comment'></div>孙子曰：「善用兵者无赫赫之功」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165071_comment'></div>使斯人而不用也，则吾言为过，而斯人有不遇之叹，孰知其祸之至于此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165071_comment'></div>不然，天下将被其祸，而吾获知言之名，悲夫！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1165071_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。《六家谥法》二十卷编成，上书。此书乃范镇、周沆编，姚闢与其事。既成，苏洵撰《上六家谥议》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《六家谥法》为著作，苏洵参与编写。）</span>《上六家谥议》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注·佚文》）</span><div id='poem_1164973' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164973' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164973?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上六家谥法议</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐六年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164973")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164973_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164973'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164973'>谨按世之以谥著书而可以名家者止于六家，其王彦威之徒皆祖述旧文，无所增损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164973_comment'></div>六家之中，其名《周公》者最无条贯，同谥异条，或分见数处，纷纭杂乱，难以省览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164973_comment'></div>其馀《春秋》、《广谥》、沈约、贺琛、扈蒙，虽纲目具存，而脱谬已甚，或当时之妄误，或传写之讹失，有司行用，实难依据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164973_comment'></div>臣等今已讲求别本，證之史传，别其同异，去其重复，刊谬补缺，务令完正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164973_comment'></div>其有讹谬已久，世俗承用不复疑，如以「壮」为「庄」，以「僭」为「替」，如是者亦不敢辄改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164973_comment'></div>皆随件加注，凡注数十百条，号曰《六家谥法》二十卷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1164973_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。苏洵撰《谥法总论》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见曾枣庄、刘琳主编《全宋文》第43册第160页。）</span><div id='poem_1165073' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165073' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165073?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谥法总论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165073")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165073_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165073'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165073'>嘉祐六年七月，诏修礼书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165073_comment'></div>十月，诏古谥法有不可用者，以属修书之吏，臣洵实典其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165073_comment'></div>按始论谥者起于今文《周书·谥法》之篇，今文既以鄙野不传，其《谥法》之上篇独存，又简略不备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165073_comment'></div>诸儒所传又有《周公》、《春秋》、《广谥》、沈约、贺琛、扈蒙六家之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165073_comment'></div>《周公》、《春秋》为名尤古，然条贯尤为杂乱而不精，《广谥》又疏略而不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165073_comment'></div>独沈约、贺琛纪纲粗备，然琛好加以己意，务为多而无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165073_comment'></div>扈蒙最后出，酌取诸家，简而不精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165073_comment'></div>六书之中，稍近古而可据者，莫如沈约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165073_comment'></div>然亦非古之《谥法》，约言之详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165073_comment'></div>其最旧者见于《世本》、《大戴礼》，而约之时已不见于其书，约徒得刘熙《乘奥》之所增广<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165073_comment'></div>与《广谥》以为据依，不闻有所谓《周公》、《春秋》者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165073_comment'></div>琛又因约，而加之以其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165073_comment'></div>今《周公》、《春秋》之法，往往反取琛之新法而载之其书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165073_comment'></div>至王彦威、苏冕之书，因前人之法，附世人之谥，非有他也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165073_comment'></div>贾山有言：「古者圣王作谥，不过三四十字」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165073_comment'></div>而蔡邕《独断》所载，亦不过四十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165073_comment'></div>臣受诏之三年二月，而《谥法》乃定，凡一百六十有八<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165073_comment'></div>贺琛之法有君谥、臣谥、妇人谥，离而为三，今取而合之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165073_comment'></div>妇人有谥自周景王之穆后始，匹夫有谥自东汉之隐者始，宦者有谥自东汉之孙程始，蛮夷有谥自东汉之莎车始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165073_comment'></div>自《周公》以来，籍而记之，为三十五卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165073_comment'></div>善者可以劝，恶者可以惧，善恶之失当者可以长叹息也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1165073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1165073'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_1165073_2'>⑴ 今隋唐《志》作《帝王本纪》，《隋书》又作《来奥》，未知孰是。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_1165073_0'>⑵ 沈约为《谥例》，记周以来帝王公卿之谥，至宋而止。王彦威继之，至唐而止。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1165073_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。苏洵撰《论诸家谥法》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见曾枣庄、刘琳主编《全宋文》第43册第161页。）</span><div id='poem_1165074' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165074' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165074?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论诸家谥法</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165074")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165074_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165074'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165074'>周公之书，文尤繁杂不经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165074_comment'></div>《春秋》次之，比周公甚简，而微为不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165074_comment'></div>《广谥》最简，比二书差为齐一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165074_comment'></div>沈约所取以成书，约采诸家，其书最详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165074_comment'></div>贺琛因而增之，尤详备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165074_comment'></div>而皆病于无所去取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165074_comment'></div>扈蒙新书，其意妄伪，反为五家之所非笑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1165074_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　沈括记苏洵言张詠（乖崖、忠定）知成都时礼成都府知录参军事。洵或晤沈括。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。从叔母杨氏卒，苏洵作挽词。作品：《从叔母杨氏挽词》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span>《从叔母杨氏挽词之二》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见刘尚荣《苏洵佚诗辑考》）</span><div id='poem_134132' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134132' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134132?labeling=true' "poem_title_134132")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_134132_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134132'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134132'>几年赠命涵幽壤，当有铭文记德音。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
