id='poem_sentence_0_134153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134153'>辞嚣乞静得此守，走兔入薮鱼投津。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134153'>徐州绝胜不须问，请问项籍何去秦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134153'>江山雄豪不相下，衣锦游戏欲及晨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134153'>霸王事业今已矣，但有太守朱两轮。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134153'>还乡据势与古并，岂有汉戟窥城闉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134153'>论安较利乃公胜，行矣正及汴水匀。<div id='poem_title_1165084' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165084?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴道子画五星赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1165084_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165084'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165084'>世称善画，曹兴、张繇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1165084'>墙破纸烂，兵火所烧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1165084'>至于有唐，道子姓吴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1165084'>独称一时，蔑张与曹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1165084'>历岁数百，其有几何？<div id='poem_sentence_4_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1165084'>或镵于碑，以获不磨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1165084'>吾世贫窭，非有富豪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1165084'>堂堂五行，道子所摹。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1165084'>岁星居前，不武不挑。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1165084'>求之古人，其有帝尧。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1165084'>盛服佩剑，其容昭昭。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1165084'>荧惑惟南，左弓右刀。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1165084'>赫烈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1165084", 1165084, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>奋怒</span>，木石焚焦。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1165084'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1165084", 1165084, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>震怛</span>下土，莫敢有骄。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1165084'>崔崔土星，瘦而长腰。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1165084'>四方远游，去如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1165084", 1165084, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>飞飙</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1165084'>倏忽万里，远莫可昭。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1165084'>太白惟将，宜其壮夫。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1165084'>今惟妇人，长裙飘飘，抱抚四弦，如声嘈嘈。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1165084'>辰星北方，不丽不妖。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1165084'>执笔与纸，凝然不嚣。<div id='poem_sentence_20_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1165084'>妆非今人，唇傅黑膏。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1165084'>唯是五星，笔势莫高。<div id='poem_sentence_22_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1165084'>愈后愈远，知其若何？<div id='poem_sentence_25_1165084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1165084'>吾茍不言，是亦不遭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1165084_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。文同（与可）许惠赠苏洵所画舒景，洵作诗督之。作品：《与可许惠所画舒景以诗督之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》）</span><div id='poem_134143' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134143' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134143?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与可许惠所画舒景以诗督之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134143")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134143_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134143'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134143'>枯松怪石霜竹枝，中有可爱知者谁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134143_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134143'>我能知之不能说，欲说常恐天真非。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134143_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134143'>羡君笔端有新意，倏忽万状成一挥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134143_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134143'>使我忘言惟独笑，意所欲说辄见之。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134143_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134143'>问胡为然笑不答，无乃君亦难为辞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134143_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　苏洵尝以仁宗欲率百官朝正章献太后事质之欧阳修。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。苏洵《嘉祐谥法》三卷撰成。上之朝廷不用。郑樵称其书为前人所不及。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《嘉祐谥法》为编著，共三卷。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。苏洵《皇祐谥录》编成。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《皇祐谥录》为编著，久佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　欧阳修与苏洵简，赞洵所撰《谥法》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。蜀僧去尘返蜀，苏洵作送行诗。作品：《送蜀僧去尘》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》、《类编增广老苏先生大全文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_134137' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134137' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134137?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送蜀僧去尘</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134137")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_134137_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134137'><div class='poemSentence' target='_blank'>香</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134157")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_134157_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134157'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134157'>捣麝筛檀入范模，润分薇露合鸡苏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134157'>一丝吐出青烟细，半炷烧成玉箸粗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134157'>道士每占经次第，佳人惟验绣工夫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134157'>轩窗几席随宜用，不待高擎鹊尾炉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 清邵仁泓刻《苏老泉先生全集》卷一六</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_134157_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。苏洵作《藤樽》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134173' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134173' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134173?labeling=true' target='_blank'>藤樽</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134173")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134173_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134173'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134173'>枯藤生幽谷，蹙缩似无材。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134173'>不意犹为累，刳中作酒杯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134173'>君知我好异，赠我酌村醅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134173'>衰意方多感，为君当数开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134173'>藤樽结如螺，村酒绿如水。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134173'>开樽自献酬，竟日成野醉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134173'>青莎可为席，白石可为几<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作机）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134173'>何当酌清泉，永以思君子。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134173'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_134173_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年9月3日</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。九月辛酉（初三日），《太常因革礼》修成。欧阳修提举编纂此书。赐修及苏洵等银帛。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《太常因革礼》为编著，苏洵参与编著。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年9月9日</a>　在开封，为霸州文安县主簿。九月九日重阳节，韩琦（魏公）宴客，苏洵与。琦赋诗，洵归寓所后次琦韵。作品：《九日和韩公》<span id='poem_sentence_1_1165000_comment'></div>承惠教，祇增愧悚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165000_comment'></div>晴暖，尊体佳胜。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　杜叔元（君懿）藏许敬宗之砚，苏洵求之，叔元不可。<br /><a href="javascript: class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164999'>久承借示新文，及累为临访，甚荷勤眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164999_comment'></div>文字已细观，甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164999_comment'></div>必欲求所未至，如《中正论》引舜为證，此是时文之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164999_comment'></div>凡论但意立而理明，不必觅事应副，诚未思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164999_comment'></div>专此不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164999_comment'></div>洵白。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1164999_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1164999'><span class='label'>按：</span>《嘉祐集》卷一三，影印文渊阁四库全书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1164999_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年</a>　时范镇（景仁）在陈州，梦苏洵来告别。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年4月25日</a>　四月戊申（二十五日），苏洵卒。<br /></div>

-----title
西安（长安）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='381a79e7986848feb31e2022fb8d152a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("381a79e7986848feb31e2022fb8d152a");'><span id='381a79e7986848feb31e2022fb8d152a_link' class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》（苏洵著，曾枣庄、金成礼笺注。上海古籍出版社1993年3月第1版。下同）卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134142' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134142' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134142?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上田待制诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134142")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134142_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134142'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134142'>日落长安道，大野渺荒荒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134142'>吁嗟秦皇帝，安得不富强。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134142'>山大地脉厚，小民十尺长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134142'>耕田破万顷，一稔粟柱梁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134142'>少年事游侠，皆可荷弩枪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134142'>勇力不自骄，颇能啖乾粮。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134142'>天意此有谓，故使连西羌。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134142'>古人遭边患，累累斗两刚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134142'>方今正似此，猛士强如狼。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134142'>跨马负弓矢，走不择涧冈。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134142'>脱甲森不顾，袒裼搏敌场。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134142'>嗟彼谁治此，踧踧不敢当。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134142'>当之负重责，无成不朝王。<div id='poem_sentence_12_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_134142'>田侯本儒生，武略今洸洸。<div id='poem_sentence_13_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_134142'>右手握麈尾，指麾据胡床。<div id='poem_sentence_14_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_134142'>郡国远浩浩，边鄙有积仓。<div id='poem_sentence_15_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_134142'>秦境古何在，秦人多战伤。<div id='poem_sentence_16_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_134142'>此事久不报，此时将何偿。<div id='poem_sentence_17_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_134142'>得此报天子，为侯歌之章。<div id='poem_sentence_18_134142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_134142'></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_134142_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b5fae00cca424ef19f5bc3ccfe259943_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b5fae00cca424ef19f5bc3ccfe259943");'><span id='b5fae00cca424ef19f5bc3ccfe259943_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　苏洵过长安，见石昌言。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='acd6a386464444598ccbf4a90576a8fa_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，48岁</div><div id='acd6a386464444598ccbf4a90576a8fa' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>至长安，苏洵上王拱辰书。作品：《上王长安书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1164985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164985?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上王长安书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164985")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164985'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164985'>判府左丞阁下：天下无事，天子甚尊，公卿甚贵，士甚贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164985_comment'></div>从士而逆数之，至于天子，其积也甚厚，其为变也甚难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164985_comment'></div>是故天子之尊至于不可指，而士之卑至于可杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164985_comment'></div>呜呼，见其安而不见其危，如此而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164985_comment'></div>卫懿公之死，非其无人也，以鹤辞而不与战也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164985_comment'></div>方其未败也，天下之士望为其鹤而不可得也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164985_comment'></div>及其败也，思以千乘之国与匹夫共之而不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164985_comment'></div>人知其卒之至于如此，则天子之尊可以慄慄于上，而士之卑可以肆志于下，又焉敢以势言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164985_comment'></div>故夫士之贵贱，其势在天子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164985_comment'></div>天子之存亡，其权在士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164985_comment'></div>世衰道丧，天下之士学之不明，持之不坚，于是始以天子存亡之权，下而就一匹夫贵贱之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164985_comment'></div>甚矣夫，天下之惑也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164985_comment'></div>持千金之璧以易一瓦缶，几何其不举而弃诸沟也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164985_comment'></div>古之君子，其道相为徒，其徒相为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164985_comment'></div>故一夫不用乎此，则天下之士相率而去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164985_comment'></div>使夫上之人有失天下士之忧，而后有失一士之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164985_comment'></div>今之君子，幸其徒之不用，以茍容其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164985_comment'></div>故其始也轻用之，而其终也亦轻去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164985_comment'></div>呜呼，其亦何便于此也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164985_comment'></div>当今之世，非有贤公卿不能振其前，非有贤士不能奋其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164985_comment'></div>洵从蜀来，明日将至长安，见明公而东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164985_comment'></div>伏惟读其书而察其心，以轻重其礼，幸甚幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1164985_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在长安，苏洵晤都漕傅求，临行，赠以诗。作品：《途次长安上都漕傅谏议》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134158' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134158' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134158?labeling=true' target='_blank'>途次长安上都漕傅谏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134158")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134158_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134158'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134158'>丈夫正多念，老大自不<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作不自）</span>安。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134158'>居家不能乐，忽忽思中原。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134158'>慨然弃乡庐，劫劫道路间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134158'>穷山多虎狼，行路非不难。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134158'>昔者倦奔走，闭门事耕田。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134158'>蚕谷聊自给，如此已十年。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134158'>缅怀当今人，草草无复闲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134158'>坚卧固不起，芒刺<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作背）</span>实在肩。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134158'>布衣与食肉<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作肉食）</span>，幸可交口言。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134158'>默默不以告，未可遽罪愆。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134158'>驱车入京洛，藩镇皆达官。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134158'>长安逢傅侯，愿得说肺肝。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134158'>贫贱吾老矣，不复苦自叹。<div id='poem_sentence_12_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_134158'>富贵不足爱，浮云过长天。<div id='poem_sentence_13_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_134158'>中怀邈有念，惝恍难自论。<div id='poem_sentence_14_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_134158'>世俗不见信，排斥仅得存。<div id='poem_sentence_15_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_134158'>昨者东入秦，大麦黄满田。<div id='poem_sentence_16_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_134158'>秦民可无饥，为君喜不眠。<div id='poem_sentence_17_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_134158'>禁军几千万，仰此填其咽。<div id='poem_sentence_18_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_134158'>西蕃久不反，老贼非常然。<div id='poem_sentence_19_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_134158'>士饱可以战，吾宁为之先。<div id='poem_sentence_20_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_134158'>傅侯君在西，天子忧东藩。<div id='poem_sentence_21_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_134158'>烽火尚未灭，何策安西边。<div id='poem_sentence_22_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_134158'>傅侯君谓何，明日将东辕。<div id='poem_sentence_23_134158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_134158'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_134158_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
九江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='382b43c2376e41cebb9637ae3e94ac02_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("382b43c2376e41cebb9637ae3e94ac02");'><span id='382b43c2376e41cebb9637ae3e94ac02_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>，39岁</div><div id='382b43c2376e41cebb9637ae3e94ac02' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　苏洵游庐山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　苏洵游圆通禅院，讷禅师、景福顺公与游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年5月11日</a>　苏洵南游期间，五月十一日，父序卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　约在江州。苏洵南游，暑中，答友人提举监丞简。先是道中与提举监丞简，提举监丞来简，乃答之。作品：《与提举监丞帖》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《眉山苏氏三世书翰·苏洵第一简》；此文收入曾枣庄、刘琳主编《全宋文》（上海辞书出版社、安徽教育出版社2006年版第43册第51页）此条活动具体地点不详，姑系于此。苏洵“道中”简已佚。）</span><div id='poem_1165001' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165001' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165001?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与提举监丞帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165001")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165001_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165001'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165001'>洵顿首再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165001_comment'></div>昨日道中草草上记，方以为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165001_comment'></div>介使□武伏奉教翰，所以眷藉勤厚，见于累纸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165001_comment'></div>感服情眷，愧怍益甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165001_comment'></div>晨兴薄凉，伏惟台候万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165001_comment'></div>洵以病暑加眩，意思极不佳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165001_comment'></div>所以涉水迂涂，不敢入城府者，畏人事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165001_comment'></div>宠谕常每每行仰戢爱，与之重深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165001_comment'></div>欲力疾少承绪言，但闻台候不甚清快，冒暑远行非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165001_comment'></div>兼水浸道涂，恐今晚亦未能至彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165001_comment'></div>虚烦大旆之出，曷若相忘于江湖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165001_comment'></div>不过廿日后便可承颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165001_comment'></div>或同涂为鄱阳之行，如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165001_comment'></div>更几见察，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165001_comment'></div>匆匆拜此，不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165001_comment'></div>洵顿首再拜，提举监丞兄台坐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1165001_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
鄱阳

-----title
南昌

-----title
赣州
-----detail

-----title

-----title

-----title
渑池
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8a3c13eba92e4739adebc9f8a770961d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8a3c13eba92e4739adebc9f8a770961d");'><span id='8a3c13eba92e4739adebc9f8a770961d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，48岁</div><div id='8a3c13eba92e4739adebc9f8a770961d' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏洵父子经华清宫，出关中，至渑池。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>约在渑池。苏洵东往京师途中，遇故人陈公美。公美赠诗，洵答之。作品：《答陈公美》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。陈公美时在豫西一带为官，具体地点不详，苏洵诗姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_134167' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134167' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134167?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答陈公美</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134167")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134167_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134167'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134167'>少壮事已远，旧交良可怀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134167'>百年能几何，十载不得偕。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134167'>念昔居乡里，游处了无猜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134167'>饮食不相舍，谈笑久所陪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134167'>拜君以为兄，分密谁能开。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134167'>齿发俱未老，未至衰与颓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134167'>我子在襁褓，君犹无婴孩。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134167'>君后独舍去，为吏天一涯。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134167'>我又厌奔走，远引不复来。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134167'>岁月杳难恃，区区老吾侪。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134167'>况从与君别，多事岁若排。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134167'>心力不能救，衰病侵筋骸。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134167'>二子皆已冠，如吾苦无才。<div id='poem_sentence_12_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_134167'>君亦已有嗣，眉目秀且佳。<div id='poem_sentence_13_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_134167'>人事知几变，会合终不谐。<div id='poem_sentence_14_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_134167'>昨者本不出，豪杰苦自咍。<div id='poem_sentence_15_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_134167'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_134167", 134167, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>郁郁</span>自不乐，谁为子悲哀。<div id='poem_sentence_16_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_134167'>翻然感其说，东走陵巅崖。<div id='poem_sentence_17_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_134167'>不意君在此，得奉笑与诙。<div id='poem_sentence_18_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_134167'>君颜蔚如故，大噱飞尘灰。<div id='poem_sentence_19_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_134167'>我老应可怪，白髭生<span class='inlineComment2'>（康熙本作发垂）</span>两腮。<div id='poem_sentence_20_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_134167'>新句辱先赠，古诗许见推。<div id='poem_sentence_21_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_134167'>贤俊非独步，故旧每所乖。<div id='poem_sentence_22_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_134167'>作诗报嘉贶，亦聊以相催。<div id='poem_sentence_23_134167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_134167'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_134167_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>约在渑池。陈公美来诗，苏洵复答之。作品：《又答陈公美三首》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。陈公美时在豫西一带为官，具体地点不详，苏洵诗姑系于此。）</span>《又答陈公美三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134166' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134166' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134166?labeling=true' id='poem_content_134166'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134166'>仲尼鲁司寇，官职亦已优。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134166'>从祭肉不及，戴冕奔诸侯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134166'>当时不之知，为肉诚可羞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134166'>君子意有在，众人但愆尤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134166'>置之待后世，皎皎无足忧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134166'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_134166_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_134165' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134165' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134165?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134165'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134165'>仲尼为群婢，一走十四年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134165'>荀卿老不出，五十干诸田。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134165'>顾彼二<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_3_134165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134165'>彼亦诚自信，谁能恤多言。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134165'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_134165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_134165'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_134165_0'>⑴ id='poem_title_134164_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134164'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134164'>公孙昔放逐，牧羊沧海滨。<div -----title
丰都
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='398e75f1482349569d9147e379a14582_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("398e75f1482349569d9147e379a14582");'><span id='398e75f1482349569d9147e379a14582_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>，51岁</div><div id='398e75f1482349569d9147e379a14582' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏洵父子至忠州丰都县，游仙都观。洵有题诗，并作《题仙都观》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》、《类编增广老苏先生大全文集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_134168' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134168' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134168?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题仙都观</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134168")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134168_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134168'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134168'>飘萧古仙子，寂寞苍山上。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134168'>观世眇无言，无人独惆怅。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134168'>深岩耸乔木，古观霭遗像。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134168'>超超不可揖，真意谁复亮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134168'>蜿蜒乘长龙，倏忽变万状。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134168'>朝食白云英，暮饮石髓鬯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134168'>心肝化琼玉，千岁已无恙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134168'>世人安能知，服药本虚妄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134168'>嗟哉世无人，江水空荡漾。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134168'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_134168_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏洵父子至忠州丰都县，游仙都观。洵有题诗，并作《题仙都山鹿》诗。（并叙）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》、《类编增广老苏先生大全文集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_134128' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134128' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134128?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仙都山鹿<span class='inlineComment2'>（并叙）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134128")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_134128_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134128'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134128'>客来未到何从见，昨夜数声高出云。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134128'>应是仙君老僮仆，当时掌客意犹勤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134128'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_134128_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

万州（武宁）

-----title
巫山
-----detail

-----title
巴东
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0473fa3289cd478380da19d66876402c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0473fa3289cd478380da19d66876402c");'><span id='0473fa3289cd478380da19d66876402c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>，51岁</div><div id='0473fa3289cd478380da19d66876402c' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏洵父子过巴东。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏洵经巴东时，应杨美球之请，赴江陵途中，为其父作墓志铭。与美球书，论墓志铭之作在于使死者不泯于后；论墓志铭当实书，当为亲讳。作品：《丹稜杨君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五、《苏洵集》卷二十。）</span>《与杨节推书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十三、《苏洵集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1165090' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165090' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165090?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丹棱杨君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165090")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165090_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165090'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165090'>杨君讳某，字某，世家眉之丹棱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165090_comment'></div>曾大父讳某，大父某，父某，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165090_comment'></div>君娶某氏女，生子四人：长曰美琪，次曰美琳，次曰美珣，其幼美球。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165090_comment'></div>美球尝从事安靖军，余游巴东，因以识余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165090_comment'></div>嘉祐二年某月某日，君卒，享年若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165090_comment'></div>四年十一月某日，葬于某乡某里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165090_comment'></div>将葬，从事来请余铭，以求不泯于后，余不忍逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165090_comment'></div>盖美琳先君之丧一月而卒，美琪、美珣皆志于学，而美球既仕于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165090_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1165090'>岁在己亥月在子，培高穴深托后土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165090_comment'></div>夫子骨肉归安此，生有四息三哭位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165090_comment'></div>后昆如云不胜记，其后岂不富且贵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165090_comment'></div>嘱余作铭赖其季，更千万年岂不伟？</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1165090_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1164993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164993' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164993?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与杨节推书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164993")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164993_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164993'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164993'>洵白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164993_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164993", 1164993, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>节推</span>足下：往者见托以先丈之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1164993", 1164993, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>埋铭</span>，示之以程生之行状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164993_comment'></div>洵于子之先君，耳目未尝相接，未尝辄交谈笑之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164993_comment'></div>夫古之人所为志夫其人者，知其平生，而闵其不幸以死，悲其后世之无闻，此铭之所为作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164993_comment'></div>然而不幸而不知其为人，而有人焉告之以其可铭之实，则亦不得不铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164993_comment'></div>此则铭亦可以信行状而作者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164993_comment'></div>今余不幸而不获知子之先君，所恃以作铭者，正在其行状耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164993_comment'></div>而状又不可信，嗟夫难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164993_comment'></div>然余伤夫人子之惜其先君无闻于后，以请于我；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164993_comment'></div>我既已许之，而又拒之，则无以恤乎其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164993_comment'></div>是以不敢遂已，而卒铭其墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164993_comment'></div>凡子之所欲使子之先君不朽者，兹亦足以不负子矣，谨录以进如左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164993_comment'></div>然又恐子不信行状之不可用也，故又具列于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164993_comment'></div>凡行状之所云，皆虚浮不实之事，是以不备论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164993_comment'></div>论其可指之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164993_comment'></div>行状曰：「公有子美琳，公之死由哭美琳而恸以卒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164993_comment'></div>夫子夏哭子，止于丧明，而曾子讥之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164993_comment'></div>而况以杀其身，此何可言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164993_comment'></div>余不爱夫吾言，恐其伤子先君之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164993_comment'></div>行状曰：「公戒诸子无如乡人，父母在而出分」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164993_comment'></div>夫子之乡人，谁非子之宗与子之舅甥者，而余何忍言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164993_comment'></div>而况不至于皆然，则余又何敢言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164993_comment'></div>此铭之所以不取于行状者有以也，子其无以为怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164993_comment'></div>洵白。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1164993_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
沙市（江陵）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a5fae310d79e4f7baceb911bd8286c3d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a5fae310d79e4f7baceb911bd8286c3d");'><span id='a5fae310d79e4f7baceb911bd8286c3d_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　江行途中，杨纬赠苏洵木山，洵作诗。作品：《寄杨纬》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》、《类编增广老苏先生大全文集》卷一。此条活动具体地点不详，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_134159' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134159' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134159?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄杨纬</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134159")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134159_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134159'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134159'>家居对山木，谓是忘言伴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134159'>去乡不能致，回顾颇自短。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134159'>谁知有杨子，磊落收百段。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134159'>拣赠最奇峰，慰我苦长叹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134159'>连城尽如削，邃洞幽可款。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134159'>回合抱空虚，天地耸其半。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134159'>舟行因乐载，陆挈敢辞懒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134159'>飘飘忽千里，有客来就看。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134159'>自言此地无，爱惜苦欲换。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134159'>低头笑不答，解缆风帆满。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134159'>京洛有幽居，吾将隐而玩。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年12月</a>　十二月，苏洵父子至江陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　在江陵。杨美球节推赠诗，苏洵和。作品：《和杨节推见赠》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》、《类编增广老苏先生大全文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_134148' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134148' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134148?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和杨节推见赠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134148")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134148_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134148'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134148'>与君多乖睽，邂逅同泛峡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134148'>宋子虽世旧，谈笑顷不接。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134148'>二君皆宦游，畴昔共科甲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134148'>唯我老且闲，独得离圈柙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134148'>少年实强锐，议论今<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑当作令）</span>我怯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134148'>有如乘风箭，勇发岂顾帖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134148'>置酒来相邀，慇勤为留楫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134148'>杨君旧痛饮，浅水安足涉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134148'>嗟我素不任，一酌已赪颊。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134148'>去生<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑当作去）</span>别怀怆，有子旅意惬。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134148'>舍棹治陆行，岁晚筋力乏。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134148'>予懒本不出，实为人事劫。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134148'>相将犯苦寒，大雪满马鬣。<div id='poem_sentence_12_134148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_134148'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_134148_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　在江陵。张子立寄诗来，苏洵答之。先是子立见洵于渝州途中，欲从学于洵，洵辞。作品：《答张子立见寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》、《类编增广老苏先生大全文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_134163' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134163' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134163?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答张子立见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134163")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134163_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134163'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134163'>舟行道里日夜殊，佳士恨不久与俱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134163'>峡山行尽见平楚，舍舡登岸身无虞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134163'>念君治所自有处，不复放纵如吾徒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134163'>忆昨相见巴子国，谒我江上颜何娱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134163'>求文得卷读不已，有似骏马行且且。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134163'>自言好学老未厌，方册几许鲁作鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134163'>古书今文遍天下，架上未有耿不愉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134163'>示我近所集，漫如游通衢。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134163'>通衢众所入，癃残诡怪杂沓不辨可叹吁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134163'>文人大约可数者，不过皆在众所誉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134163'>此外何足爱，刓破无四隅。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134163'>况予固鲁钝，老苍处群雏。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134163'>入赵抱五弦，客齐不吹竽。<div id='poem_sentence_12_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_134163'>山林自窜久不出，回视众俊惊锟铻。<div id='poem_sentence_13_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_134163'>岂意误见取，骐骥参羸驽。<div id='poem_sentence_14_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_134163'>将观驰骋斗雄健，无乃独不堪长途。<div id='poem_sentence_15_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_134163'>凄风腊月客荆楚，千里适魏劳奔趋。<div id='poem_sentence_16_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_134163'>将行纷乱苦无思，强说鄙意惭区区。<div id='poem_sentence_17_134163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_134163'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_134163_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　在江陵。苏洵及二子轼、辙汇江行诗文一百篇为《南行集》（《南行前集》）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此《南行集》实为《南行前集》，又名《江行唱和集》此集收三苏诗文共一百篇（首）；今存八十三首，佚十七首。所存诗文中，苏洵十篇（首）、苏轼四十六篇（首）、苏辙二十七篇（首））</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　在江陵。苏洵父子晤王荆州并其子。洵作画像赞。作品：《王荆州画像赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。此“王荆州”，其名不详。）</span><div id='poem_1165083' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165083' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165083?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王荆州画像赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165083")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1165083_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165083'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165083'>太山崇崇，东海滔滔，蟠为山东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1165083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1165083'>公惟齐人，齐方千里，而吾独见公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1165083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1165083'>公在荆州，或象其仪，白发红颜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1165083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1165083'>谓公方壮，公生辛丑，天子之老。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1165083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1165083'>谁谓公老，其威桓桓，镇天子之南邦。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1165083_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　苏洵父子食荆州黄鱼，留江陵度岁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　是岁，苏洵长孙苏迈生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　苏洵父子观息壤，游渚宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年1月5日</a>　正月五日，苏洵父子发江陵，陆行赴京师。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
钟祥（长寿）

-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4149d5f0348c4fea8d0cfb86a7896b74_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4149d5f0348c4fea8d0cfb86a7896b74");'><span id='4149d5f0348c4fea8d0cfb86a7896b74_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>，52岁</div><div id='4149d5f0348c4fea8d0cfb86a7896b74' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏洵父子渡汉水，至襄阳。洵作《襄阳怀古》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》、《类编增广老苏先生大全文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_134172' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134172' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134172?labeling=true' target='_blank'>襄阳怀古</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134172")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134172_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134172'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134172'>我行襄阳野，山色向人明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134172'>何以洗怀抱，悠哉汉水清。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134172'>辽辽岘山道，千载几人行。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134172'>踏尽山上土，山腰为之平。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134172'>道逢堕泪碣，不觉涕亦零。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134172'>借问羊叔子，何异葛孔明。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134172'>今人固已远，谁识前辈情。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134172'>朅来万山下，潭水转相萦。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134172'>水深不见底，中有杜预铭。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134172'>潭水竟未涸，后世自知名。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134172'>成功本无敌，好誉真儒生。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134172'>自从三子亡，草中无豪英。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134172'>聊登岘山首，泪与汉流倾。<div id='poem_sentence_12_134172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_134172'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_134172_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在襄阳，苏洵游万山，题诗。作品：《万山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》、《类编增广老苏先生大全文集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_134141' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134141' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134141?labeling=true' target='_blank'>万山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134141")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134141_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134141'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134141'>万山临汉江，杰立与岘偶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134141'>杜公破三吴，磊落叔子后。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134141'>当年爱山意，无乃求自附。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134141'>自比诚不惭，山水亦奇秀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134141'>羊公苟有知，当为颔其首。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134141'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_134141_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
叶县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bf228e2f426744b79fec7286435c9d34_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bf228e2f426744b79fec7286435c9d34");'><span id='bf228e2f426744b79fec7286435c9d34_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>，52岁</div><div id='bf228e2f426744b79fec7286435c9d34' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏洵父子过昆阳，吊昆阳故城。洵作《昆阳城》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》、《类编增广老苏先生大全文集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_134149' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134149' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134149?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昆阳城</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134149")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134149_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134149'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134149'>昆阳城外土非土，战骨多年化墙堵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134149'>当时寻邑驱市人，未必三军皆反虏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134149'>江河填满道流血，始信武成真不误。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134149'>杀人应更多长平，薄赋宽征已无补。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134149'>英雄争斗岂得已，盗贼纵横亦何数。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134149'>御之失道谁使然，长使哀魂啼夜雨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134149'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_134149_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏洵父子至叶县。<br /></div>
-----end
