-----title
杞县（雍丘）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b57707ad38984e9183a75c93b8da9891_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b57707ad38984e9183a75c93b8da9891");'><span id='b57707ad38984e9183a75c93b8da9891_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1061')">1060-1061年</a>，52-53岁</div><div id='b57707ad38984e9183a75c93b8da9891' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　苏洵寓雍丘。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年8月8日</a>　在雍丘。八月甲子（初八日），苏洵为秘书省试校书郎。以赵抃等之荐也。洵以书谢。作品：《谢赵司谏书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1164995' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164995' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164995?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赵司谏书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年8月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164995")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164995_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164995'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164995'>洵启：向家居眉阳，以病懒不获问从者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164995_comment'></div>常以为阁下之所在，声之所振，德之所加，士以千里为近，而洵独不能走二百里一至于门，纵不获罪，固以为君子之弃人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164995_comment'></div>今年秋始见太守窦君京师，乃知阁下过听，猥以鄙陋上塞明诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164995_comment'></div>不知阁下何取于洵也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164995_comment'></div>洵固无取，然私独喜，以为可辞于世者，其不以驰骛得明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164995_comment'></div>洵不识阁下，然仰闻君子之风，常以私告于朋友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164995_comment'></div>特恨其身之不肖，不得交于当世，以遍致阁下之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164995_comment'></div>所告者皆饥寒自谋不暇之人，虽告而无益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164995_comment'></div>然犹以素不相识之故，得免于希势茍附之嫌，是其不识贤于识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164995_comment'></div>今世之所尚，相见则以数至门为勤，不相见则以数致书为忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164995_comment'></div>夫数至门者，虚礼无用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164995_comment'></div>数致书者，虚词无观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164995_comment'></div>得其无用与其无观而加喜，不得而怒，此与婴儿之好恶无异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164995_comment'></div>今阁下举人而取于不相识之中，则其去世俗远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164995_comment'></div>寓居雍丘，无故不至京师，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1164995", 1164995, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>詹望</span>君子，日以复日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164995_comment'></div>顷者朝廷猥以试校书郎见授，洵不能以老身复为州县之吏，然所以受者，嫌若有所过望耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164995_comment'></div>以阁下知我，故言及此，无怪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1164995_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　在雍丘，为秘书省试校书郎。苏洵上欧阳修书。作品：《上欧阳内翰第五书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1164984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164984?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上欧阳内翰第五书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164984")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164984'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164984'>内翰侍郎执事：洵以无用之才，久为天下之弃民，行年五十，未尝见役于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164984_comment'></div>执事独以为可收，而论之于天子，再召之试，而洵亦再辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164984_comment'></div>独执事之意，叮宁而不肯已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164984_comment'></div>朝廷虽知其不肖，不足以辱士大夫之列，而重违执事之意，譬之巫医卜祝，特捐一官以乞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164984_comment'></div>自顾无分毫之功有益于世，而王命至门，不知辞让，不畏简书、朋友之讥，而茍以为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164984_comment'></div>此所以深愧于执事，久而不至于门也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164984_comment'></div>然君子之相从，本非以求利，盖亦乐乎天下之不知其心，而或者之深知之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164984_comment'></div>执事之于洵，未识其面也，见其文而知其心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164984_comment'></div>既见也，闻其言而信其平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164984_comment'></div>洵不以身之进退出处之间有谒于执事，而执事亦不以称誉荐拔之，故有德于洵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164984_comment'></div>再召而辞也，执事不以为矫，而知其耻于自求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164984_comment'></div>一命而受也，执事不以为贪，而知其不欲为异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164984_comment'></div>其去不追，而其来不拒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164984_comment'></div>其大不荣，而其小不辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164984_comment'></div>此洵之所以自信于心者，而执事举知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164984_comment'></div>故凡区区而至门者，为是谢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164984_comment'></div>《礼》曰：「仕而未有禄者，君有馈焉曰献，使焉曰寡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164984_comment'></div>违而君薨，弗为服也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164984_comment'></div>古之君子重以其身臣人者盖为是也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164984_comment'></div>子思、孟轲之徒，至于是国，国君使人馈之，其词曰：「寡君使某有献于从者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164984_comment'></div>布衣之尊，而至于此，惟不食其禄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164984_comment'></div>今洵已有名于吏部，执事其将以道取之邪，则洵也犹得以宾客见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164984_comment'></div>不然，其将与奔走之吏同趋于下风，此洵所以深自怜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164984_comment'></div>惟所裁择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1164984_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　在雍丘，为秘书省试校书郎。苏洵有《谢相府启》。先是朝廷欲召洵试紫微阁，洵辞不至，乃除秘书省试校书郎。洵至是作谢启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1165002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢相府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165002")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165002'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165002'>朝廷之士，进而不知休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165002_comment'></div>山林之士，退而不知反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165002_comment'></div>二者交讥于世，学者莫获其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165002_comment'></div>洵幼而读书，固有意于从宦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165002_comment'></div>壮而不仕，岂为异以矫人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165002_comment'></div>上之则有制策诱之于前，下之则有进士驱之于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165002_comment'></div>常以措意，晚而自惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165002_comment'></div>盖人未之知，而自衒以求用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165002_comment'></div>世未之信，而有望于效官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165002_comment'></div>仰而就之，良亦难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165002_comment'></div>以为欲求于无辱，莫若退听之自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165002_comment'></div>有田一廛，足以为养；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165002_comment'></div>行年五十，将复何为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165002_comment'></div>不意贫贱之姓名，偶自彻闻于朝野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165002_comment'></div>向承再命以就试，固以大异其本心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165002_comment'></div>且必试而审观其才，则上之人犹未信其可用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165002_comment'></div>未信而有求于上，则洵之意以为近于强人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165002_comment'></div>遂以再辞，亦既获命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165002_comment'></div>于匹夫之贱，而必行其私意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165002_comment'></div>岂王命之宠，而敢望其曲加？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165002_comment'></div>昨承诏恩，被以休宠，退而自顾，愧其无劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165002_comment'></div>此盖昭文相公左右元君，舒惨百辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1165002_comment'></div>德泽所畅，刑威所加，不旸而熙，不寒而慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1165002_comment'></div>顾惟无似，或谓可收，不忍弃之于庶人，亦使与列于一命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1165002_comment'></div>上以慰夫天下贤俊之望，下以解其终身饥寒之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1165002_comment'></div>仰惟此恩，孰可为报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1165002_comment'></div>昔者孟子不愿召见，而孔子不辞小官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1165002_comment'></div>夫欲正其所由得之之名，是以谨其所以取之之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1165002_comment'></div>盖孟子不为矫，孔子不为卑，茍穷其心，则各有说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1165002_comment'></div>虽自知其不肖，常愿附其下风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1165002_comment'></div>区区之心，惟所裁择！</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1165002_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年11月</a>　在雍丘，为秘书省试校书郎。十一月辛丑（十六日），欧阳修拜枢密副使。苏洵有贺启。作品：《贺欧阳枢密启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注·佚文》）</span><div id='poem_1165003' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165003' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165003?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺欧阳枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165003")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165003_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165003'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165003'>伏审光奉帝诏，入持国枢，士民欢哗，朝野响动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165003_comment'></div>共惟国家所以设枢密之任，乃是天下未能忘威武之防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165003_comment'></div>虽号百岁之承平，未尝一日而无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165003_comment'></div>兵不可去，职为最难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165003_comment'></div>任文教则损国威，专武事则害民政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165003_comment'></div>伏自近岁，屡更大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165003_comment'></div>皆由省府而来，以答勋劳之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165003_comment'></div>一历二府，遂超百官，既无跂足之求，仅若息肩之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165003_comment'></div>自闻此命，欣贺实深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165003_comment'></div>盖因物议之所归，以慰民心之大望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165003_comment'></div>伏惟某官一时之杰，举代所推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165003_comment'></div>经世之文，服膺已久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165003_comment'></div>致君之略，至老不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165003_comment'></div>顾惟平昔起于小官，曷尝须臾忘于当世？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165003_comment'></div>以为天下之未大治，盖自贤者之在下风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165003_comment'></div>自今而言，夫复何难？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165003_comment'></div>愿因千载之遇，一新四海之瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1165003_comment'></div>洵受恩至深，为喜宜倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1165003_comment'></div>尝谓未死之际，无由知王道之大行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1165003_comment'></div>不意临老之年，犹及见君子之得位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1165003_comment'></div>阻以在外，阙于至门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1165003_comment'></div>仰祈高明，俯赐亮察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1165003_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年11月</a>　在雍丘，为秘书省试校书郎。十一月辛丑（十六日），欧阳修拜枢密副使。苏洵有代人作贺启。作品：《代人作贺欧阳枢密启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见孔凡礼《苏洵佚文》文题为录者所加。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　苏洵自本岁，复读《易》，作《易·传》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　在雍丘，为秘书省试校书郎。苏洵作《谱例》、《大宗谱法》。先是欧阳修见洵所撰《苏氏族谱》，亦出其所作《欧阳氏族谱》，洵乃为此二文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十四。）</span>《大宗谱法》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十四。）</span><div id='poem_1165085' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165085' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165085?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谱例序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165085")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165085_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165085'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165085'>古者，诸侯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1165085", 1165085, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>世国</span>，卿大夫世家，死者有庙，生者有宗，以相次也，是以百世而不相忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165085_comment'></div>此非独贤士大夫尊祖而贵宗，盖其昭穆存乎其庙，迁毁之主存乎其太祖之室，其族人相与为服，死丧嫁娶相告而不绝，则其势将自至于不忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165085_comment'></div>自秦、汉以来，仕者不世，然其贤人君子犹能识其先人，或至百世而不绝，无庙无宗而祖宗不忘，宗族不散，其势宜忘而独存，则由有谱之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165085_comment'></div>盖自唐衰，谱牒废绝，士大夫不讲，而世人不载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165085_comment'></div>于是乎由贱而贵者，耻言其先，由贫而富者不录其祖，而谱遂大废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165085_comment'></div>昔者，洵尝自先子之言而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1165085", 1165085, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>咨考</span>焉，由今而上得五世，由五世而上得一世，一世之上失其世次，而其本出于赵郡苏氏，以为《苏氏族谱》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165085_comment'></div>他日欧阳公见而叹曰：「吾尝为之矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165085_comment'></div>出而观之，有异法焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165085_comment'></div>曰：「是不可使独吾二人为之，将天下举不可无也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165085_comment'></div>洵于是又为《大宗谱法》，以尽谱之变，而并载欧阳氏之谱以为《谱例》，附以欧阳公《题刘氏碑后》之文，以告当世之君子，盖将有从焉者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1165085_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1165089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1165089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1165089?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宗谱法</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1165089")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1165089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1165089'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1165089'>《苏氏族谱》，小宗之法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1165089_comment'></div>凡天下之人，皆得而用之，而未及大宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1165089_comment'></div>大宗之法，冠以别子，由别子而列之，至于百世而至无穷，皆世自为处，别其父子，而合其兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1165089_comment'></div>父子者，无穷者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1165089_comment'></div>兄弟者，有穷者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1165089_comment'></div>无穷者相与处则害于无穷，其势不得不别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1165089_comment'></div>然而某之子某，某之子某，则是犹不别也，是为大宗之法云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1165089_comment'></div>故为大宗之法三世，自三世而推之，无不及也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1165089_comment'></div>人设二子而广之，无不载也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1165089_comment'></div>盖立法以为谱，学者之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1165089_comment'></div>由谱而知其先以及其旁子弟，以传于后世，是古君子之所重，而士大夫之所当知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1165089_comment'></div>以学者之事不立，而古君子之所重，与士大夫之所当知者随废，是学者之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1165089_comment'></div>于是存之《苏氏族谱》之末，以俟后世君子有采焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1165089_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1165089'>别子/一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1165089_comment'></div>别子之适子甲/庶子乙/二世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1165089_comment'></div>甲之适子丙/庶子丁/乙之适子戊/庶子己/三世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1165089_comment'></div>丙之适子庚/庶子辛/丁之适子壬/庶子癸/戊之适子子/庶子丑/己之适子寅/庶子卯。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1165089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1165089'><span class='label'>按：</span>《苏老泉先生全集》卷一四<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1165089_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　在雍丘，为秘书省试校书郎。净因院大觉怀琏禅师馈以唐阎立本所画《水官图》，苏洵作诗。作品：《水官诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注·佚诗》）</span><div id='poem_134170' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134170' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134170?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题阎立本画水官</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134170")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134170_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134170'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134170'>水官骑苍龙，龙行欲上天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134170'>手攀时且住，浩若乘风船。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134170'>不知几何长，足尾犹在渊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134170'>下有二从臣，左右乘鱼鼋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134170'>矍铄相顾视，风举衣袂翻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134170'>女子侍君侧，白颊垂双鬟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134170'>手执雉尾扇，容如未开莲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134170'>从者八九人，非鬼非戎蛮。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134170'>出水未成列，先登扬旗旃。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134170'>长刀拥旁牌，白羽注强拳。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134170'>虽服甲与裳，状貌犹鲸鳣。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134170'>水兽不得从，仰面以手扳。<div id='poem_sentence_11_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_134170'>空虚走雷霆，雨电晦九川。<div id='poem_sentence_12_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_134170'>风师黑虎囊，面目昏尘烟。<div id='poem_sentence_13_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_134170'>翼从三神人，万里朝天关。<div id='poem_sentence_14_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_134170'>我从大觉师，得此诡怪编。<div id='poem_sentence_15_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_134170'>画者古阎子，于今三百年。<div id='poem_sentence_16_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_134170'>见者谁不爱，予者诚已难。<div id='poem_sentence_17_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_134170'>在我犹在子，此理宁非禅。<div id='poem_sentence_18_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_134170'>报之以好词，何必画在前<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_134170'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_134170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_134170'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_134170_0'>⑴ 以上宋苏轼《东坡续集》卷一　接：二诗朱熹《晦庵诗话》定为苏洵作。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_134170_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　在雍丘，为秘书省试校书郎。陆绾（权叔）提举江淮茶税，苏洵作送行诗。作品：《送陆权叔提举茶税》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134156' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134156' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134156?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送陆权叔提举茶税</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134156")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134156_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134156'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134156'>君家本江湖，南行即邻里。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134156'>税茶虽冗繁，渐喜官资美。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134156'>嗟君本笃学，寤寐好文字。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134156'>往年在巴蜀，忆见《春秋》始。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134156'>名家乱如发，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_134156", 134156, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>棼错</span>费寻理。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134156'>今来未五岁，新传满盈几。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134156'>又言欲治《易》，杂说书万纸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134156'>君心不可测，日夜涌如水。<div id='poem_sentence_7_134156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_134156'>何年重相逢，祗益使余畏。<div id='poem_sentence_8_134156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_134156'>但恐茶事多，乱子《易》中意。<div id='poem_sentence_9_134156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_134156'>茶《易》两无妨，知君足才思。<div id='poem_sentence_10_134156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_134156'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_134156_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　在雍丘，为秘书省试校书郎。苏洵上韩琦书。求官。作品：《上韩丞相书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1164989' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164989' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164989?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上韩丞相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164989")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164989_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164989'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164989'>洵年老无聊，家产破坏，欲从相公乞一官职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164989_comment'></div>非敢望如朝廷所以待贤俊，使之志得道行者，但差胜于今，粗可以养生遗老者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164989_comment'></div>去岁蒙朝廷授洵试校书郎，亦非敢少之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164989_comment'></div>使朝廷过听，而洵侥倖，不过得一京官，终不能如汉唐之际所以待处士者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164989_comment'></div>则京官之与试衔，又何足分多少于其间，而必为彼不为此邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164989_comment'></div>然其所以区区无厌，复有求于相公者，实以家贫无赀，得六七千钱，诚不足以赡养，又况忍穷耐老，望而未可得邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164989_comment'></div>凡人为官，稍可以纾意快志者，至京朝官始有其髣髴耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164989_comment'></div>自此以下者，皆劳觔苦骨，摧折精神，为人所役使，去仆隶无几也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164989_comment'></div>然天下之士，所以求之如不及，得之而喜者，彼诚少年，将有所忍于此，以待至于纾意快志者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164989_comment'></div>若洵者，计其年岂足以有待邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164989_comment'></div>今且守选数年，然后得窥尚书省门，又待阙岁馀而到任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164989_comment'></div>幸而得免于负犯废放，又守选、又待阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164989_comment'></div>如此十四五年，谨守以满七八考，又幸而有举主五六人，然后敢望于改官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164989_comment'></div>当此之时，洵盖七十矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164989_comment'></div>譬如豫章橘柚，非老人所种也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164989_comment'></div>洵久为布衣，无官长<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1164989", 1164989, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>拘辖</span>，自觉觔骨疏强，不堪为州县趋走拜伏小吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164989_comment'></div>相公若别除一官，而幸与之，愿得尽力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164989_comment'></div>就使无补，亦必不至于恣睢漫漶，以伤害王民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164989_comment'></div>今朝廷糊名以取人，保任以得官，茍应格者，虽屠沽不得不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164989_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164989_comment'></div>虽欲爱惜而无由也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164989_comment'></div>今洵幸为诸公所知似不甚浅，而相公尤为有意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164989_comment'></div>至于一官，则反覆迟疑不决者累岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164989_comment'></div>嗟夫，岂天下之官以洵故冗邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164989_comment'></div>洵少时自处不甚卑，以为遇时得位，当不卤莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1164989_comment'></div>及长，知取士之难，遂绝意于功名，而自托于学术，实亦有得而足恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1164989_comment'></div>自去岁以来，始复读《易》，作《易传》百馀篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1164989_comment'></div>此书若成，则自有《易》以来，未始有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1164989_comment'></div>今也亦不甚恋恋于一官，如必无可推致之理，亦幸明告之，无使其首鼠不决，欲去而迟迟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1164989_comment'></div>世人施恩则望报，茍有以相博，则叩之也易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1164989_comment'></div>今洵已潦倒，有二子又皆抗拙如洵，相公岂能施此不报之恩邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1164989_comment'></div>相公往时为洵言，欲为欧阳公言子者数矣，而见辄忘之，以为怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1164989_comment'></div>洵诚惧其或有意欲收之也，而复忘之，故忍耻而一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1164989_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1164989_comment'></div>洵再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1164989_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年7月</a>　七月，苏洵为霸州文安县主薄，与项城令姚闢修纂礼书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　苏洵与李育（仲蒙）游。育与修《太常因革礼》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　苏洵之兄苏涣赴利州路提点刑狱任。轼送行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　在雍丘，为霸州文安县主簿。苏洵上《议修礼书状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1164974' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1164974' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1164974?labeling=true' target='_blank'>议修礼书状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_1164974")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1164974_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1164974'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1164974'>右，洵先奉敕编礼书，后闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1164974", 1164974, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>臣寮</span>上言，以为祖宗所行不能无过差不经之事，欲尽芟去，无使存录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1164974_comment'></div>洵窃见议者之说，与敕意大异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1164974_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1164974_comment'></div>前所授敕，其意曰纂集故事，而使后世无忘之耳，非曰制为典礼，而使后世遵而行之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1164974_comment'></div>然则洵等所编者，是史书之类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1164974_comment'></div>遇事而记之，不择善恶，详其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1164974", 1164974, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>曲折</span>，而使后世得知而善恶自著者，是史之体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1164974_comment'></div>若夫存其善者，而去其不善，则是制作之事，而非职之所及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1164974_comment'></div>而议者以责洵等，不已过乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1164974_comment'></div>且又有所不可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1164974_comment'></div>今朝廷之礼虽为详备，然大抵往往亦有不安之处，非特一二事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1164974_comment'></div>而欲有所去焉，不识其所去者果何事也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1164974_comment'></div>既欲去之，则其势不得不尽去，尽去则礼缺而不备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1164974_comment'></div>茍独去其一，而不去其二，则适足以为抵捂龃龉而不可<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1164974", 1164974, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>齐一</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1164974_comment'></div>且议者之意，不过欲以掩恶讳过，以全臣子之义，如是而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1164974_comment'></div>昔孔子作《春秋》，惟其恻怛而不忍言者而后有隐讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1164974_comment'></div>盖桓公薨，子般卒，没而不书，其实以为是不可书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1164974_comment'></div>至于成宋乱，及齐狩，跻僖公，作丘甲，用田赋，丹桓宫楹，刻桓宫桷，若此之类，皆书而不讳，其意以为虽不善而尚可书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1164974_comment'></div>今先世之所行，虽小有不善者，犹与《春秋》之所书者甚远，而悉使洵等隐讳而不书，如此，将使后世不知其浅深，徒见当时之臣子至于隐讳而不言，以为有所大不可言者，则无乃欲益而反损欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1164974_comment'></div>《公羊》之说灭纪灭项，皆所以为贤者讳，然其所谓讳者，非不书也，书而迂曲其文耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1164974_comment'></div>然则其实犹不没也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1164974_comment'></div>其实犹不没者，非以彰其过也，以见其过之止于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1164974_comment'></div>今无故乃取先世之事而没之，后世将不知而大疑之，此大不便者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1164974_comment'></div>班固作《汉志》，凡汉之事，悉载而无所择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1164974_comment'></div>今欲如之，则先世之小有过差者，不足以害其大明，而可以使后世无疑之之意，且使洵等为得其所职，而不至于侵官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1164974_comment'></div>谨具状申提举参政侍郎，欲乞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1164974", 1164974, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>备录</span>闻奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1164974_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年10月3日</a>　十月三日，诏编定谥法。苏洵与其事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　传苏轼尝闻父洵言破雾珠事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　苏轼辞父洵离京师赴凤翔府任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　在雍丘，为霸州文安县主簿。苏洵作《朝日载升》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134178' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134178' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134178?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝日载升</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134178")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_134178_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134178'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134178'>朝日载升，薨薨伊氓。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134178'>于室有绩，于野有耕。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134178'>于涂有商，于边有征。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134178'>天生斯民，相养以宁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134178'>嗟我何为，踽踽无营。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134178'>初孰与我，今孰主我。<div id='poem_sentence_5_134178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_134178'>我将往问，安所处我。<div id='poem_sentence_6_134178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_134178'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_134178_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　在雍丘，为霸州文安县主簿。苏洵作《有触者犊》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134175' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134175_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134175'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134175'>有触者犊，再箠不却。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134175'>为子已触，安所置角。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134175'>天实畀我，子欲已我。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134175'>恶我所为，盍夺我有。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134175'>子欲不触，盍索之笠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134175'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_134175_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　在雍丘，为霸州文安县主簿。苏洵作《有骥在野》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《嘉祐集笺注》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_134176' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_134176' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/134176?labeling=true' target='_blank'>有骥在野</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29837, "北宋", "苏洵", "poem_title_134176")'>苏洵</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_134176_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_134176'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_134176'>有骥在野，百过不呻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_134176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_134176'>子不我良，岂无他人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_134176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_134176'>絷我于厩，乃不我驾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_134176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_134176'>遇我不终，不如在野。<div id='poem_sentence_3_134176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_134176'>秃毛于霜，寄肉于狼，宁彼我伤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_134176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_134176'>宁人不我顾，无子我忘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_134176_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
